1.1 UMmonomansuonk Isaiah wunnaumonuh Amoz, ne nag* papaume Judah kah Jerusalem, pâmontog Uzziah, Jotham, Ahaz, kah Hezekiah Judae ketass8tamwog.
1.2 N8tam8k woi kesukquog, & kuhkeitash woi ohke: newutche Jehovah ket8hkau, nummahche sohkomm8s8wam, kah nukkésukeh mukkiésog, kah nag nutcheketunkquog.
1.3 Ox waheau[m]eh wadtihéunitcheh wuhhog, kah asse wahteoh wussontimomuh ne ahhut assamukqut: qut Israel matta wahteóou, nummissinninneumog matta natwontam8[o]g.
1.4 Yea matcheseáe wutohtimóin, missinninnúog neg nayeutogig matcheseongash, 8skannémune8h matchesécheg: mukki[ó]g neg ánusséhuácheg, nag ohquanumáog Jehovah, nag m8m8sqhe[á]og 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, musquánittamunat, nag qushkée amaéog.
1.5 Toh$waj wonk woh tattogkomitteaog? pish nano kutassaemw8: mamusse muppuhkuk mahchimom8, kah mamússe metah sauunum8m8.
1.6 Wutch agwusseet, wehque muppuhkukqut, na wanne menuhkano, qut annehikanash, kah woskissinn8ongash, kah ánue kehkechésuongash, matta yanémun8ash, asuh weesquabi[n]i[nn]8ash, asuh matta wutogkunnum8unash nashpe pummee.
1.7 Kutohk8 touushin, kutotanáoash chikoht[á]ash n8taut, kutohke, penuwohteáog ummatchteauuneau ut anaquabeóg kah ne touushin, onatuh sohkomuk nashpe penuwohteáog.
1.8 Kah Zione wuttaunin nukkonau onatuh wetuomémesut ut seenominneohtekonit, onatuh kohkouémuk ut cucumbere tanohketeaonganit, onatuh wéenuhkausik keitotan.
1.9 Kuttumma Jehovah ayeuhteáanit sequnnumunkqueog peásin sequnittuonk, woh keáneyeu8mun Sodom, kah woh kutogqueneunkqussimun Gomorrah.
1.10 N8tam8k wuttinn8wâonk Jehovah, kenaau Sodome nanawunnuaenúog, kukkeitam8k wuttinnaumatuonk kut$Jehovahumun, woi Gomorrahe missinninnúog.
1.11 Ne teag wutch mataáneum kussephammayeuongan8, n8wau Jehovah? nunnumwohtóh ramse chikohtáe mag8ongash, kah 8weesum8 wunogque puppinashimwog, kah matta nuttapeneam8 8sqheongan8 oxinog, asuh lambsog, asuh namposhimwe goatsog.
1.12 Peyôog kenógqussinneaóut ut anaquabeh, [h]owan yeu wunnat8tamuhkon ut kenutcheganit, tattashkukomuneat, nutchippinneutungash.
1.13 Padtauúhteogk wonk tahn8che mag8ongash, incense ne nehchanumukquodt ut nuhhogkat, wuske nepâuzsaog, kah sabbathaash, moáe wehkomonát nutjishontamun, ne matcheseonk, ne moáe miya[é]onk.
1.14 K8ske kenepâuzs8m8óog, kah kukkuhquttum8we mishadtupp8ongan8oash, nukketeahogkou nish wutjishontamunash: nish n8tamêhikqunash, nussauunum nish nutchequnehtamunat.
1.15 Kah sepagenumog kenutch[e]gan8oash, pish nutadtahtóh nuskesukquash wutch kuhhogkaout, nux, ayimog monatash peantam8ongash, matta pish nunn8tam8h, kenutchegan8out numwohte[á]u wusqueheongash.
1.16 Kutchessumók, pahkheuk kuhhogkóog, amaunum8k kum̃atcheseongan8oash wutch anaquabeh, netahshe matchesek,
1.17 Kodnetuhtau8k wunnésen, natinneham8k wussittumóonk, aninnumok noh sonkqutchahwhut, wussumok touwies, ken8tamwa[n]sheuk sekousq.
1.18 Yeuyeu peyunk, kah moáe ennóm[á]iyeuhteadtuh, n8wau Lord; t[ô]hkonogque k[u]m̃atcheseongan8ash onatuhheyeu8 skarletut, nish pish ogque wompiyeuash k8nit: tôhkonogque nish unnemusqui crimson, nish pish onatuhyeu8ash w8lut.
1.19 Unnantamóg kah n8swehtamóg, pish kummeechum8 ohkée wunnummeechum.
1.20 Qut sekeneamóg, kah cheketamóg, pish kummohtuppaémo nashpe togkodt[e]g: newutche wutt8n Jehovah ket8hkontamun.
1.21 Uttôh en pâbuhtantam8e keitotan nanwun8dsquaáesuenúin? ne numwohtop wussittumóonk, sampweusseonk ne ayeum8, qut yeuyeu nushehteaenúog.
1.22 Kus$silverum p[e]htóou, k8winum kenuksheau nippe.
1.23 Kussontimomog cheketamwog, kah weechayemá[h]etticheh kumm8towa[é]nuog, nishnoh pasuk womantam mag8ongash; kah asuhkom kemunkquatungash: nag matta wussumauóog touwiesoh, kah wuttinniyeuonk sekousq matta uppeyógk8uneau.
1.24 Newaj n8wadt Lord, Jehovah ayeuhteaanit, noh masugkenuk ut Israel, yâ nunnunkeh nuhhog wutch yeu ay8kausitcheg, kah nutann8tau nummatwomog.
1.25 Kah nukquinnuppinnum nunnutcheg en kuhhogkat, kah nuppannuppe pahketeoh kuppehtom, kah nutamaúnum wame kuttinnum.
1.26 Kah kenompenumoush k8sittumwaéneumwog neáne negonne, kah ken8snaéneumog neáne waj kutchissik: ompetak pish kuttéhenit, sampweusseáe keitotan, pabahtanumwe keitotan.
1.27 Zion pish pohquohwhuttauun, nashpe wussittumóonk, kah n[e]g ne adt quinnuppecheg, nashpe sampweusséonk.
1.28 Kah pagwanoungan8 panneseaénûog, kah matcheseaenúog pish moeyeu88: kah nág ohquanumoncheg Jehovah pish mohtuppaéog.
1.29 Newutche nag pish akodchuog n8timisseash nish kodtantogish, kah pish kukquequenauánumumw8, newutche tanohketeaongash nish pepenamogish.
1.30 Newutche pish kutogqueneunkqussum8 n8timisseit noh 8neepóg pánshunk, kah onatuh tanohketeáonk ne mat napén8g
1.31 Káh manuhkésitcheg pish onatuhyeu8og hashabput, kah noh ayik, onatuh chikinn[a]sit, kah nag pish neeswe moeu chikossuog, kah wanne pish howan wutontáhwoh.
2.1 WUttinn8waonk ne Isayah wunnaumonuh Amoz nag*, papaume Judah kah Jerusalem.
2.2 Kah pish n$nih majish kesukodtash, wek Jehovah 8wadcheum, ne pish menehketeauun ut koduhkô[á]e wadchukontu, kah pish anue tahshinausu onk wadchuash, kah wame wutohtimóineash uppeyaont[á]muneau.
2.3 Kah monaog missinninn[u]og pish moncheog[;] kah n8waog, peyunk, kuhkuhquehtuh 8wadcheum Jehovah, en wekit um-Manitt8moh Jakob, kah noh pish nuppomushamun ummayut: newutche Zion wutch sohham ennaumatuonk, kah wuttinn8waonk Jehovah wutch Jerusalem.
2.4 Kah noh pish wussittum ut kenugke wutohtim[o]inneat, kah pish áushkomau mónaoh missinninnuh: kah nag pish plowshearehteáog wuttogkodtegan8óash, kah pish tisaskwheganéhteáog ukqunuhtugquash: wutohtimóin matta pish ayeuuhkonit[t]ue tohshinnumauóou togkodteg wutohtimóiñeuh, kah matta pish wonk netuhtauóog ayeuwuttuonk.
2.5 Woi wek Jakob, peyunk, kah pomushadtuh 8wequaiyeumut Jehovah.
2.6 Newaj nukkonadt kummissinninneumog, wek Jakob: newutche tapauwaméog wutch wutchepwoiyeu, kah ogquonnetuog Philistiansut, kah tapheaog wuhhogkauh nashpe wunneechan8oh penuwohteáog.
2.7 Kah nag wutohkou numwohteau silver kah gold, kah matta wohkukquoshininn8 wunnompakounn8ash; wonk wutohkeeu wunnumwábeneau horsesoh, kah matta wohkukquos[n]in8 wut-chariotsumash.
2.8 Kah wonk wutohkéim8 wunnumwábeneau nunneukontunkanog, wowussittumwog néhenwonche wunnutchegane anakausuongan8oash, ne nehenwonche wuttinwhunnitche8 kestoum8uk.
2.9 Kah noh peississit, nauwáeu, kah noh masugkenuk hohppáheau wuhhogkuh, newutche ahquontamauúhkon.
2.10 Petutteah qussukquanit, kah puttogqush ut puppissiyeuut wutche qushaonk Jehovah, kah wutche wussohsumóe maumuttanussuonk.
2.11 Ukqunuhqunneunkqussuonk wosketomp pish hohpóm8, kah uppehtuánum8ongan8 missinninnúog pish nauwa[é]m[X], kah Jehovah nussu pish misheh[e]au ne kesukok.
2.12 Newutche ukkesukodtum Jehovah ayeuhteáanit, pish nuhkuhkauau nish$noh howane noh pahtuánumit, kah noh pohtuanumwinneunkqussit, kah nish$noh pasuk noh tahshinit, kah noh pish tiuhquon[a]heuh.
2.13 Kah ut wame Lebanone Cedaro[h], nish quanunkquokish kah tohshiná[unk]ish, kah ut wame Bashanne n8time[s]éash.
2.14 Kah ut wame qu[n]u[h]qui wadchuuhkontu, kah ut wame wadchuuhkontu nish tahshinaúsikish.
2.15 Kah ut nish$noh qunuhqui tower, kah ut nish$noh pummeneutausue pummeneútunk.
2.16 Kah ut wame Tarshish-kuht8nogquehtu, kah ut wame tapeneunkquotte nunneukontu[n]kanéhtu.
2.17 Kah uppehtuanumwunneunkqussuonk wosketomp pish nauwaemo, kah tiuhquonkqutteau: kah Jehovah nussu pish tahshinau ne kesukok.
2.18 Kah nunneukontunkoh papuhquáne matcheheau.
2.19 Kah nag pish petutteáog qussukquanónogqut, kah puhpohkohteaiyeuut, newutch qusháonk Jehovah, kah newutch sussohsum8ongane maumutta[n]suonk, noh omohkit unkquanumwe nunnukshadtunk ohke.
2.20 Ne kesukok wosketomp pish amaúhteau wussilvere nunneukontunkoh, kah uk-golde nunneukontunkoh, neh ayimáhetticheh nish$noh pasuk nehenwonche wowussumónat, en molsut, kah en mattabashquásit.
2.21 Petukonat passipskodtut, kah woskeche passipskodtut, wutche qusháonk Lord, kah wutche wussohsumóemaumuttá[u]suonk omohkeit wutunkquánume nunnukshadtauunat ohke
2.22 Ahqueteau8k wutch wosketompaut, noh wunnasháonk ohtag wutchanit newutche, uttoh ut ogquanumon?
3.1 NEwutche kusseh, Lord, Lord ayeuhteáanit amaunum wutch Jerusalem, kah wutch Judah, ompatissun8 kah anwohhou, mamusse petukqunnegane ompatissun8onk, kah mámusse nippee ompatissun8onk
3.2 Menuhkésuénin, kah ayeuteaénin, wussittumwaénin, kah quoshodtumwaènin, kah waantamwen kah kehchisog.
3.3 Napanna adtahshinchagkussitcheg kah quohtiánumukqussuénin, kah ken8suaénin, nehtóanakausuénin, kah wowúnonuhk8waénin.
3.4 Kah nussontimôhteam mukkiésog, kah peissesog pish wunnánauwunóuh.
3.5 Kah missinninnúog nish$noh pasuk, pish sonkqutchahwhuttuog, kah, nishnoh pasuk nashpe weetatteamungoh: mukkies pish ayeuuhkonittue pehchuánumwe ussehtauau kehchisoh, kah meshananumukqussit ayeuuhkonittue quohtianumukqussinitcheh.
3.6 Wosketomp tohqunont wematoh, wutch wekit 8shoh, n8wadt, k8htogk8in, nanawi[n]yean, kah yeu matchehteoonk ohtaj agw[é] kenutcheganit.
3.7 Ne kesukok noh pish chadchekeyeuau, n8wau, matta neetskehuwáenu8: newutche ut nekit matta petukquanegan8 asuh hogk8unun8: ahque nanawunnumw[á]heh ut missinninnútu.
3.8 Newutche Jerusalem paguatauun, kah Judah penusheau, newutche weenaneu, kah wutusseongan8oash wutayeuuhkonukquanash Jehovah, m8m8squeteauunat wussohsum8e wuskesukquash.
3.9 Ne[-]anompamukqussimuk ne 8wauwaónukquneau, kah nag ogque wahteauwáhuwaog ummatcheseongan8 Sodom, matta wutadtahtau8uneau: pish onkapunnaoh ukketeahogkôun8oh, newutche matonkquottauáog wuhhogkauh.
3.10 Unnok sampwesecheg, nag pish 8niyeuwontamuneau: newutche nag pish meechwog wutanakausuongane meechummuonganóash.
3.11 Pish onkapunáog matcheetowog, pish ummatchiyeuôntamun: newutche wunnutchegane onkquatunk pish aninnumau[ó]n.
3.12 Papaume nummissinninneumog, mukkiog neh wussonkqutchahwhóuh, kah mittamwussissog nanawunóuh, woi nummissinninneumog, neg sogkompagunukquéaneg kuppanneáhikquog, kah nag paguatoog kuppomushaongane mayash.
3.13 Jehovah neepau ukken8tamunat, kah neepau 8sumónat missinninnúh.
3.14 Jehovah pish uppas8oh wussittum8onganit ummissinninneum8e ke[h]chisumoh, kah wussontimom8[ó]h: newutche kummahchepumw8 weenominneohteuk, sequttahhamauáonk matcheku, ut kekuóut.
3.15 Toh kuttin nauwuttamumw8, kussukquéhtahwhônaóont nummissinninneumog, kah togguhhamunat wuskesuk8oash matchekuog, n8wau Lord Jehovah ayeuhteaanit.
3.16 Nano Jehovah n8wau, newutche Sione wuttauneunk, pehtuánumóog, kah sekoushquáusháog, kah nanwun8dsquaeskesukquáog, pomushaog, kah wowunnomâusháog pomusháhettit, kah papónshittáusháog.
3.17 Newaj Lord pish tádteadt mukkeontupaonk ut kodto[n]tupont wuttaunoh Zion; kah Jehovah pish poshkinum ukkôsuonganú8ash.
3.18 Ne kesukok Lord pish amaunum wunn8whôsue wanegukish ut wusseetut, kah ukkaulsum8ash, kah woweeyôwe wunn8whosuongash onatuh nahnepâush[á]dtaut.
3.19 Chainsash, kah kehtippittenápeash, kah mufflersash,
3.20 Bonnetsash, kah muhkontee wunnuhwhosuongash, kah assuhquabeash, kah tabletsash, kah soggussohhouunash,
3.21 Pehtehhennitchabheash, kah mutchâne hogqunnu[m]aongash.
3.22 Os8ogk8unaongash kah m8[na]kinash, kah wimplsash, kah 8wutchippussum8e auwohteaongash,
3.23 Pepenauutchitchunkquongash, kah wunne hashabponak, kah h8dsash, kah onkquequohh8unash.
3.24 Kah pish n$nih, nompe ne weetemungquok, pish annimmungquot: kah nompe puttukquobpus, nehneksh[á]eu, kah nompe wanoht[ó]e muhpuhkuk, mukukkontupáonk; kah nompe mohpanôganit ahhohtag man8t[i]ónak puttukquobpissinneat, kah chikkossuonk nompe wunnetuonganit.
3.25 K8wosketompomog pish penusháog nashpe togkodteg, kah kummenuhkesuene[ú]mog ut ayeuwuttineat.
3.26 Kah 8squontamash pish neuantam8m8ash, kah noh nâsiit, pish appu ohkeit.
4.1 KAh ne kesukok nesausuk tahsuog mittamwussissog pish togqunáog pasuk8 wosketompuh, n8waog, nummeechimun nehenwonche nuppetukqunneganun, kah nuth[o]gkumun nehenwonche nuthogk8onganun: webe k8wesuonk uss8wésitteaongunan, nutamaunumunnanónut nukkekómitteaonganun.
4.2 Ne kesukok, 8tuhqunnum Jehovah pish pahkeneunkquot, kah sohsum8eyeu8, kah ummeechummúonk ohke pish wunnegen kah tapeneunkquot, wutche yeug Israelitsog pohquohhogig.
4.3 Kah pish n$nih noh ashqunit ut Zion, kah noh ashqunit ut Jerusalem, pish hennau wunneetupanatamwen, nishnoh pasuk noh wâsukuhwhôsit kenugke neg pâmontogig ut Jerusalem
4.4 Lord amâpadtunk wunnishkeneunkquodt8m8 Zione wuttauneunk, kah pahketeunk Jerusaleme wusqueheonk, wutch ne nôeu, nashpe wussittum8e nashauanit, kah nashpe nashqunnae nashauanit.
4.5 Kah Jehovah pish kesteau ut nishnoh ayeuonganit ut wadchuut Zion, kah ut umm[ó]eonganéhtu, matokqs kah pukut kesukodáe, kah wôhsum8e n8n8náe n8teau nukkonáeu, newutche ut wame sohsum8onganit pish onk8wôhkussú8nú8.
4.6 Kah na pish tabernakle, wutch wutonka[u]óhtóm8 wutch kesukodáe kussittaut, kah wutche spuhh8aé ayeuonk, kah wutch abohquos mehshittahshik kah sokanon.
5.1 YEuyeu nukket8homau wâmonog, an8homáonk, papaume n8womonog, papaume 8weenominneohteuk: n8womónog 8weenominneohtekoneu ahche mishummeechummúe wadchuut.
5.2 Kah uppummeneutauun, kah mukkinnum nish qussukquanash, kah wutohtekontamuneash pepenamwe weenomwussippagwash, kah ayim towér ut nashaue, kah wonk ne wuttittannehteauun wine-presse: kah ukkenompadtamun woh paudtau[ó]m8t weenominneash, kah tannegen touohkomukque weenominneash.
5.3 Kah yeuyeu, woi kenaau wadohkeógish Jerusalem, kah Judae wosketompaog, wussittum8k k8wehquetumauonumw8, nashaue nen kah n8weenominneohteuk?
5.4 Toh woh wonk uñehteauun n8weenominneohteuk, ne matta á[h]teau8? tohwutch, ashkauwompadtamon woh paudtauóm8 weenominneash, paudtauóm8uk tauohkomukque weenominneash.
5.5 Kah yeuyeu éhha, kuttinnonuneau uttoh a[h]teáu n8weenominneohteuk: nutamaunum ne pumme[n]eutunk, kah pish mahchipun; kah nussukqunnum ne pummeneutunk kah pish tahtashkuhkomun
5.6 Kah pish n8wôhshwushittea[n]un, kah matta pish wunnehteauun, asuh wônuhkontam8un, qut na pish wutut neekineau kôussog kah asinnekôussog: kah wonk nutann8tam matokqs woh matta missippano sokanunk.
5.7 Newutche 8weenominneohteuk Jehovah ayeu[t]eaanit, ne wek Israel, kah Judae wosketompoh ne wuttapeneam8e ohketeaonk: kah askauwompattam wussittumóonk, qut kusseh s[o]nkqutcha[w]huttuonk, sampweseonk qut kusseh mauonk.
5.8 Onkapunáhettich neg ahasuhkauunukeg wetuómash, kah ahasuhkauunukeg ohteuhkonash, noh pajeh matta ayeuonga[n]in8g, onk woh nag nussiyeuog ut nôeu ohkeit.
5.9 Ut nuhtauogut n8wau Jehovah ayeuhteanit, wunnamuhkut monatash wetuómash pish touushin, mogkiyeuash, kah wowunnegenash matta ayéin.
5.10 Nux, piukque akerseu8 weenominneohteuk, pish wutchegen pasuk bath, kah homere wuskannem pish wutchegen ephah.
5.11 Onkapunáhettich neg nompoáe o[X]ohkécheg, onk woh nag asuhkomwog onkup, nag wunnagwutteanumuneau nô pajeh wunnonk88k, nô pajeh wine kussopposikqhettit.
5.12 Kah harp, kah viol, kah tabret, kah puhpegq, kah wine wutohtauuneau ut mishadtupp8onganit, qut nag matta wutt8antamóog wutanakausuonk Lord, kah matta natwontamóog wunnetchegane anakausuonk
5.13 Newaj missináhettit nummissinninneumog, newutche matta 8wahteauonganéog: kah ukquttiánumweneum8uh paskonontamwoh, kah ummuttaán8m8uh nunnassuoh nashpe kûhkuht8[n]8onk.
5.14 Newaj chepiohkomuk mishe kishkeheont wuhhogkuh, kah mishe wôshwunnum wutt8n, wanne quttuhham8e: kah wussohsum8ongan8 kah umm[u]ttaán8ongan8, kah 8nauwámeongan8, kah noh mashkouá[n]atog, pish na wuttin w8ms[i]u.
5.15 Kah peississitcheg pish tiohquonkhéaog, kah masukenuk pish hohpáheau, k[á]h wuskesuk8oash pehtuánumóog pish hohpóm8ash.
5.16 Qut Jehovah ayeuhteaanit pish misheheau ut wussittum8onganit, kah wunneetupanatamwe God pish wunneetupanatamwe ogquanumau ut sampweusseonganit.
5.17 Neit lambsog pish unnadtupp8og ne áhhunnadtupwéhettit, kah wuttouwashinneume wutayeuongan[ó]ash pen8wohteáog pish wuttit meetsinneau.
5.18 Onkapunáhettich neg wádto[ntn]uk[e]g panneseonk nashpe tahn8che pemeneohtanash, kah matcheseonk onatuh nashp[é] carte pemeneohtanit.
5.19 Neg án8wacheg, kenuppe usseitch, kenupanakausitch, onk woh naumunán: kah ukeen8s8wáonk 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, pas8tsh[a]úm8utch, kah peyaum8utch, onk woh n8wahteauuna[n].
5.20 Onkapunâhettich nag an8wacheg papaume machuk, ne wunnegen, kah wanegik ne matchet, neg nompatunkig pohkenái wutch wequai, kah wequai wutch pohkenái, neg nompatunkig weesogkon wutch weekon, kah weekon wutch weesogkon.
5.21 Onkapunáhettich nag waantogig ut nehenwonche wuskesuk8óut, kah napwóncheg ut nehenwonche anaquabhettit.
5.22 Onkapun[á]hettich neg manuhke wuttattogig wine, kah menuhk[é]suenuog kenukkeaumunat onkup.
5.23 Neg sampweogquanumoncheg matcheet8oh wutche onkquatunk, kah amaunumauoncheg wussampweusseongan8 sampwesécheg.
5.24 Newaj onatuh n8teau mahchukkissuk sequekepunneg, kah n8n8uneau mahchukki[ss]um wussadteámuneash, ne ne 8wadchabuk8 pish anit, kah wunnet8nunk pish o[g]que us[h]pém8 puppissiyeuut, newutche pogketamwog wuttinnaumatuonk Jehovah ayeuhteáanit, kah jishantamwog wuttinn8wáonk 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
5.25 Newaj ummusquantam8onk Jehovah ayeuuhkonittue nashqunneau en ummissininneumut, kah mahche ayeuuhkonittue summagunúmauau wunnutcheg, na[h] wuttogkomuh: kah wadchuash nunnukshaash, kah nupp8e wuhhogkáuh nehnehkohkou[X]uh ut nôeu toumaogqu[e]htu: wutch wame yeu, ummusquanittam8onk matta ámaémun8, qut wunnutcheg ashpumme summagunum.
5.26 Kah noh pish tahshinum ensigne wutch nôadtit wutohtimóneat, kah pish ukkehke[m]womuh, wutch wehqshik ohke, kah kusseh, nag pish kenuppe kenupsháe peyaog.
5.27 Matta howan pish sauunnum8, asuh togkussittassun8 ut nah kenugke: wanne pish howan ukkogkou[ó]quoh, asuh koueu, kah matta pish mussuk[q]unádtikame puttukquobpus ompenum8un, kah mattógquonápeash matta pish poshkishán8ash.
5.28 Ukkouhquodt8oash kenag, kah wame wutahtompeyeumoh wutonkqunosuoh, wuthorsese 8kossum8oh pish ogquanumukqussuoh qussukquanit, kah 8wheelum8 ogqueneunkqusseum8 pemsquahut.
5.29 OOwadtauatonkqussuongan8 pish tatuppeyeu8 qunnonouut, nag pish ogquont8aog wuske qunnonouut: nux, nag pish mishont8waog, & togqunumwog sequttahhamukeh, kah pish 8wohque moncha[u]ouh, kah wanne howan pish uppohquohwhunuh.
5.30 Kah ne kesukok nah pish ummishont8waounouh, onatuh mashont8wom8uk keitoh: kah howan monunneog ohke, kusseh pohkenai kah unkquanumoonk, kah wequáei pohkenahteauun ut ukkesukquehteaum8ouh.
6.1 NE kodtum8k ketass8t Uzziah napuk, wonk nunnauomp Lord quenappu appuonganit, qunuhque kah tahshinau: kah ne asukunkqut numwohteau templeut.
6.2 Wa[a]be neepoog seraphimsog, nish$noh pasuk nequtta tahshe nuppohwhunau, nashpe nees8oh onkquequohhou, nashpe nees8oh onkhum wusseetash, kah nashpe nees8oh pt8wu.
6.3 Kah pasuk mishont8wohtauau onkatogeh, kah n8wau wunneetupantam, wunneetupantam, wunneetupantam Jehovah ayeuhteaanit, mamusse ohke numwohteau wussohsumoonk.
6.4 Kah squontame nepattunkquongash o[n]tahtaash nahspe 8wadtauatonkqussuonk noh mashont8adt, & wetuomut numwohta pukut
6.5 Neit nussip nutonkapunam, newutche nuttammetahwhit, newutche nen nishkeneungwe mussissitt8ne wosketomp kah nuttai nashaue nishkeneungque mussissitt8ne missinninnuog: newutche nuskesukquash naau ketass8t, Jehovah ayeuteaanit.
6.6 Neit pasuk Seraphim unnunau nuhhogkat, n8tae mohkus ohteau wunnutcheganit ne nemunuk nashpe tongs wutch Altarut.
6.7 Kah mussikquomwahtou nutt8n, kah n8wau, kusseh, yeu mussuhkom8m8 kussisset8nash, kah kummatcheseonk amaunumun; kah kuppanneseonk pahketeauun.
6.8 Wonk nunn8tam 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Lord, n8wau, howan woh negont8waeh, kah howan woh moncheaunshikqueog? neit nussip, nen yeu, ann8neh.
6.9 Kah n8wau, monchish, us yeug missinninnuog, wunnamuhkut n8tam8k, qut wohtam8hteogk: kah wunnamuhkut naum8k, qut wahteau8hteogk.
6.10 Wunogquehteaha yeug missinninnuog, kah tuhkequtteauush wuhtauog8oash, kah yanunush wuskesuk8oash: ishkont nag wutch naumwog wuskesuk8out, kah n8tamwog wutch wuhtauog8oash, kah wohtamwog wutch wuttahhou, kah woh quinnuppeog kah neetskeheaog.
6.11 Neit nussip, Lord, toh utt8che? kah namp8ham, nô pajeh keitotanash mohtupp[a]em8ug, ne toh ut wanne wutohkenat, kah weetuomash wanne wosketompaun8it, kah ohke tóuushinée touushinit.
6.12 Kah Jehovah amaunont missinninnuh en nôadtit, kah na mishe nukkodtum8onganu8uk ut nashaue ohkeit.
6.13 Qut onch pish piogque chippag ohteau, kah pish quinnuppem8, kah pish ogque meechin Tyluhtugqut, kah onatuh n8times ashkunkquamuuk mahchippogkok: netatuppe wunneetupanatamwe wuskannem ne pish wutashkunkquamuonk.
7.1 KAh nniyeup pamontog Ahaz wunnaumonuh Jotham, wunnaumonuh Uzziah Judae ketass8t, Rezin Syriae ketass8t, kah Pekah wunnaumonuh Remaliah Israelle ketass8t, kuhkuhqueog nogque en Jerusalem, wutayeuuhkontamunaoont, qut wunn8numuneau sohkomunat.
7.2 Kah unnon wek David, n8wo[u], Siria wet8womau Ephraimoh, kah wuttah ontohteau, kah wuttahhou ummissinninneumoh, onatuh touohkomukque mehtugquash mamontanuhtog waban.
7.3 Neit Jehovah unnau Isaiáhoh, sohhash yeuyeu nogkushkauonat Ahaz, ken, kah Shearjashub, kenaumon, wutchehtanniyeu kuhkuhqueeu nippessepagwe Conduit$ut, kehchemayog fullerse wutohteakonit.
7.4 Kah us; nunnikqusish, kah chequnapsh: wabes[e]hkon asuh wabesuitteahuhkon newutche neesukqunnom8ugish yeush pukuttae pohquttaash, newutche ummishe musquantam8onk Rezin weeche Siria, kah wunnaumonuh Remaliah.
7.5 Newutche Syria, Ephraim Kah wunnaumonuh Remaliah, matche ken8nittuog ayeuuhkonittue ken, n8waog,
7.6 Ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhquehtauontuh Judah, kah n8chumwehteadtuh, kah naut ayimontuh to[u]wutchahtham8onk, kah ketass8t ponontuh nashaue, wunnaumonuh Tabeal.
7.7 Kah yeu wussin Lord Jehovah, matta pish menuhkohtano, kah matta pish nnano,
7.8 Newutche uppuhkuk Syria, ne Damascus, kah uppuhkuk Damascus noh Rezin, kah wuttúhshit nequtta tahshinchage kodtum8it kah napanna, Ephraim pish sohquttahwhau, matta ummissinninnu8uneat.
7.9 Kah uppuhkuk Ephraim, ne Samaria, kah uppuhkuk Samaria, noh wunnaumonuh Remaliah: matta wunnamptam8óg wunnamuhkut matta pish kummenuhkappe[u]mw8.
7.10 Nano wonk Jehovah ken8nau Ahazoh n8wau,
7.11 Wehquetumau Jehovah kuhkinneasuonk wutche ken; wehquetush asuh ut m8n[ó]iyeuut, asuh qunuhqueé ut wóhqut.
7.12 Qut Ahaz n8wau, matta n8wehquetum8, kah matta nukqutchheau Jehovah.
7.13 Kah n8wau, n8tam8k yeuyeu, woi wek David; sun peásin ken kussauunonat wosketompaog, qut wonk kussauunnumw8 num-Manitt8m?
7.14 Newaj Lord nehenwonche nagum aninnumunkqueóg kuhkinneasuonk: Kusseh, penomp pish wompequoou, kah neechau wunnaumoniinneuh, & pish wuttissowenuh Immanuel.
7.15 Butter kah hony pish peech, onk woh wahteou sekeneamunat machuk, kah pepenamunat wanegik.
7.16 Newutche asquam mukkies wahteou sekeneamunat machuk, kah pepenamunat wanegik, ohke ne jishantaman, pish ohquanumau naneeswe ukketass8tamómuh.
7.17 Jehovah pish kuppaudtunk, kah ut kummissinninneumut, kah ut k8sh weekit, kesukodtash nish asq paómun8gish, wutch na kesukok Ephraim chabeit wutch Judah; noh Assyriae ketass8t.
7.18 Kah pish nnih, ne kesukok Jehovah pish quekqsumau 8cháussoh, noh aongkoue Egypte sepuésut, kah Bee noh Assyriae ohkeit.
7.19 Kah nag pish peyaog, kah wame pish appuog ut touushinne 8nôuhkóiyeuut, kah en hassinn[ê]kómukqut, kah ut wame assinn[e]kôussehtu, kah ut wame chipishinneuhtugquehtu.
7.20 Ne$nan kesukok, Lord pish chequodtweyaheau nashpe chequodtweyáheg, n[e]h onkquattauoncheh nashpe neg ogkomut apitcheg, nashpe Assyriae ketass8t, muppuhkuk kah wusseete wishagkinash: kah pish wonk mohtupanum weeshitt8unash.
7.21 Kah pish nnih ne kesukok, wosketomp pish wadch[a]nau wuske cowishinneoh, kah nes8oh sheepsoh.
7.22 Kah pish nnih, newutche madtaaneuk sogkodtunk ne adtahshipagsehettit, pish meech butter; newutche butter kah hony, nishnoh pasuk pish ummeechin noh sequnit ut ohkeit.
7.23 Kah pish nnih ne kesukok, nishnoh ayeuonk, uttoh adt nequt muttannonganogok weenomwussippagwash anôadtik silvere nequt muttannonganogkodtash, ne pish kôussu8 kah asinnekôussu8.
7.24 Nashpe kôuhquodtash kah ahtompeh wosketompaog na pish wuttit peyoneau, newutche wame ohke pish kôussu8, kah asinnekôussu8.
7.25 Kah wame wadchuash nish pish kodhamukish nashpe mattock, na matta pish peyomun8 qushaonk k[ó]ussog kah asinnekóussog: qut ne pish sohwhun[ó]naóont oxinog, kah wuttattashkuhkomunaóont papeississitcheg neetasuog.
8.1 NAno, Jehovah nuttinuk, neemunush mishe tuttuppagenausu, kah ne wussukwhush nashpe wosketompae pen, papaume Maher-shal$al$hash-baz.

8.4 Newutche mukkies asquam wahteau8gkup n8wónat, n8sh kah nokas, Damascusse weenauwetuongash, kah Samariae sequttahamóonk, pish amaunau ut anaquabit Assyriae ketass8t.
8.5 Jehovah wonk nukken8nuk n8wau,
8.6 Newutche yeug missinninnúog sekeneamwog Shiloahe nippeash, nish mánunnutch[uo]gish, kah weekontamwog ut Rezin, kah wunnaumonat Remaliah:

8.8 Kah noh pish paumushau Judah, noh pish anúpadto, kah pish anúchuan, pish sokkoshkittuk8, kah nean sep[á]ginont wunnuppuhwhunash, pish numwohteau ne koshkag kutohke, woi Immanuel.
8.9 Miyán8k kuhhogkaóog, woi kenaau missinninnúog, kah pish kussukqutteawhuteamw8, kah n8tam8k, wame kenaau nôohtáe wutohtimóneash, puttukquobpissegk, kah pish kussukqutteawhutteamw8, puttukquobpissegk, kah pish kussukqutteawhutteamw8.
8.10 Moáe ken8nittegk, kah pish matteagwunninno: n8wagk kutt8wonk, kah matta menuhkotano: newutche God k8weetomukqun.
8.11 Newutche Lord yeu nuttin ken8nukqun, nashpe menuhki menutcheg, kah nukkuhk8tomunk matta woh nuppomushóunat ummayeuóut yeug missinninnúog, n8wau,
8.12 N8wáhteogk, weetuódtuonk en wame nag, n[e]h pish ánoncheh yeuh missinninnuh, weetu[u]ódtuonk: kah ahque quihtam8k nag qushaongan8, asuh wabesehteogk.
8.13 Wunneetupanatamwe ogquanumok Jehovah ayeuteaanit nagum, kah noh qush8k, k[a]h noh wabesu[óm]8k.
8.14 Kah noh pish Sanctuarih88, togkussittass[im]8e qussuk, kah chamsquassunóe hassun, en naneeswe Israelle wekuóo[n]t: wutch appeh, kah sinnukkeg wutch neg wadóhkitcheg Jerusalem.
8.15 Kah monaog na ut kenugke pish togkussittassunwog, kah kepshaog, kah pish sohqussunwog, kah pish puttahhamwog, kah pish togqunóog.
8.16 Weesquabenuash wauwaonk, sealoh naumatuonk ut kenugke nunnetuhtauw[á]en[e]umut.
8.17 Kah nuppah Lord, noh padtogguhhuk wuskesuk wutch Jakob, kah nutaskauwompam[,]
8.18 Kusseh, nen kah mukkiog neh Jehovah anummiitcheh, nukkehkinneásuonganeumun, kah nummonchanatam8onganeumun ut Israelut: wutch Jehovah ayeuteaanit, noh ayit wadchuut Zion.
8.19 Kah nag unnukqueog, natinneah8k neg wámatchinahshaóngan[ú]mitcheg, kah mamontamáog, neg peant8wácheg, kah tadtumwácheg: sunnummatta woh missinninnuog natinnewhauóog um-Manitt8m8oh? wutch pomontamunutcheh en neh napunutcheh?
8.20 En naumatuonganit, kah en wauwaonganit: matta n8wahetteg neaunak yeu kutt8wonk, yeu, newutche matta wequaiyeumu.
8.21 Kah nag pish auwakonche kah kodtupp8e uppannupushoneau: kah pish nnih, nag kodtupwehettit, nag pish m8m8skumáog wuhhogkauh, kah matanumaog ukketass8tam8m8oh, kah um$Manitt8m8oh kah pish ushpuhquaéog.
8.22 Kah nag pish monunneamwog ohke, kah kusseh wuttamehpunáonk, kah pohkenái, pogkenum[ó]e wuttamehpunáonk, kah nag pish n8hkauôog en pohkenahtu.
9.1 QUt onch, pohkennumóonk matta pish neanéinn8, wunn8wadtaméhpunadt, negonne ogguhse onkapunadtunk Zebulone ohke, kah Naphtalie ohke, kah ompetak, wutúhque onkquanu[m]wéheuh, ut kehtahhanne mayit, ogkomut Jordan, ut wutohtimóinne Galile.
9.2 Missinninnúog neg pomushácheg pohkenahtu naumwog mishe wequai: neg wadohkitcheg nupp8ongane onkauohtáe ohkeit, neh 8wôhsumauoh.
9.3 Kummuttaanteóh wutohtimóneas, kah matta nano mishehteaou wekontamóonk: weekontamwog ut anaquabean, neaunak kepenumwe weekontamóonk, kah neáhhenn8weekontamwéhettit wosketompaog, chachabenumohetticheh sequttahhamóonk.
9.4 Newutche kussohqutahham 8wéassue yoakumoh, kah wuttippomóne anwohhou: wussonkqutchóh8wae pogkommunk, neane ut Midiane kesukodtut.
9.5 Newutche nishnoh wutayeuwuttuonk ayeuhteaen, ne wodtauatonkquodt, kah hogk8unash unuhkónash ut wusqueheonganit, qut yeu pish nashpe chikkósuonk, kah n8tae wuttuhqunash.
9.6 Newutche ut kuhhogkanónut mukkies neetu, ut en kuhhogkanónut Wunnaumoniin magun, kah nanaánittuonk pish ohteau ut wuttukeit: kah pish ussowesu Monchanu nukqussuaen Ken8s8waénin, Manuhkésit God, Machemapit Wut8shimau, Wunohteáe Sontim.
9.7 Kah matta pish wohkukquoshininno nano missáe wunnanawunnum[o]onk, kah wunohteáonk, ut wutâppuonganit David, kah ut wutass8tam8onganit, wunohtauunat, kah menehkheonat, nashpe wussittumóonk kah s[á]mpweseonk, yeu$wutch onk yean micheme: wus$zealum Lord ayeuhtea[a]nit yeu pish wutussen.
9.8 Lord negonshhuau kutt8onk en Jakobut, kah upp[a]gs8kqun Israel.
9.9 Kah wame missinninnúog pish wahteauog, Ephraim kah wadohkitcheg Samaria, neg pi[t]uánumóe kah menehketeaháe an8wacheg.
9.10 Briksash penushaash, qut pish n8weekitteahtómun wunnáguttahham8e qussukquanash: Sycomorúhtugquash tummehthamunash, qut pish nutôs8wunnununnánonash en cedaruhtugqut.
9.11 Newaj Jehovah pish ayeuuhkonittue wunoht[a]uou ummatwomoh Rezinoh, kah weech8hamau ummatwomoh.
9.12 Syriansog negonáeu, kah Philistiansog wuttát, kah nag mahchipp8og Israeloh nashpe woshwohtáe mutt8n: newutche yeu waame, ummusquanittam8onk matta am[a]émun8, qut wunnutcheg ashpumme su[n]maguna[u]sh.
9.13 Ne[u]utche missinninnuog matta quinnuppeog en néh togkomukquehetticheh, kah matta natinneahwho8og Jehovah ayeuhteaanit.
9.14 Newaj Jehovah tummehthog wutch Israelut muhpuhkuk, kah wussukqun, wuhtuk puppishashquash ut pasuk kesukodtut.
9.15 Kohchisu8it, kah quohtianumukqussit, noh muppuhkuk88; kah quoshodtumwaen noh kohk8tomwehteadt pann8waongash, noh wussukqu[n]eiyeu.
9.16 Newutche sampshano[n]cheg yeuh missinninnuh uppanneseaheouh, kah neg neh sagkompagunukqhetticheh paguanuoh.
9.17 Newaj matta Lord woh weekontamuonunk wuskeneuh, asuh matta pish monanumôou touwyesoh, kah sekousquoh, newutche nish$noh p[a]suk eiantogkei, kah matcheseaenin, kah nish$noh mutt8n as8tueyeum8: newutche yeu wame, matta ummusquanittam8onk qushkemun8, qut ash s[um]ogohteau wunnutcheg.
9.18 Newutche matcheseonk ogque chikohteau n8taut: pish mahchukiswau kôussoh kah assinnekôussoh, kah pish nashqunneau touo[h]komukque kuppahtu, kah neg pish ogque waabpem8uk pukuttau.
9.19 Nashpe ummusquanittam8onk Jehovah ayeuteaunit ohke pohkenai kah pish missinninnuog ogqunneunkqussuog ne woh chogkohtag: wanne pish howan kushpaoou weematuh.
9.20 Kah pish wuttinnohkounit wutch neemp8au kah pish onch kodtupp8, k[a]h pish menadchipp8, kah matta pish tap[e]p8og, nag pish meechwog nish$noh pasuk wuhpitteanue weyaus.
9.21 M[e]nasseh, Ephraimoh, kah Ephraim Manassehoh: kah nag na moeu pish ayeuuhkon[á]og Judahoh.
9.22 Newutche yeu$wutch wame, ummusquantam8onk matta qushkemun8h, qut ash sumogohteau wunnutcheg.
10.1 MIssi wutonkapunnaongan8 kohk8wachég mat sampweusseae naumatuongash: kah wosukuhh8keg ûhquanum8ongash, nash kohkinnum8hettichish.
10.2 Qushkeheonao[u]t quenahukqutcheg wutch wussittum8onganit, kah ama[u]numauonat wussampwohtoongan8 wutch machekitcheg: onk woh sekousquoh tohquomáog: onk woh nag mukk8ki[n]ó[o]g touwiêsoh.
10.3 Kah toh woh kutussemw8 natauwahuwae kesukok, kah pagu[a]nuonk peyont wutch n8adtut? howan pish kutushphouonomw8 wutch kuttannumunkqunnaout? kah uttoh pish kénukkodtumunneau kussohsumoongan8?
10.4 M[e]hcheu nen, nag pish n[à]uwaehtauaog kuppishagkinnuw[h]enuh, kah nag pish penushaog agwu nohshitcheg: yeu nashpu wame, asquam qushkemun8 ummusqu[an]tam8onk qut askq wuñutcheg sussumohogteau.
10.5 Woi wut-Assyrian nummusquantam8e sasamatuhh8waontug, kah ne anwohhou ut wunnutchegan8wout, ne nummusquanittam8onk.
10.6 Nutann8noog ayuuhkontamunat eiantukeiyeue wutohtimoin, kah ayeuuhkononat missinninnuog n[e]g musquanumogig nuttinninnumau meechummuonk nemunnumunat sequehtahhamukish, kah nemunnumunat wutohqu[a]muwaongan8, kah tahtasku[h]kauonaoont onatuh matehchuogkok tau8maogwash.
10.7 Qut matta ne ukkodsei[n], onk wuttah maata ne wuttenamam8un: qut ne wuttahh8wout, paguanonat, kah koshksumunat wutohtimoneash matta ogguhsinash.
10.8 Newutche n8w[a]u sunnummatta nussontimomog pannuppe kehtass8tam8og?
10.9 Suñummatta Calmo, neane Carchemish? Sunnummatta Hamath neane Arphad? sunnummatta Samaria neane Damaskus?
10.10 Neane nunnutcheg namehteau nunneukontungane kehtass8tam8ongash; kah neg unnunneukontunkanog anue mishanumukqussuog, onk neg wadchiitcheg Jerusalem kah Samaria
10.11 Neane nea[n]teau Samaria kah neh wuttinneu[x]o[h]tunkanoh, Sunnummatta ne nan woh nuttinteauouun Jerusalem, kah wuttinneukontunkanoh?
10.12 Newajeh pish n$nahk, ne Lord pogkojteunk wame wutanakausuonk ut wadchuut Sion, kah ut Jerusalem, nussasamatuhham ummeechummuonk máhshetahh8wae ketass8t ut Assyria, kah wussohsumóe quonohquttauwompuonk.
10.13 Newutche n8wau, nashpe nunnutchegane menuhkesuonk yeu nutussen, kah nashpe n8waantamóonk, newutche nutompuwussuénúh: kah nutontahtoh ukkuhkinonkanóash missinninnuog, kah nummukk8kinóog wunnompak8unóash, kah nuttinnuhkauóog neg noh wadohkitcheg, onatuh menuhkesuenuut.
10.14 Kah nunnutcheg mehqunum 8weenauwetuongan8ash misinninnuog, neáne wadchishadt: & neáne mohmounuk wôanash, uttiyeush sequnumukish, nuttinne mohmóunumun wame ohke, kah wanne howan wutt8we wuttauóuunash, asuh wôhshinum8 wutt8n, asuh sesék8.
10.15 Sun togkunk woh waenomau wuhhogkuh ayuuhkononat neh kauhunkquahukqutche: asuh poksunkquonk sun woh mishehheau wuhhogkuh ayeuuhkonau neh mâmamóntinukqutcheh? neáne sauobpunk nehenwonche mâmamo[n]tshont ayeuuhkonónát ashpunukqutcheh, asuh neàne anwohhou nehenwonche ushpéit, neane matta mahtugk88uk.
10.16 Newajeh Lord, um-Manitt8m8uh kehche8shaog, pish ununau ônauwussinutcheh, ut kenugke waonogqutcheg, kah ut agwe wussohsum8onganit, pish pasqunnánum ch[i]kohsumóo[n]k, neane n8tae chiko[k]sum8ongánit.
10.17 Kah 8wequa8m Israel ne pish n8to8, kah 8neetupanatam8moh noh n8n8uneau: kah pish nashqutteau, kah mahchekuswau wutásinnekôsumoh, kah ukkôussumoh ut pasuk kesukodtut.
10.18 Kah pish mahchikussum wuttouohkomukque sohsumóonk, kah ummissegane ohteuk, naneeswe keteahogkou kah muhhog: kah nag pish ogqueneungqussuog noh kôunuk muttô[a]gk, sauwunuk.
10.19 Kah sequeneádtunkish wuttouohkomukque mehtugquash pish ogguhsinash, onk woh mukkies 8sukuhhumunash.
10.20 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok, neg sequttahwhutcheg Israel, kah neg wadchiitcheg Jakob wekit neg pohquohhukeg, matta pish wonk wutompattussun8unah noh togkomo[n]t, qut pish ompatussen Jehovah, 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, wunnamuhkutée.
10.21 Neg sequttahwhutcheg pish qushkeog, sequttahhamauutcheh Jakob, en masugkenuk Manit.
10.22 Newutche tókonogque kummissinninneumog Israel wutteas8unneáont ketahhane nagu[n]tuut, neg aguhsikeg pish qushkeog: mahchekonaéonk noh káhtimit, pish tomogkeu ut sampweusseonganit.
10.23 Newutche Lord wut-Jehovanum8oh ayeuteaog, pish ayeuau mahchekonae onkoh, noh kahtimit ut nashaue wame ohkeit.
10.24 Newutche yeu wussin Lord God ayeuwutteaunit, woi nummissinninneumog wadohkéogish Sion, ahque wabesuón8k wut-Assyrian: noh pish kuttogkomuk pogkomunk, kah pish kutayeuuhkonittue tahshinumunk wutanwohhou, ne asehetteup Egyptianéog.
10.25 Newutche ogguhsese sepe, kah unkque m8squanetam8onk pish ahquohteau kah nummusquanittam8onk ut uppaguanuongan8óut.
10.26 Kah Jehovah ayeuteaunit pish 8wogkauunumauoh sasamatahwhuttuonk netatupe paguanáonk Midian, kishke Orebe qussukquanit: kah onatuh ne ônohtagkup uppogkomunk woskeche kehtahanit, ne pish wuttinne tahshinumun neanheomp wut-Egyptianeh.
10.27 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok, 8wéanun pish amaunumun wutch kuttugkeet, kah weyoakumoh wutch kussittipukanit, kah yoak pish matcheheau newutche sesequnáonk.
10.28 Noh peyau Ajath, noh pahmohkom Migron, ut Michmash na upponamun ukkenúm8ongash.
10.29 Qushkodteáog ósukongkanit, nag kaueneau Geba, Ramah wabesu, uk-Gibeahum Saul wussem8.
10.30 Mishont8ash, woi wuttaunoh Gallim: n8tamwah Laish, woi kuttamunge Anathoth.
10.31 Madmenah ontsum, wadohkitcheg Gebim moèog wussemuneát.
10.32 Ashpume pish appu ut Nob ne kesukok: pish ayeuuhkonittue tattauunkauau wunnutcheg 8wadcheum wuttaunoh Zion; Jerusaleme wadchu.
10.33 Kusseh; Lord, Jehovah ayeuteaanit pish tumehtham wuttuhqunash nashpe wabesuonk, kah quaquonunkquokish pish kouwehthamunash, kah pahtuánumweenunkqussit pish hohpaheau.
10.34 Kah noh pish tumehtham touohkomukque kókuppagish, nashpe m8uhshog, kah Lebanon pish penushau wutch masukkenuk.
11.1 KAh sauobpunk pish wutchegen 8wepunkquamut Jesse, kah Wuttuhk pish wutchegen 8wadchabukqut.
11.2 Kah wunnashauanitt8moh Jehovah pish wutapehtunkquoh, wa[a]ntamóe kah wohwohtamóe nashauanit, kuhquttue kah menuhkesue nashauanit, wahteóe nashauanit, kah qushónat Jehovah.
11.3 Kah pish wutayimunkquoh kogkinne wohtamu[m] ut quoshonat Jehovah, kah noh matta pish unne wussittum8 neaunak wuskesukque naum8onk, asuh áushkomuóou neane wohtog wutch wehtauogkut.
11.4 Qut nashpe sampweusseonk pish wussumau matchekuoh, kah pish áushkomuau nashpe sampwagk, wutche manunnissitcheg ut ohkeit: kah noh pish togkodtam ohke nashpe wutt8n8e pogkomunk, kah nashpe wussissitt8n8e nashauonk pish nushau matchet8oh.
11.5 Kah sampweusseonk ne pish uppetukquobpis ut wusseganit: kah pabahtanumukqussuonk ne pish uppetukquobpis ut wutt8unussit.
11.6 Kah wonk mukquoshom pish weetomau lamboh, kah leopard pish sepsinn8wehtauau kidsoh, kah kalfsoh, kah qunnonouwem, kah wanogqunutcheh moeu, kah mukkies pish wussagkompanoh
11.7 Kah cow kah mosk pish weetatup8tuog, wunnechan8oh pish neesinwoh, kah qunnonou pish meech sékupoghegash onatuh ox.
11.8 Kah n8n8e mukkies pish tannuppompu 8wonogqut asp, kah 8chininnáe mukkies pish pethennum wunnutcheg sesegq 8wonogqut.
11.9 Matta nag pish woskehuwau8og asuh pagwahteau8og ut wame n8neetupanatamwe wadcheumut: newutche ohke pish numwohteau wahheáonk Jehovah, onatuh nippe nuhkokkog keihtoh.
11.10 Kah ne kesukok na pish 8wadchabuk Jesse ne pish nepatag wutch muttaagk kônunumauont missinninneuh; nehhoh Gentils pish wunnatinneahwhoh, kah wutanwôhsin8onk pish sohsum88.
11.11 Kah pish nnih ne kesukok, Lord pish wunnutcheg nahohtoeu ne ponumun, uppohquohwhunonat asquttawhutcheh ummissinninneumoh wutch Assyria, kah wutch Egypt, kah wutch Pathros, kah wutch Cush, kah wutch Elam, kah wutch Shinar, kah wutch Hamath, kah wutch kehtahhanne aquidnehtu.
11.12 Kah noh pish wunnashau muttaagk kohkinnunnumunutcheh wutche wutohtimoneash, kah pish miyanau Israelle pagkenitcheg, kah pish miyanau Judahe nanwisinitcheh, wutch yaue p8chag muttaohke.
11.13 Wutiskauanittuonk Ephraim pish amaem8, kah ummatwomoh Judah pish tummehtahwhoog, Ephraim matta pish iskauonoou Judahoh, kah Judah matta pish m8m8sqheoou Ephraimoh.
11.14 Qut nag pish ushpuhh8waog, ut wuttugkeout Philistinsog, nogque en wutcheksuiyeu, nag pish matcheheaog neg wadohkitcheg wutchepwoieu moaeu nag pish ponamwog wunnutchegan8 ut Edom kah Moab: kah wunneechanoh Ammon pish wunn8swehtauouh.
11.15 Kah Jehovah pish papuhquanne paguanau ketahanne Egyptiane meenan, kah nashpe ummishetahshinneumoh pish tattauohteau wunnutcheg waabe sepuut, kah pish wuttogkodtamun ut nesausuk tahshe po[m]utchuanit, kah pish qushkodteaheau missinninnuh nobohteaouut.
11.16 Kah ne pish nanwe ummayou asquttahwhutcheh ummissinninneumoh, nég asquttawhutcheg wutch Assyria, neanagkup wutch Israel ne kesukok waj sohhog ohkeit Egypt.
12.1 KAh nekesukok pish kussim, woi Jehovah, k8waeenomush: tohkonogque kummusquanuminneah, kummusquantam8onk qushkem8, kah kuttapheh.
12.2 Kusseh God noh n8wadchanitteaonk: nuppabuhtanum, kah matta n8wabesuh, newutche Lord Jehovah noh nummenuhkesuonk, kah nukket8homaonk, noh wonk n8wadchanitteaonkanin.
12.3 Newutche wekontamoe pish k8thuppam8 wutch wadchanittuae wuttahhamonganit.
12.4 Kah ne kesukok pish kussimw8 wowussumok Jehovah, wehquetumok 8wesuonk, wahteauwahuwagk wutusseongash ut kenugke missinninnutu, missohham8k 8weesuonk mishehteauun.
12.5 Ket8hamok Jehovah newutche noh usseu waunnegukish, yeu wahteauun ut wame ohkeit.
12.6 Wuttauate[u]kqussek, kah mishont8wagk ken wadohkean Zion, newutche masugkenuk 8neetupanatam8moh Israel ut kenashomut.
13.1 OOWeanun Babilon, ne Isaiah wunnaumonuh Amoz nagkup.
13.2 Tahshinum8k muttaagk ut kussòhkôiyeuut, mishont8wanumok, tattauwunnumok kenutcheg onk petutteaog wuttusquontam8out puhponkompoog.
13.3 Nuttaann8nomp n8neetupanatam8mog: kah n8wehomomp nummenuhkeseumog, wutche nummusquanittam8onk, neg weekontogeg ut nukqununkqussuonganit
13.4 OOwadtauatonkqussuongan8 monacheg ut wadchuuhkontu, ogqunneunkqussu[o]g mutta[a]nukeg missinninnuog wogkouee wuttauatonkqussuonganu8 wutohtim[ô]unne tass8tam8ongash miyaé[m]8ash: Jehovah ay[e]uteaunit 8sukkomp[a]nh mattompagwe ayeuteuh.
13.5 Nag 8mwog nôadtit wutohtimóneat, wutch weekqshik kesuk, noh Jehovah, kah ummusquantamwe auwohteaongash, pagwohtauunat mamusse ohke.
13.6 Mau8k, newutche ukkesukkodtum Jehovah paswohteau: pish ogque peyau pagwanuonganit wutch wame manuhkesitteáut.
13.7 Newutche wame menutchegash pish sauunum8m8ash, kah nishnoh wosketomp wuttah pish mohtupohteau.
13.8 Kah nag pish wabesuog: onkquommom8ongash kah unkquanum8ongash pish wuttohqunóuh; nag pish unúhquommom8og mittamwossis neechadt, nag pish chepsh[á]ettuog, wuskesuk8oash pish onatuh n8hn8unag.
13.9 Kusseh ukkesukodtum Jehovah peyom8, onkuppunohteáe naneeswe nashpe unkque musquanittam8onk kah mishe musquantam8onk, touwishinneat ohke, kah noh pish paguanau ummatcheseaéneumoh na$wutch.
13.10 Newutche kesukque anogqsog kah chippanogqussog matta pish wóhsumóog: nepauz pish pogkenum sohhog, kah nanepâushadt matta pish 8wequai wohsum8mun8.
13.11 Kah pish nussasamatahham muttaok, wutche uppaneseongan8, kah matchetoog wutch ummatcheseongan8oash: kah uppehtuánúmweenungqussuongan8 pehtuánum8og, n8wohkuhquôshitteauwahtauun: kah nutti[u]hquonkqutteoh uppehtuánumwenunkqussuongan8 uhqueneunkqussitcheg.
13.12 Kah wosketomp nutanue mish[ô]adteh onk ne wanegik gold: nux wosketomp onk ne Ophire golde wedge.
13.13 Newutche nuttattauwohteam kesukquash, kah o[h]ke pish ontohteau wutch wutayeuonganit, ut ummusquanittam8onganit Jehovah ayeuteaunit, kah ne kesukok uhque musquantog.
13.14 Kah pish tatuppeyeu8 key8hkauut ayomp, kah ontauh sheeput, ne matta howan wadchanunkeh, nishnoh pasuk qushkeu en nehenwonche missinninneumut, kah pish spuhh8waog nishnoh pasuk en nehenwonche wutohket.
13.15 Nishnoh pasuk noh namhit pish asishahtahwh[á]u: kah nishnoh pasuk noh weetomont pish penushau nashpe togkodteg.
13.16 Kah wonk ummukkieseum8uh pish sukquóhkônunk an[a]quabhettit, week8oash pish mukkinumwó[n]tamunash, kah ummittamwuss8oh pish chekehéonunneoh.
13.17 Kusseh, n8wogkouun Medsog ayeuuhkonittue n[a]goh, neg matta pish tohhe[n]tup anatam8gig silver: kah wonk gold matta wuttapeneam8uneau.
13.18 Wutahtompeyeuoh pish sukquehtahwaog 8skeneum8uh, kah nag pish matta kitteamonteanumau8og ummeechu[m̃]uonk ôontomuk: wuskesuk88ash matta pish wohquanumauôog mukkiesoh.
13.19 Kah Babylon wussohsum8wongan8oash ass8tam8onganog, 8neetuonk Caldeansog, ummissugken8ongan8 pish onatuh God kepuhteadt Sodom kah Gomorrah.
13.20 Matta pish wonk wutohkein, asuh matta pish ayéin wutch pometuonganit onk ye[á]n pometuonganit: kah Arabian matta pish na 8weekéin, kah nanawesheepsaenuog matta pish na ponam8uneau wekuòash.
13.21 Qut touohkomukque puppinashimwog na pish wusseepsineau, kah wekuoash pish wunn[á]numw[à]pine u[t] [n]ishkeneunkque ow[à]asineg, kah k8k8khôsog na pish 8tohkineau, kah Satyrsog ka pish wuttit pumukoneau
13.22 Kah munnohhanne puppinashimwog pish 8n8og ut mahchikomukque wekuout, kah Dragonsog ut 8nekomuk8out: kah wutaquompiyeum pas8che peyaum8, kah ukkesukodtum8oash matta pish sepohtan8ash.
14.1 NEwutche Jehovah pish monanumau Jakoboh kah ohnch pish pepenauau Israeloh, kah pish upponuh nehenwonche wutohkeyeu[o]ut: kah pen8wot pish weetomuk: kah pish menuhkappuog wekit Jakob.
14.2 Kah missinninnuog pish nag wuneemunnouh, kah uppas8ouh ut wutayeuongan8out, kah wek Israel nag pish 8tohtauonganinnéauh ut wutohkit Jehovah wutche wuttinneumuonk, kah mittamwossisse wuttinneumineunk, kah pish ummissi[n]uhkonauh nag neh masinohteacheg: kah pish nanawunaog neh woskhikqhettipoh.
14.3 Kah pish n$nih, ne kesukok Jehovah anwosumwahikquean wutch kutungquanumwinneat, kah wutch k8wabesuonganit, kah wutch siogke missinnainneat ut$toh adt wuttinneumuhkonuninumukup.
14.4 Neit pish kussim yeu woweenuhwh[á]muae kutt8wonk ayeuuhkonittue Babylone ketass8t: uttoh in woskehuwaenin wôhkuhquosinin?
14.5 Jehovah pohquetahham wutánwohh8un8 matchet8og, kah uppiuhquttumwe anwoh8un8 nananuwach[e]g.
14.6 Noh musquantamwe togkomont missinninnuh nagwutteauhshine, moh musquantamwe nanawunuk wutohtimoneash, noh woskeheau, kah matta howan wuttamehh[u]waunuh.
14.7 Mamusse ohke anwohsin, kah chequnohteau: nag pohqua8homaog
14.8 Nux qunonuhquaog kummuskauanatam8[ó]nukquog, Lebannonne chikupog n8waog, nadteuh pagkenumuk, matta kouuhkukquaenin ayeuuhkonittue nukkuhkuhquéhtunk8un.
14.9 Chepiohkomuk wutch agwe ontohteau wutche ken, kenogskunkqunat peyôa[n], wogkouineau n[á]pinitche wutche ken, wame puppunkompóog muttaohkit, wutomohkinuh wutch wutappuonganehtu, wame wutohtimóinne ketass8tamwog.
14.10 Wame nag pish ket8kaog, kah kuttukquog, ken wonk sun ken8chumwes netatupe nenawun? ken k[ù]ttatuppinneunkqusseumumun?
14.11 K8nadchéseum paudtauun weenohkeit, kah k8wadtauatonkqussue wanont8wagk: 8hqua[ó]g sepakéog ut kutagwéiyeumut, kah 8hquaog kenuhkuhkunk.
14.12 Uttoh kuttinne penushon wutch kesukqut, woi Lucifer, wunnaumonuh mohtompan? uttoh kittin tummehtawhuttean en ohkeit, ken n8chumwehteauop wutohtimóneash?
14.13 Newutche kussip ut kuttahhut, nukkuhkuhquem en kesukqut, pish nuttahshinum nutappuonk anue wutannogqusseumut God: kah wonk nukquenáp mukkinneáe wadchuut nannumiy[ê]u.
14.14 Nukkuhkuhquem anue ne sohkunkquok mahtókqs, pish ne[a]nenunkqus noh anue quanunkquapit.
14.15 Qut pish ken8t[n]init en chepiohkomukqut, ut sussippôe psahtheganit.
14.16 Neg nogqueáneg pish kuppapásinunk kah kenatwánumuk, n8waog, sun yeuoh wosketomp noh nunkshadtauwahtunkup ohke, noh nánukkishadtunkup ketass8tam8ongash?
14.17 Noh áyikup muttaok onatuh touohkomuk, kah pagwatunkup wutotanash? noh matta wohshinumauonk wek8 ukkupshagki[n]omuh?
14.18 Wame wutohtimóinne wuttahs8timwog, nag wame sohsumohteásinwog, nishnoh pasuk nehenwonceh wekit.
14.19 Qut ken kussohwhôhkonit wutch weenohkeit, onatuh nishkeungque wuttuhqunit, kah onatuh wuthogk8un8oash neg na[h]shitcheg, papashpetahwhut togkodteg, neg w8mussitcheg psahthegane qussukquanéhtu, ontuh nupp8e muhhog tahtashkuhka[ú]ut ut musseetut.
14.20 Matta pish nag k8weechayeumôog posekinitteóg, newutche kuppagquadtoh kutohke, kah nushonat kummissinninnúmog; 8skannémunnu matchet8g matta pish w[a]eenódtum8un.
14.21 Quoshauwehtau wunneechanoh shehteaénuh wutche ummatcheseongan88ash 8sh8oh, nag woh matta wutomohkéinnaout, kah matta wutohta8unaóut ohke, kah matta numwohtau8unat wuskesukqut muttaok 8tanash.
14.22 Newutche nag ayeuuhkonittue n8waabehtauóog, n8wau Jehovah ayeuteaunit: kah pish nuttummetahham wutch Babylon, wesuonk, wunnaumoniin, kah 8w[á]dtunkquassin, n8wau Jehovah.
14.23 Kah wonk n8ta[h]tauonga[n]éhheon Bittern, kah nippissepagwash, kah nutchekhamun nashpe paguanue chekhikunk, n8wau Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
14.24 Jehovah ayeuteaunit chadchekeyeuau, n8wau, wunnamuhkut, neanantamup, ne pish n$nih,, kah ne pakodtantamup, ne pish unne menehketeauun.
14.25 Nuppokshan wut-Assyrian ut nutohkit, kah ut n8wadchumehtu nuttahtashkuhkau ut agwe nusseetut, neit pish weyoakum8oh âmaehtunkquog, kah 8weanun pish amaem8 wutch wuttugkeit.
14.26 Yeu pogkodtantam[ó]onk ne pakodtantamuk ut mamusse ohkeit, kah yeu menutcheg ne samogkinumuk en wame wutohtimóneat.
14.27 Newutche Jehovah ayeuhteaanit uppogkodtanatamun, kah howan woh uppanshadta[u]wahtauun? kah wunnutcheg summagohteau, & howan woh ukqushkinnumun?
14.28 Ne kodtum8k ketass8t Ahaz napuk, yeu wéanunúo8p.
14.29 Ahque muskouantash ken mamusse Palestina, newutche uppogkomunk noh togkomukqueóp pokshau: newutche wutch 8wadchaubukqut ask8k pish 8tsohhamu[n] sesekq, kah ummechummuonk pish n8tae pt8wée ask8k.
14.30 Kah ummohtommegitteomoh noh machekit pish meetsuoh, kah quenauhikquit pish wunniyeue sepsin[,] kah nunnehto k8wadchabuk nashpe mashshagquot, kah noh pish nushau sequttahhamaúúnumukeh.
14.31 OO[n]sh, woi squont, maush, woi keitotan, ken mamusse Palestina kussukqunit, newutche pukuttau pish 8m88 naunummiyeu, kah wanne pish nussiyeoh ut ukkuhquttumoe aquompiyeumut.
14.32 Neit toh pish unneu namp8hamauau wutann8teamweneum8uh wutohtimmoneunk? Jehovah ummenuhkehteauun Zion, kah ummissinninnúme matchekeumoh, pish uppanuhtantamunin.
15.1 OWeanun Moab: newutche nukonáeu Ar ut Moab mohtupohsin, kah chequnapheau, newutche nukonàeu Kir ut Moab moh[tu]pohsin, kah chequnapheau.
15.2 Kuhkuhquéi en Bajith kah en Dibon, qunuhqui ayeuonganéhtu, mauunat: Moab pish 8nowontam Nabo, kah Medeba: wame uppuhkukquash pish mukukkiyeuash, kah nishnoh weeshitt8n tummuhs[ô]su.
15.3 Ut wutaumaogk8out, pish puttukquobpissuwontamog man8tionak: ut woskechekomukquehtu kah ut wutaumaogk8out, nish$noh pasuk pish 8n8, m8cheke mauun.
15.4 Kah Heshbon pish mau kah Elealeh 8wadtauatonkqussuonk pish n8tamun weehque Jahaz, newaj ukkenauwamee matwomoh pish mishont8wauh, uppomantamoonk pish uhquanittamhik.
15.5 Nuttah pish mishont8wau wutche Moab, 8sem8moh pish usishauh Zoar, nashwe kodtumohkog kouwashinem; newutche adt kutóhkoag Luhith[.] nashpe mauonk pish kuhkuhqueog, newutche ut Haronaimme mayut, na pish wutch waapem8 paguanue mauonk.
15.6 Newutche Nimrimme nippeash pish touwushinneash: newutche moskehtuash ohp8htaash, askoshquosh wanne ohtan8ash, wanne ashkoshqun8.
15.7 Newutche madtauneuk ne ohtauwehettit, kah ne wadchanumohettit, pish ummonchadtauunneau, en anumussikkuppeyeue sepuwussut.
15.8 Newutche wuttauatonkqussuonk quinnuppem8 en wame wussissippoiyeumut Moab: 8n8onk weehque Eglaim kah 8n8onk weque wussissippoiyeumut Be[o]r$Elim.
15.9 Newutche wunnuppeimash Dimon pish numwohteau musqueheonk, newutche nukk8tne pas8 ut Dimon qunn8n8óh quentunkqutch noh pohquohhogkup wutch Moab, kah neg asquttahwhutcheg ut ohkeit.
16.1 NEgonshhuagk lamb en noh nanawunuk ohke, wutch Sela wehque touohkomukqut, wehque 8wadchumut wuttaunoh Zion.
16.2 Newutche pish n$nih, onatuh kogkeish[á]e psukses: ne pish wuttattúppeyeuwunneau wuttaunoh Moab, ut Arnone t8skeonganit.
16.3 Kogkáhquttegk, ussek wussittum8onk, ogquehteaush kutonkauohtom nohkog, ut noeu pohshequaut, puttogquehtog neg sohwohteamukeg, ahque wa[n]shan8k noh nánwushadt.
16.4 Neg pakenogeg wutch ontogkit weetomukqush Moab, ken wunnenéhuwaéneush wutch wuskesukqut woskhuadt, newutche mukk8kinnuwaenúh wohkuhquosinwoh, matchehuwaenin áhquappu, woskehuw[à]enuog mahchekussuog wutch ohkeit.
16.5 Kah monaneteáe appeuonk pish menehketeauun; kah pish ukquenappin ut wunnamuhkuteyeu8ut, ut wut-tabernaklumut David, wussittum kah natinneham wussittumóonk kah kenuppeteau sampweusseonk.
16.6 Nunn8tamumu[n] uppehtuanumôonk Moab (noh mishe pittuánum8) ukqunuhqunneunkqussuonk, kah uppehtuánumóonk, kah ummusquantamóonk: qut uppann8waongash matta pish ne nano.
16.7 Newaj pish Moab 8n8wonont Moaboh, nishnoh pasuk pish 8n8, wutch ukquenohtag8mash Kir-hareseth, pish kummaum8 wunnamuhkut togkomóog.
16.8 Newutche Heshbone ohteuhkonash kôhkutt[a]ash, 8wenomassippog Sibmah, wussontim8m8oh penuwohteaog pokshadtóog negonneyeugish wutohkehte[a]ongash, peyaog wehque Jazer, nanwushaog pannuppe touohkomuk, wuttuhqunash summagnunumunash, qushkodteaog keitoh.
16.9 Newutche nummauwétam nashpe Jazere mauonk, 8wenomussippog Sibmah, kutogquechipanash nussippeguash, woi Heshbon, kah Elealeth: newutche mishontowaonk wutche sequ[a]nnáe kummeechum8mash, kah wutche kukkepenum8onk penusheau.
16.10 Kah wekontamóonk amaunumun, kah muskouantam8onk wutch mishummeechume ohteuhkonit, kah ut weenominneohtekontu, na matta pish ket8hammaonganunn8, kah matta pish mishont8waonganunn8: tahtashkuhkomwenuog pish matta tahtashkuhkom8og wine ut wine$pressut, n8wohkuhquoshitteop ummishont8waonk.
16.11 Newutche nunnogkus pish wunnont8wanshau Moaboh onatuh Harp: kah nuttinnomiyeum Kirha[r]esh.
16.12 Kah pish nnih, naumuk Moab sauwunum ut qunuhque ayeuonganit, neit pish peyau ut wus$Sanctuareumut peantamunat: qut matta pish sohkohseu.
16.13 Yeu kutt8onk ne an8wop Jehovah papaume Moab, nádteuh na ahquompak.
16.14 Qut yeuyeu Jehovah ukket8kontamun, n8wau, ash nanshwu kodtumun8gkup, onatuh ukkodtum8ut wahwuttinninneumuk, kah wuss[ô]hsum8onk Moab pish pogkodchimau, nashpe mamusse neg mataanukeg: kah neg asquttahwhutcheg pish ogguhsesuog kah n8chumwesuog.
17.1 OWeanun Damascus, kusseh, Damascus amaunôi wutch wut8tanau[n]neat, kah pish webe weep8toou,
17.2 Ukkeitotanash Aroer ahquontamunash, nish pish wutch puppinashimwog, neg pish sepsukeg, kah matta pish howan 8wabesuwaheuh.
17.3 Wonkônous wonk pish wohkukquoshin wutch Ephraimut, kah ass8tamoonk wutch Damaskus, kah Syriae sequttahwhutceg: nag pish tatuppeyeu8og wussohsum8ongan8out wunnaumonuh Israel, n8wau Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
17.4 Kah ne kesukok pish nnih, wussohsumóonk Jakob pish woss[à]ppeteáuun, kah 8weeyauseé wees pish ônauwuss[é]um8.
17.5 Kah pish yáneyéu8 kepenumwaenúut kepenuk weatchiminneash, kah kepenuk missunkquaminash wutch wuhputteit, kah pish yaneyeu8 noh kepenuk missunkquaminnash ut Rephaimme 8n[ó]uhkôi.
17.6 Qut onch pish mukupashquae weenominneash na$ut sequnumunash: onatuh né[u]emonteamuk olivuhtug, neesinash asuh nishwinásh berrisash ut wanashquonk: yauunash asuh napanna onkouee mishummeechummue wuttuhqunash, wussin Lord um-Manitt8moh Israel.
17.7 Ne kesukok wosketomp pish monunnea[n]au neh kezhukqutcheh, kah wuskesukquash pish k[e]nompamau 8neetupanatam8m[ó]h Israel.
17.8 Kah matta pish monunneauôou Altarsash wunnutchegane anakaus[ú]onk, kah matta pish kenompattam8 ne wuttinwhunnutcheash kezteunkupash, asuh kuppahtu, asuh nunneukontunkanog.
17.9 Ne kesukok ummenuhke 8tanash pish tatuppeyeu8ash ahquontam8e wuttuhkq, kah wanaskkunkquame wuttuhq, ne sequenum[o]hettit, newutche wunnaumonuh Israel: kah na pish tauwushin.
17.10 Newutche k8wanánum k8wadchanuae Manit, kah matta kummehqutonam8 kumme[n]uhkesue qussukquanum, newaj pish ohkehteaan wunneohkehteaongash, & pish kutohteuhkon penowe ontsohkodtoongash.
17.11 Ne kesukok pish kenetuwohto kutohketeaonk, kah mohtompanáeu pish kenekitteáuun k8skannem: qut kepenumoonk pish numwunkquae ut unkquanu[mo]e kesukodtut mat anno[ó]sue unkquanumwi[t].
17.12 Missi wut[o]nkapunnaongan8 monacheg missinninnuog, ogque wadtauatonkqussuog kehtah, 8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah wutohtimoinne munnumuhkeonk onatuh manumuhkem8uk menuhkee nippeash.
17.13 Wutohtimoinash pish munumuhkem8ash, onatuh manumuhkem8ut monatash nippeash: qut God pish nah wutaushkomuh, kah nag pish nóadtit spuhh8waog, kah pish wunnaumatuhkauóog onatuh ut wuss[a]dtreamunne wadchuut ut anaquabit waban, kah onatuhyeu8 tatuppequashunk ut anaquabit pemsquoh.
17.14 Kah kusseh, wunnonk88k wuttamehpunáonk kah asquam mamohtompan8gkup, matta ohtan8, né wutchippiyeum8 neg waskhikqueagig, kah wuttittanohtôadtuongan8 neg mag8kqunukqueagig.
18.1 MIssi wutonkapunnaongan8 ne ohke wunnuppawhunne onkauuhtohhup, ne ogkomut Ethiopiáe sepuut.
18.2 Neg ann8noncheg ann8naénuh en ketahhanniyeu, ut misa[ssi]que kuht8nogquash ut wosketupam: n8waog, monchek kenupshae ann8nutcheg en naswae kah pissagkinnumwe wutohimoneat, en uhqueneunkque missinninnúut wutch wadj kutchissik yeu pajeh,; kuhkohhamwe kah tahtashkuhkôsue wutohtimoineat, noh wutohke sepu[á]sh matchehteauunash.
18.3 Wame kenaau wadohkeógish muttaohket, kah wadohkitcheg ohkeit, naum8k, tahshinuk muttôag ut wadchutu, puhpequohtunk monopupeg, n8tok.
18.4 Newutche ne nuttukqunah Jehovah, nutanwôhsin, kah nunnatwontam ut n[ú]tayeuonganit, onatuh pohkôntag wunnepogquehtu, kah onatuh matokqse neechippog k[ô]soppittag kepenum8onk.
18.5 Newutche asquam kakepenumómukup[,] wunn[e]ht8nunk pakodcheyeu88k, kah seane wenom kesan8htag tanohketeaonganit, pish wunnaneeswe tummussumunash wuttuhqunesash nashpe mukk8kussauwae h8ksash, kah amaunumunash, kah kouwehthamunash wuttuhqunash.
18.6 Nish pish moae nukkodtumunash wutche wadchue puppinshasog, kah ohkee puppinashimwut, kah puppinshasog pish wussequannussinuneau, kah wame ohkee puppinashimwog pish uppopónamineau.
18.7 Ne ahquompak mag8onk pish paudtauun Jehovah ayeuteaunit, wutch nasw[á]yeue kah pissagkinnumwe missinninnuut, wutch unkqueneúnkqué missinninnúog wutch waj kûtchissik yeu pajeh, kuhkohhum8e wutohtimoin kah tahtashkuhkôsue ut musseetut, noh wutohke sepúash máchtteómuk, wehque wutayeuonganit Jehovah áyeuhteaunit, wadchuut Zion.
19.1 OOWeanun Egypt, kusseh, Lord naiyeumuk kenupshae matokqs, kah pish peyaum8 Egypt, kah Egyptie nuuneukontúnkanog pish ontappúog ut anaquabit, kah wuttah Egypt pish mohtupohteau ut nôeu.
19.2 Kah Egyptiansog nummekonitteh Egyptiansog, kah nag nishnoh pasuk pish ayeuuhkonau wematoh; kah nishnoh pasuk ayeuuhkonittue weetatteamungoh, otan ayeuuhkonnittue otan, kah ass8tamóonk ayeuuhkonittue ass8tamóonk.
19.3 Kah wunnashauonguh Egypt pish sauunumwoh ut nashauwe, kah pish nuppaguan ukkogkáhquttuongan8, kah nag pish natinnewhaog enineuhkontungoh, & mamontomoh kah pauwaoh, kah kôsukquomoh.
19.4 Kah nukkuppoh Egyptiansog en wunnutcheganit unkapinohteae sontimoh, kah chenauausu ketass8t pish nah wunnanawunuh, n8wau Lord, Jehvoah ayeuhteaunit.
19.5 Kah nippe pish mahtsheau wutch ketahhanit, kah seip pish mahchim8 kah nunohteau.
19.6 Kah pish quinnuppechu[i]numwog seip en nôadtut, kah pummeneutonkane sepuash pish mohchiyeuash kah nunohtaash: wekinashquash, kah uppeanashkonog pish upp8taash.
19.7 Wussukhum8e wekinashquash ut kishke sepuwussit, ut kutt8n8out sepuwussash, kah nishnoh teag ohteuhkon ut kishke sepuwussit pish uhp8taash, kah t8hanash, kah matta wonk ohtan8ash.
19.8 Káh wonk n8tamogquaenuog pish mauog, kah neg wame omácheg sepuwussehtu pish mauog, kah nag sepagkenoncheg quomphunkoh ut nippekontu pish mahchimóog.
19.9 Kah wonk neg anakausitcheg ut wunne hashabput, kah neg quompho[n]kônehteácheg, pish wohwohkukquianumóog,
19.10 Kah nag pish pohquetahhamauóog uppogkodtantam8ongan8oash, wame neg ayigeg pahsohthegash kah nuppesash wutche nomohsog.
19.11 Wunnamuhkut Zoane sontimóog as8tuog, kogahquttuonk 8waantamwe Pharo kogagqutteam8moh, puppinashimweyeu8: toh woh kuttin unnomw8 Pharoh, nen wunnau[m]onuh waantog, wunnaumonuh kehchiyeue ket[à]ss8tamwog?
19.12 Uttoh nag wutapinneau? uttiyeug waantamwog, kah nag yeuyeu unnukqush, kah wahteauhettich uttoh Jehovah ayeuhteaanit en pogkodtantog ut Egypt.
19.13 Zoane sontimóog as8tuog, Nophe sontimóog neg as8kekomóog, nag wonk panne[n]osheaog Egyptiansog, neg k[ô]namunoncheh ut wuchipán8ongan8out.
19.14 Jehovah kenukunau wonke nashauonguh ut nôe, kah panneseaheáog Egyptiansoh nishnoh pasuk wutanakausuonganit, onatuh kogkeussippamwenin kehkepshont ut ummenadtam8onganit.
19.15 Kah matta pish na anakausuonganinno wutch Egipt, ne muhpuhkuk asuh wussukqun, wuttuhkq asuh rush woh wutussen.
19.16 Ne kesukok Egypt pish ogqueneunkqussu mittamwossissut, kah pish wabesu, kah nag pish wabesuog newutch wuttattauwunnumóonk wunnutcheg Jehovah, ayeuteaanit, neh ogkomáe tattauwunnumauumpoh.
19.17 Kah Judae ohke pish ukquohquaquênauwanum8onganin en Egypt, nishnoh pasuk ne weogqutuk noh pish wabesu, wutche ukken8n8waonk Jehovah ayeuteaunit neh ayeuuhkonittue pakodtantog,
19.18 Ne kesukok napanna tahshinash keitotanash, ut ohkit Egypt, unnont8waog Canaane unnont8w[à]onk, kah chadchekeimau Jehovah ayeuhteaanit, pasuk pish hennau, pagwanue keitotan.
19.19 Ne kesukok na pish Altareu8 en Jehovahut ut nôeu Egypte ohkeit, kah pogkomuhquonk sussippôeu en Lord$ut.
19.20 Kah ne pish kuhkinneasuonganu8, kah wauwaonganu8 en Jehovah ayeute[à]anit ut ohkeit Egypt, newutche neg pish mauunitteauaog Jehovah wutche woskhuwacheg, kah noh pish ann8nau wadchanuwaenu[h], kah missugken, kah noh pish uppohquohwhunoh.
19.21 Kah Jehovah pish waheau ut Egypt, kah Egyptiansog pish wahheaog Jehovah ne kesukok, kah pish sephausuog, kah mag8og, nux pish nag quoshauwaog quoshauwaonk en Jehovahut, kah pish wutusseneau.
19.22 Kah Jehovah pish togkodtam Egypt, pish wuttogkodtamun, kah wunnetskehteauun: kah nag pish qushkeog en Jehovahut, kah noh pish nupweshanau, kah pish wunnetskeheuh.
19.23 Ne kesukok na pish wunne may wutch Egypt en Assyria, kah wut-Assyrian pish petutteau Egypt, kah wut-Egy[g]tian en Assyria, kah Egyptiansog pish wuttinneumuhkauóog Assyriansoh.
19.24 Ne kesukok, Israel noh pish nash8it weeche Egypt, kah weeche Assyria, wunanitteaonk ut nashaue ohkeit.
19.25 Jehovah ayeuteaunit neh pish wunánumuh, n8wadt, Wunnánumunaj Egypt nummissinninneumog, kah Assyria nunnutchegane anakausuonk, kah Israel nutohtóonk.
20.1 NE kôdtum8k Tartan paont Ashdod (Sargon Assyriae ketass8t ann8nont) kah mátomppagwuhkontog Ashdod, kah sohkog.
20.2 Kah ne na[n] ahquompi Jehovah ket8kau Isaiahoh wunnaumonuh Amoz, n8wau, Monchish ompanish man8tionak wutch kusseganit, kah kodokkussináish, kah ne wutussenáh, pòsqushau, kah mamóhchishkussitteau.
20.3 Kah Jehovah n8wop, neane nuttinneum Isaiah posqushadt, kah mamóhchishkussitteadt nishwe kodtumwae wutche kuhkinneasuonk kah monchanatam8onk ut Egypt, kah ut Ethiopia.
20.4 Ne pish wuttinne Assyriae ketass8t missinóhko[uh] Egyptiansoh kah Ethiopiansoh, wuskênúh kah kutchisoh, poskissue kah mamohchishkussittaeu, kah poskitteáeu wutakodchinat Egypt.
20.5 Kah nag pish wabesuonóuh kah akodchuwóunóuh Ethiopia, annóonáhetticheh, kah Egypt wussohsum8ongan8uh.
20.6 Kah neg wadohkitcheg yeu ohkeit pish n8waog ne kesukok, kusseh, ne n$nih annoósuontamog uttoh asph8aogkup wutch nontummóadtuonk, pohquohwhunnittinneat wutch Assyriae ketass8t: kah uttoh woh kuttin pohquohhamunan?
21.1 OWeanan ketahhanue touohkomuk: onatuh sowanishinne pemsquoh paumshadt, ne ne 8m88 touohkomuk, wutch u[n]kqunneunkquotte ohkeit.
21.2 Uhqunneunkquotte unnaumanissuonk n8wahteauwahit: wunass8muwaénin wanass8muwae unnéhhuau, kah matchehuwaénin matchehuau, kuhkuhquish, woi Elam: weenussumwehtok, woi Media; wame ummishanóm8ongan8 n8wohkukquoshitteauun.
21.3 Newaj nusséganit numwohteau onkquomom8onk, onkquomom8ongsh nuttohqunuk, onatuh wutonkquomom8onk mittumwussis neechadt, nunnauwáeep n8tamon, kah nutchepshomp naumon.
21.4 Nuttah nunnuksheau, wabesuonk n8w[a]buwunuk: n8wekontam8e nuhkon8m, ukquinnuppinnumun en 8wabesuontamunut.
21.5 Quashauwehtam8k table, askuhwekontam8k askuhwete[à]e$komukqut, meetsek kah wuttattam8k: omohkek sontim[ó]og, sussequnnumok ogqunneg.
21.6 Newutche yeu nuttugqunah Lord, monchish askuhwheteaénin wunnash, wahteauwahuwaj uttoh [án] nag*.
21.7 Kah naum chariot, kah neesuog horsesoh nay8mukqutcheg, assese chariot, kah kamelse chariot; kah menuhke ahchuwussittámup.
21.8 Kah mishont8wop, qunnónou: nussontimom nunnagwutteae neepoh ut askuhwheteáe komukqut: kesukodtáe, kah askuhwhekonat n8nashit wowompannu.
21.9 Kah kusseh, yeu ut peyom8 wosketompàe chariot, nes8og horsesoh nay8mukqutcheg, kah namp8ham kah n8wau, Babylon penushau, penushau, kah wame ummanitt8mue nunnukontunkanouh, uppohquttahwhoh en ohkeit.
21.10 Woi nuppogham8onk, kah ahhuttanuppoghamuk weatchiminneash, ne n8tamauogkup Lord ayeuteaanit, um$Manitt8moh Israel, k8wahteauwáhununeau.
21.11 OOweanun Dumah: n8wehkomuk wutch Seir, askuhwheteaènin toh utt8che tipukod? askuhwheteaénin toh utt8che tipukod?
21.12 Askuhwheteaénin n8wau, mohtompan peyaum8, kah wonk nuhkon: kod nat8tomwehteáog, nat8tomwehteagk: qushkek, peyunk.
21.13 OOweanun Arabia. Ut Arabiae touohkomukqut ne pish kukkouéneau, woi Dedanimáe chippan8e pomushaog.
21.14 Wadohkitcheg Tema paudtauáog nippe noh kuhkutt8nutche, koshkomme assamáog petukqunneg neh wusseemunutcheh.
21.15 Newutche nag wussemóog wutch tohkodteganehtu, wutch kodtunnum8e togkodteg[a]nit, wutch wonkinnónat ohtomp, wutch unkqunneungane mattompagwut.
21.16 Newutche yeu nuttugqunat Jehovah, ash nánukqut kodtumun8gkup, neaunag ne ukkodtum8m noh ann8nit, neit wame wussohsumóonk K[e]dar pish penusheau.
21.17 Kah neg ashqushoncheg ne adtass8hettit pepummuwaenuog, ummissugkeneumoh wunnaumonuh Kedar, pish ogqusheáog, newutche Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel wussin.
22.1 OOWeanun monoma[u]sue 8nouhkoi, tohkutushpunam mamusse kuhquhqueog woskeche kommukquehtu.
22.2 K[é]n nomwabetunkquean wogkouongash, menumuhquáeu keitotan, wekontamwae otan, nushae k8wosketompomog, matta nushóog nashpe togkodteg, asuh matta nupp8[o]g ut ayeuwuttinneat.
22.3 Wame nanawunnuácheg moáeu wussem8og, k[è]nepunukquog pepummuwaénúh, wame neg námteauunumukeg nehnesippissuog, neg nôadtit wadt8k[au]utcheg.
22.4 Newaj n8wi, p8nampameh, pish n8weesogkohpûs, ahchue taphehkon, wutche matcheheaongan8 wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog.
22.5 Newutche ne wuttamehpunáe kesukod, kah tahtashkuhkôadtin, kah unkque wuttaméhpunon nashpe Lord Jehovah ayeuteaunit, ut monomo[n]sue 8nouhkóiyeuut, n8kuhkonat wonkôn8sinash, kah mauongash nogque wadchuuhk[ó]ntu.
22.6 Kah Elam kenunnum petan, nashpe wosketompae chariotsash, kah horsesoh nayeumukqutcheg, kah Kir poshkinumun ogqunneg.
22.7 Kah pish n$nih, k8ne 8nouuhkóiyeumash pish nanumwohteau ch[e]riotsash, kah horsesoh nayeumukqutcheg, pish sepunnego[n]éhteaog en nogque squontam[é]htu.
22.8 Kah miskom upputtaguhwheg Judah, kah ne kesukok, kummónunneamup ukkenauwameonk touohkomukque komukqut.
22.9 Kah wonk kenaumumw8 pohquiyeue ukkeitotan David, nish monatash, kah kummohmóunumumw8 w8muhkôáge nippesse nippeash.
22.10 Kah kutogketamumw8 Jerusalem wetuomash, kah ken8kahteamw8 wetuomash menehketeauunat ummánsk.
22.11 Kah wonk kutayimumw8 pasahtheg ut nashaue neese ummanskut, wutche nukkone nuppisse nuppe: qut matta kummonunnéan[ô]mw8 noh ne kezteunk, kah matta k8t8anumw8 noh kahkenauwehteunkup noadt.
22.12 Kah ne kesukok Lord Jehovah ayeuhteaunit k8wehkomukqun en mauunat, kah neuantamunat, kah mupukkontupónat, kah puttukquobpissineat man8tionak.
22.13 Kah kusseh weekontamóonk, kah muskouantamoonk, nushaonk oxenóg, kah shepsog, meechuonk weyaus, kah wuttattamoonk wine meetsitteuh kah wuttattamutt[u]h, newutche saup pish kenupmun.
22.14 Kah wahteauwahuwonáh ut nehtauogkut, nashpe Jehovah ayeute[a]anit, wunnamuhkut yeu matcheseonk matta pish pahketeauun ut kuhhogkaóut, nô pajeh kenuppunnaôont, n8wau Lord Jehovah ayeuhteaunit.
22.15 Yeu wussin Lord Jehovah ayuhteaunit, monchish, aush noh nompak8 wadchanuk, noh Shebna, noh piohquttuk wetu, n8wash.
22.16 Teagus kutahto yeu$ut? kah teaguas kutahto na$ut? waj 8neeteáan weenohke yeu$ut: noh weenohkéhkauont wuhhogkuh qunuhqu: kah waneúhquttamauont wuhhogkuh wetu ut qussukquanit?
22.17 Kusseh Jehovah pish kummishe missinóhkônittue monchanuk, kah pish wunnamuhkut kupputtaguhhuk.
22.18 Noh pish wunnamuhkut chekee k8wahwaapuhkunk onatuh pompasukonganit, en mishékishku wutohtimóneat, na pish kuttit nuppuneau: kah na pish kuttit sohsumoe chariotsash akodjteauunat kussontimom wek.
22.19 Kah push kutáma8koush wutch kutayeuonganit, kah wutch k8niyeuonganit pish ken8kinuk.
22.20 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok, pish n8wehkom nuttinneum Eliakim wunnaumonuh Hilkiah.
22.21 Kah pish nuthogqueh kuppetashqusháonk, kah nummenuhkeh wutch kupputtukquobissu, kah nupponam kena[n]ánuwaonk ut wunnutcheganit, kah noh pish 8sh8oh wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, & en wekit Judah.
22.22 Kah David weke pohquoshadtikunk, nukquenohtauun wuttugkit: ne pish wuttin wôshinnumun, kah matta pish howan kupham8un, kah noh pish ukkuphamun, kah matta pish howan uppohqu[à]num8un.
22.23 Kah nukkishpun onatuh kenontukqueg ut wunnamuhkutée ayeuonganit, kah noh pish sohsumóe appuonk 8shoh wekit.
22.24 Kah nag pish 8waôhshanóuh wame 8shoh week8e sohsumóonk, wutontseon, kah wutontsétuonk, wame papeasike wishquash wutch wuttattamóe wishquadt, pajeh wame kehchéshquadt.
22.25 Ne kesukok, n8wau Jehovah ayeuhteaunit, kenontukquontunk ne manuhkehteamuk ut wunnamuhkutée ayeuonganit, pish ontahtauun, kah pish tummes[s]umun, kah penusheau; kah weanun ne na quenohtagkup ish tummussumun, newutche Jehovah ukkutt8kontámun.
23.1 OOWeanun Tyre. OOn8k kenaau Tarshishe kuht8nogquog, newutche mahchim8, newaj matta wetuwomun8g, wanne petutteau[n]: wutch Chittimme ohkeit nag wahteauwahuoneau.
23.2 Chequnappek wadohkeógish munóhhanéhtu, ken, Zidone anaqushaenuog neg quoshkodteacheg keitoh, ken[a]mwamechumuhkonukquog.
23.3 Kah nashpe mishe nippeash, wusk[a]nnem Sihor, sepue kepenumóonk ne wutteashegen8m, kah noh wutohtim[o]inne ahhut kodtauwompa[simu]k.
23.4 Akodchish, woi Zidon, newutche keitoh ket8hkau, ummenuhkesuonk keitoh, n8wau, matta nukkodta[u]wekhe[ó]h, asuh nunneechóh, asuh matta n8nadchan8 wuskenuog, asuh matta n8wadchan8 nunksquaog.
23.5 Onatuh neantunkquok papaume Egypt, ne pish wuttin unkque onkquomominneau n8tamwahettit papaume Tyre.
23.6 Qushkodteagk Tarshish 8n8k kenaau wadohkeógish munohhanit.
23.7 Sun yeu k8wekontamwe otaneau, na wunnukkoneayeu8onk wutch n8adt? nehenwonche wussetash pish noadtit uss8unuk pen8wohteauneat.
23.8 Howan yeu nemunuk kogahquttaonk ayeuuhkonittue Tyre, chetuhquabinnuwae keitotan, wutanaqushaenúmoh sontimaúooh, ukkodtauwompasuéneumoh neg quttiánumukqussuog ut ohkeit?
23.9 Jehovah ayeuteaunit uppogkodtantamun nishketeauunat wame pehtuánumwe sohsumóonk, kah jishónumwaheonaóont wame quohtianumukqussitcheg ohkeit.
23.10 Papannupohkash kutohke onatuh sepuut, woi wuttaunoh Tarshish: matta na wonk menuhkesuonganunn8.
23.11 Summ[a]gunum wunnutcheg woskeche kehtahhanit, nunnukshadto ass8tam8ongash, Jehovah ann8team8 ayeuuhkonittue anaqusháe otan, paguatauunat ummenehtekomukquash.
23.12 Kah n8wau, neketeashe wekontamun, woi ken mukk8kinae penomp, wuttaunoh Zidon, omkish qushkodteash en Chittim, na$ut wonk matt apish wonk k8tanwôsinn8onganéin.
23.13 Kusseh, wutohkeeu Caldeansog yeug missinninnuog matta appupaneg noh pajeh Assyriansog quenohtae ponamwog wutche nag wadohkitcheg touohkomuk: nag wunohtóog ukqunuhque kommuk88ash, nag tahshinnumwog ummishe kommuk88ash, kah uppaguatauun.
23.14 OOn8k kenaau Tarshishe kuht8[n]ogquog, newutche kummenuhkesuognan8 mohtupa[sh]in.
23.15 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok, Tyre pish wanantamun nesausuk tahshinchage kodtumwae, neaunak ukkesukodtumash pasuk ketass8t, mahtshunk nesausuk tahshinchage kodtum8, Tyre pish ogk8humau kogkeeusqua[u]t.
23.16 Nemunush harp papaumwushash otanat, ken kogkeeusquau wananumunumuk, wunont8ash, m8cheke, unn8humush onk woh kummehquanumit.
23.17 Kah pish n$nih, mahtshunk nesausuk tahshinchage kodtumm8, Jehovah pish nátauwahto Tyre, kah noh pish quinnuppu ponampóadtinneat, kah pish nanwun8dsquáôsu en wame ass8tam8onganehtu muttaohket, ut woskeche ohkeit.
23.18 Kah nish kodtauwompasitcheh, kah ne ponampauut pish wunnetupanatamweyeu8 Jehovahut: ne matta pish nompak8unehtaun asuh wadchanum8un, newutche ukkodtauwompasuonk pish wutche nag apitcheg anaquabit Jehovah, tapupwunneat, kah sephogk8unon.
24.1 KUsseh, Jehovah wussequnnumun ohke kah ummohtupáshitteauun, kah 8nim[usk]inumun, kah seahwau neh ne wadohkinitcheh.
24.2 Kah pish n$nih, ne anihettit missinninnuog, ne wuttinninneau sephausuaenuog, nea[in]it wuttinneumin, ne wuttinniin wussontimomun, neaniit nunksquoh, ne wuttinniin wussonksquomoh, neaniit adtôadt ne wuttinniin noh maguk, neaniit nagohkouaenin ne wuttinniin noh nogo[h]kouónit, ne aniit noh neemunuk onts[a]uohteaonk ne wuttinniin noh maguk ontsouohteaonk.
24.3 Ohke pish papuhquanne sequnnumun kah papuhquanne matcheteauun, newutche Jehovah wussin yeu kutt8onk.
24.4 Ohke maum8, kah mohtsheau, muttaok mahchum8, kah mahchum8, pahtuánumwee[n]unkqussitcheg ohkeit mahchum8og.
24.5 Kah wonk ohke nishketeauun ut agwe neg wadohkitcheg, newutche panneussehtauáog naumatuonguh, ôs8wunnumwog kuhk8waonk, pohquenumwog m[à]chemohtag wunn8waonk.
24.6 Newaj matánittuonk paguodtunk ohke, kah neg na apitcheg touwiyeuog, newaj wadohkitcheg ohkeit chikohsuog, kah ogguhsuog sequhkussuog.
24.7 Wuske wine mau, weenomwussippog mahchum8, wame pôanittamwutteahoncheg mishanom8og.
24.8 Tabretse wunont8waonk ahquohteau, 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 neg wekontogig wohkukquoshin, harpe wekontamóonk ahquohteau.
24.9 Nag matta pish unn8hamae wuttattamwog wine, onkuppe pish 8wesogkonhúkquneau neg wadtattogig.
24.10 Nanwohteae otan pokshadtauun, nish noh wetu kuppuhhôsu, onk woh mo howae wosketomp petutteóou.
24.11 Wuttohposuog wine ut maikontu, wame wekontamóonk pohkenashin, 8wekontamóonk ohke mohtsheau.
24.12 Ut otanat touushin nukkodtumun, kah ussquont togkodtamun paguanuonk.
24.13 Yeu n$nagk ut noeu ohkeit, ut kenugke missinninnútu, na pish neaneyeu8 nenemonteamuk oliveuhtug, kah mukkuposquae weenominneash mohtouwunneamuk.
24.14 Nag pish mishont8waog, pish unn8homa[o]g newutche ukquttianumukqussuonk Jehovah, nag pish mishont8waog wutch kehtahhannit.
24.15 Newutche sohsum8wón8k Jehovah ut n8taut, 8wesuonk Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel ut ketahhanne munnahanash.
24.16 Wutch aongkauohkomuk n8tamumun ket8homàongash, sohsum8ón8k sampweusseaen, qut nussip, nutônauwussuonk, nutônauwussuonk, missi nutonkapunnaonk: wunass8muwaenuog wunass8muwaog, nux wunass8muwaenuog ahche wunass8muwaog.
24.17 Wabesuonk, kah pahsahtheg, kah ahpeh kenuhkuhkongquog, woi w[a]dohkeógish ohkeit.
24.18 Kah pish n$nih, noh waseemwuhteog wadtauatonkqussue wabesuonk, pish petshau psahtheganit, kah noh sohhog wutch noeu psahtheganit, pish puttahwhôu: newutche kenogkanégash wutch waabe wôhshwohtaash, kah ohkee quenohtagish nunnukshaash.
24.19 Ohke papuhquanne poksheau, ohke papaquanne naswáshin, ohke m8cheke ontohteau.
24.20 Ohke pish kekepsheau onatuh kogkeissippamwén, kah pish ogque ontaht[à]uun wetuómut, kah uppanneusseonk pish wuttuhkékhúkqun, kah pish penusheau, kah matta wonk omohkemun8[-]
24.21 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok, Jehovah pish sasamatahwhau wutayeuwehtóm8uh quanunkqussitcheg, neg quanukquapicheg, kah ohkee ketass8tamwog, wosketohke.
24.22 Kah nag pish miyaéog onatuh kopshagkinatcheg moéhettit ut psahtheganit, kah pish kuppuhwhóog ut kuppishshagkinnittuonganit, kah mahtshik monatash kesukquash pish natauwaheóop.
24.23 Neit nahnepauhshadt pish mishakodcheheau, kah nepâuz akodchu, Jehovah ayeuteaunit tahs8tam8it ut Zion kah ut Jerusalem, kah ut anaquabenit ukkehchiyeumoh, sohsumóe.
25.1 WOi Jehovah, ken num-Manitt8m, kummishhesh, n8woweenodtum k8wesuonk, newutche kummonchanatamwe ussem, kenukkone kogohk8waongash pabuhtanumukqussuonk, kah wunnamuhkutéyeuuk.
25.2 Newutche kenumwonkwâhteoh keitotan, k8weepótóhteam pummeneutaúsue otan: wanne kutotanáhtu ut papeáhetti penuwohteaog, matta pish wonk ayim8un.
25.3 Newaj pish menuhkesue missinninnuog sohsum8ónukquean, unkqueneunkque wutohtimonne keitotan pish k8wabesuonuk.
25.4 Newutche ken ummenuhkesuonk machéku, ummenuhkesuonk quenauhikquit, ut ukquehquenauánumwinneat, ushpuhh8waonk wuch mishe tahshinit, onkauohteau wutche kussitteau, upp8tómuwaonk uhqunneunkqussitcheg moshtashuhkontamwéhhettiche pummeneutunk.
25.5 Pish kuppeéhteoh 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 penuwohteaog, onatuh kussittea[u] ut nunnobohteaoúut, kussitteau nashpe mahtohqse onkauohteau: 8tukqunn8 uhqunneunkqussitcheg pish n8kinnumun.
25.6 Kah yeuut wadchuut Jehovah ayeuteaunit pish weesée mishadtupweheau wame missinninnúh, sekqskausháe wine mishadtup8onk, wâónogqutcheg numwohteau ween sekqskaushae wine, wunnehteausu.
25.7 Kah yeuut wadchuut, pish paguanau woskechee onkwheg, onkwhut wame missinninnúog, kah puttogwheg sepáginaúsik wame wutohtim[ô]neat.
25.8 Pish sohkôsue misheáskóu nupp8onk, kah Lord Jehovah pish jishkham wussippwegwash wutch wame muskesukqut, kah auskomaonk ummissinninnúmoh pish wutamaunumun wutch ohkeit: newutche Jehovah ukkutt8kontamun.
25.9 Kah pish unn8won ne kesukok, kusseh, yeuoh kum-Manitt8mun, nuppáhtsuwóunóun, kah noh pish k8wadchanukqun, yeuoh Jehovah, nuppáhtsuwóunnóun, n8wekontamumun, kah nummuskouantamumun ut 8wadchnuonganit.
25.10 Newutche yeu$ut wadchuut wunnutcheg, Jehovah pish anwohshin, kah Moab pish tahtashkuhkauaû ut wutagwiyeumut, onatuh sekuppogheg tahtashkuhkomuk wutche anadtuppúhkout.
25.11 Kah pish sepagunum wunnutchegash ut wunnashom8wóut, onatuh noh pâmôs8wit sepagunuk wunnutcheash en pamôs8wénat, kah tiahquonkheau pehtuánum8m8uh moeu, nashwunnutchegane sequttahham8ongash.
25.12 Kah negonohtog kuppummeneutausue umma[n]shk pish wunn8kinnumun, tiuhquonkshin, ohkeit uppaudtauun, puppissiyeuut.
26.1 NE kesukok, yeu unn8homaonk pish unn8hamon ut ohkeit Judah, nutohtomu menuhki keitotan, God pish kuhquttum wadchanittuonk wutche pummeneutungash kah ummaushkàsh.
26.2 W[ô]hshinum8k ushquontamash, onk woh sampweusseae wutohtimóin, noh nanawehteunk wanamuhkutéye[u]uk uppetukon.
26.3 Ken pish kenanaweh ut pannuppee wunohteaonganit, noh ompatussum8wónukquean wuttah, newutche kuppabahtanumuk
26.4 Pabahtanumok Jehovah micheme, newutche ut Lord Jehovahut noh michemohtáe menuhkesuonk
26.5 Newutche n8kinau neh quanunkquiinitcheh, quanunkquok otan, wutti[ú]hquonkqutteauun, wuttiuhquonkqutteauun pajeh ohkeit, uppuppissiyeúhkon.
26.6 Musset pish wuttashkuhkomun, matcheku wusseet, wutôntañehtuongash quenahukquit.
26.7 Ummay sampweusseaen ne samp8hássuonk: ken anue samp8hassean, kukqutompagh8toh ummay sampweusseaen.
26.8 Nux ut k8sittum8e mayut, woi Jehovah, kuppahtsuwóunumun: ukkodtantam8onk nukketeahogkôunun ut k8wesuonganit, kah kummequanumitteanat.
26.9 Nashpe nukketeahogkou kukkodtanumush nuhkonáeu, nux nashpe nunnashaonk nuttinnómiyeumut, nompoáe kenatinneáwhush, newutche k8sittum8ongash ohtag ohkeit, wadohkitcheg muttaohkit pish net[u]htauog sampweusseonk.
26.10 Nahtinit kitteamonteanittuonk matchetóog, matta pish netuhtóou sampweusseonk, ut sampweusseae ohkeit pish panne unnehuau, kah matta pish naum8 ukquehtianumáonk Jehovah.
26.11 Jehovah kenutcheg tahshinnuman, nag matta pish naum8og: qut pish wunnaumuneau: kah pish akodchuog wutche wutishkau[é]naongan8 kummissinninnumoh, nux wunn8tom8 kummatwomog pish nah ummahchukkiswôh.
26.12 Jehovah, pish kukkuhquttumaiimun wunohteaonk, newutche ken wonk kuttinanakausuwánshimun wame nutanakausuwonganonash.
26.13 Woi Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, onkatogig sontimòog chabissitcheg onk ken nanawunukqunnónuppanneg, qut nashpe ken webe nummishamumun k8wesuonk.
26.14 Nag nupp8k, matta pish pomantam8og: nag wohkukquossinwog, matta pish omohkeog, newaj natauwáhheadt, kah kuppaguanóog, kah k8wa[n]teauwahto wame mehquanumaongan8.
26.15 Nano kummishteóh wutohtimoin, woi Jehovah, nano kumishteóh wutohtimóin, kussohsumwahit: noadtit kuttinontahtauun, en wame ongkouohkomukqut.
26.16 Jehovah, wadtamehpunáhettit, kenatauwahikquog, sokanumwog peantamóonk, kussasamatahh8waonk nohkugkonkqhettit.
26.17 Onatuh póseu mittamwossis pas8sukog adt woh neechadt, onkquommamwit, kah môe onkquommamwit, ne nuttinniinnean ut anaquabean, woi Jehovah.
26.18 Nuppôosimun, nutonkquomomumun, nunneechámun onatuh wuttin, matta nutussûmun pohquawhunnittuonk ut ohkeit, asuh matta wadohkitcheg muttaohkit penusha8og.
26.19 Kenupp8mog pish pomantamwog, nashpe nunnupp8e muhhog nag pish omohkeog: t8kek kah ket8hamunk kenaau wadohkeógish p[ù]ppissiyeuut: newutche keneechippogkum tatuppeyeu8 herbse neechippogkut, kah ohke pish sohwóhteau nupp8oh.
26.20 Peyunk nummissinninnúmog, petutteash ut kutchambersumut, kah y[â]nitteanumush quinnuppu, puttogquish onatuh ogguhse, noh pajeh paumushaum8uk musquanittuonk
26.21 Newutche kusseh, Jehovah wutch sohham wutáyeuonganit sasamatahwhonat wadohkitcheg ohkeit wutch ummatcheseongan8, ohke wonk pish wóhshwem8 8sqheonk, kah matta pish wonk onkwhóou nohtauwutcheh.
27.1 NE kesukok Jehovah nashpe kehkechiyeue & missi & menuhki wutogkodteg pish sasamatahwhau Leviathanoh pannupshae ask8k, nux Leviathan noh pepemsque ask8k kah pish nushau dragonoh ut kehtahhanit.
27.2 Ne kesukok ket8hamok, musqui wine weenominneohteuk.
27.3 Nen Jehovah nanawehteauun, nutogqutchippadtauun nishnoh utt8che: ishkont howan ummatchteauun, nunnanawehteauun nukkonaeu, kah kesukodaeu.
27.4 Mishe musquantam8onk matta nutapehtunk8un: howan woh ayeuuhkonittue ponumunkque kôussoh kah hasinnekôussoh? neg woh nuppannupwushonunk, woh nummoáeu chikoswoog.
27.5 Asuh menuhkinitch nummenuhkesuonk, onk woh n8nohkonuk, kah noh pish n8nohkonuk.
27.6 Neg ontsécheg wutch Jakobut pish 8wadchabukeheuh: Israel pish péshauau, kah wunéht8nuhquamú8, kah pish numwohtou woskeche muttaohkit nashpe meechummuonk.
27.7 Sun noh togkomau, neane togkomont neg togkomoncheg? sun nushau, neaunag nushaongan8 neh náshoncheh?
27.8 Quttuhwhosue sontipohshunk, neit kukkeket8hkonau, kuppahwau ummishetashineum ne kesukok wadchepwashik
27.9 Newutche yeu nashpe, ummatcheseonk Jakob pish pahketeaun8, kah yeu wame ne meechummuonk amaunumunat ummatcheseonk: wame altare qussukquanash agqueteunk chalke qussukquanash, nish soquttahhamukish, kogkompagish kah nunneukontunkanog matta pish nepadta[n]8ash.
