27.10 Qut onch pummeneutausue keitotan pish touwashin, kah ayeuonk nukkodtumun, kah nukkodtumun netatuppe touohkomukqut, na pish wuttut natupwun calf, na pish wussepsinin, kah matcheteau nish wuttuhqunash.
27.11 Wuttuhqunash muss8pohtag pish pokshaash: mittamwossissog peyaog, kah chikohsoog, newutche nag matta wohtam8e missinninnuog, newaje ne kezheump matta pish ummonanumoh, kah noh nah kakenauwaheomp matta pish ukkitteamonteanumoh
27.12 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok Jehovah pish kummoncheahukon wutch sepue posséhteanit pajeh Egipte kussitchuwanit, kah pish kenu[h]aseu mukkinnitteamw8, woi kenaau wunnaumonuh Israel.
27.13 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok, mishe monopu[h]peg pish puhpequohtauun, kah nag pish peyaog, pakodche onkuppunacheg, ut ohkeit Assyria, kah pagkenitcheg ut ohkeit Egipt, kah pish wowussumaog Jehovah, ut wunneetupanatamwe wadchuut, ut Jerusalem.
28.1 MIssi wutonkapunaonk chetuhquabee pechuanumoonk, ukkogkeisippamwaeneumoh Ephraim, noh wussohsumoe wunnetuonk, ne pauuhshauae uppeshau, nish ohtagish 8nogk8e 8nauuhkoiyeue uppuhkuhqut neg sohkunkqutcheg wine.
28.2 Kusseh Jehovah ohto how[a] menuhkes[u] kah missugken noh, neaneyeu8g nashqutne mussegan, & pagwohte[á]e nashquttin, onatuh mishe nippeash tômogkok, pish uppenuhkon en ohkeit, nashpe wunnutcheg.
28.3 Petuanumwe chetuhqu[á]b, ukkogkeissippam8moh Ephraim pish tahtashkuhkauoog ut agwe musseetut.
28.4 Sohsumoe 8netuonk ne ohtag wunnogque 8nouhkoi uppuhkukqut, ne pish pôuhshauwae uppeshau, kah onatuh kenuppegane meechumuonk, ash achuwan8gkup, ne noh kahkinneog, nag*, ash pampohtag wunnutcheganit, mahchipwun
28.5 Ne kesukok Jehovah ayeuteaunit, noh wussohsumoe chetuhquabeyeu, kah 8neetue kenadtukquabpeyeu ashqushonitcheh ummissinninneumoh.
28.6 Kah nasháuanittoe 8sittum8onk noh apit wussittum8onganit, kah ummenuhkesuongan8 nag quoshkinukeg ayeuwuttuonk ut ushquontamut.
28.7 Qut nag wonk panneusseog nashpe wine kah nashpe onkuppe, matta appeog mâyut sephausuen kah quoshodtumwaen panneusseog nashpe unkuppe, nag misseashk8wonukquog wine: nag matta appeog mayut nashpe onkuppe, panneseae monomansuog, togkussittahsunwog wâsittumohettit.
28.8 Newutche wame tablesash numwohteau munnadtumoonk kah nishkeneunkquok, newaj wanne ayeuonk pahkan8.
28.9 Howane woh kohk8tomauont wahteauonk, howane woh kohk8tomauont wahteauonk, howane woh wahtamwaheont kuh[k]8tomwehteaonk? neg 8chininnahitcheg wutch sogkodtunkanit, kah pashkunaog wutch mohpanôganit[.]
28.10 Newutche kuhk8tomwehteaonk pish ahôsuhkaueyeu8 kuhk8tomwehteaonk, kuhk8tomwehteaonk ahôsuhkaueyeu8 kuhk8tomweheteaonk, kuhkuhheg ahósuhkaueyeu8 kuhkuhheg, kuhkuhheg ahos[ú]hkaueyeu8 kuhkuhheg, yeuut ogguhse, kah naut wonk ogguhse.
28.11 Newutche nashpe nahnogkiae mississitt8nash, kah pen8wont8waonk pish wuttinnont8wanumauon yeuh missinninnuh
28.12 Neh anoncheh, yeu anwohsinn8onk ne [á]dt anwosumoh neg sauunukeg, kah yeu ne taphettuonk, qut onch mat n8tam8og.
28.13 Qut wuttinnowaonk Jehovah appehtunkquog kuhk8tomwehteaonk ahôsuhkaueyeu8 kuhk8tomwehteaonk, kuhk8tomwehteaonk [a]hosuhkaueyeu8 kuhk8tomwehteaonk; kuhkuhheg ahôsuhkaueyeuo kuhkuhheg, kuhkuhheg ahôsuhkaueyeu8 kuhkuhheg, yeu ogguhse naut wonk ogguhse, onk woh moncheog kah woh ant8[h]shaog, kah pohksunwog, kah puttahwhoog, kah tohqunóog.
28.14 Newutche n8tam8k wuttinnowaonk Jehovah, pahtuanumweogish nanauwunogish missinninnuog neg apitcheg Jerusalem.
28.15 Newutche kussimw8, n8n8womun nupp8onk, kah n8n8womun chepiohkomuk, aneupae sasamatahwhuttuonk paumushaum8uk, matta pish nuppeyógk8unan: néwutche nutushpohhouwaonganéhteamun pann8waongash, kah agwe as8kekodteam8onganit nupputogquemun.
28.16 Newajeh yeu n8wadt Lord Jehovah, kusseh, nupponamun ut Sion wutche quenohtag, qussuk, qutchehteoe qussuk, mishoadtue nahshine qussuk, papane quenohtag, noh wanamptog matta kenupshau8.
28.17 Kah wonk wussittum8onk nupponamun kuhkuheganit, kah sampweusseonk qutompagh8teganit: kah mussegon pish chekham pann8wae ushpuhh8waongash, kah nippeash pish nehtippadt8 adtahtoe ayeuonk,
28.18 Kah k8n8waongan8 nupp8onk pish mo teagwunnehte[á]uun, kah n8n8waongan8 chepiohkomuk matta pish neepadtano: aneupae sasamatahwhuttuonk pannupwushaum8uk, neit pish kenashpe tashkuhkonteaneau.
28.19 Wutch aquompeyeue sohham8m8uk, pish kuttohqunukquneau; newutche mohmohtompanae pish paumusháum8, kesukodaeu kah nukonaeu, kah pish m8sqhettuwonganu8, webe wohtamunat unnehtunkquot.
28.20 Newutche appin tiohqui wosketomp matta woh wuttit sesekein, kah hogk8onk penompagod, matta woh uppapadtukqussun8un.
28.21 Newutche Jehovah pish omohku, ne asip ut wadchuut Perazim, pish musquantam ne asip ut Gibeone 8no[ú]hkoiye[ú]ut, onk woh wutussenat wutanakausuonk, penowe wutanakausuonk, onk woh kezteau wutusseonk, penowe wutusseonk.
28.22 Newutche ahque momonehtásuenuek ishkont kukkinnepsuongan8oash menehketeausuash; newutch nunn8tam wutch Lord Jehovah ayeuteaunit, mohchekonnaeonk kehtimau ut woskeche mamusse ohkeit.
28.23 Kuhkeitiek, kah n8tam8k n8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kuhkihtam8k, kah n8tam8k nukkutt8wonk.
28.24 Sun anaskhomwen anaskham nehteage ohteuhkonat? sun wohshinum kah pohquenum puhquohkomukquash ut wutohteakonit?
28.25 M8sitte[u]nk woskeche, sunnummatta seahham8 fitches[à]sh, kah seahhamm8 cummin kah ohkehteau wanegukish wheatash kah kuhquttumwe barly, kah rye ut wutayeaongan8out.
28.26 Newutche um-Manitt8moh ukkuhk8tomau nehtôe usseonk, kah ukkuhk8tomauuh.
28.27 Newutche fitchesash matta poggohhomwauhtugque poggohhamunash, asuh matta carte-wheel quinnuppenum8un woskeche cummin, qut fitchesash poggohhamunash nashpe anwohhou, kah cummin nashpe souobpunk.
28.28 Petukqunnegane weatchiminneash s8quttahhamunash, newutche matta kod nagwutteae uppogham8un, asuh matta pohquetahhamun nashpe uk-carte-wheelum, asuh matta sohquttahham8 nashpe nayeumukqutcheg horsesoh.
28.29 Yeu wonk 8m88 wutch Lord ayéuteaunit, noh monchanatamwe koguhtimut, kah waussinit.
29.1 MIssi wutonkapunaonk Ariel, A[a]iel, keitotan ne David ayeup k8tnehteau8k kodtum8, nehtauhettich sephausuongash.
29.2 Qut onch nukquehquenauánumweh Ariel, kah na pish nupp8anum8onk kah neuantam8onk, kah pish nuttatupontamun Ariel.
29.3 Kah pish ayeuuhkonittue k8wéenu tupuksinn8wonsh, kah k8weenussumwehtoush nashpe wadchu, kutayeuuhkonittue waápenumoush ummanshkash.
29.4 Pish ken8kinit, kah pish kukket8hkon wutch ohkeit, kah kukkutt8wongash tiuhquonkod wutch puppissiyeuut: kah k8wadtauatonkqussuonk pish tatuppeyeu8 noh apehtunkqut matche nashauonk wutch ohkeit: kah kukkutt8onk keemompeum8 wutch puppissiyeuut.
29.5 Nano, mataanukeg kuppen8wohteomogish pish ogqueneunkqussuog sohque puppissiyeuut, & kutunkqueneunkqusseume monacheg, pish tatupeyeu8og wussadteanumit, ne pamshunk, nux pish kenuppeyeu8, teanuk.
29.6 Jehovah ayeuteaunit pish kenatauwahik nashpé padtohquohhan, kah nashpe quequanash, kah mishont8waongash, nashpe nashquttin kah mishetahshin, kah n8n8nae mahchukkissuwae n8teau.
29.7 Kah mataanukish wutohtimoneash ayeuuhkontam8m8ukish Ariel, wame neg ayeuuhkononcheg, kah wutauwohteaongash, kah quehquenauanumwutcheg, pish tatuppeyeu8og nukkonae monománsue nukquom8onk
29.8 Pish tatuppeyeu8, kodtupwen ánukquonk, kah kusseh meetsu, qut t8hku, kah ukketeahogkôunoh mahtussuoh, asuh onatuh kûhkuht8n8wenin ánukquonk kah kusseh wuttattam, qut t8hku, kah kusse, sauunum, kah ukketeahogkôunoh kodtantamoh: ne pish wutti[nnii]neau mataáneukish wutohtimóneash ayeuuhkontogig Zion.
29.9 Chequnappek kah monchanatam8k, mishont8wak kah mau8k, nag kogkeussippam8og qut matta nashpe wine, kekepshaog, qut matta nashpe onkuppe.
29.10 Newutch Jehovah kussokanumunk8 kussukkouéyeue nashaonguh, yáununum kuskesuk8óash: quoshodtumwaenuog, kah kenanawunnaeneum8og, nauwacheg upputtogúhwhoh.
29.11 Kah ummonomansuongan8 wame kuttatuppeyunkquneau sukkúhkehteoeu b8ke kutt8wongash; ne wosketompaog wuttinnumauóneau, neh nohtontauunutcheh, n8waog, yeu ogketash k8wehquetumoush, kah n8wau, n8nanum newutch sukkuhkehteausu.
29.12 Kah b8k aninnumauon noh matta nohtantau8k, n8wau, yeu ogketash k8wehquetumoush, kah n8wau, matta nunnetuhtauouun.
29.13 Newaj Jehovah n8wadt, newutche yeug missinninnuog nuppas8sukkongquog nashpe wutt8n8, kah nashpe wussissitt8n8[a]sh nukquehtianumukquog, qut noadtit in nutontuhtongquog wuttahh8woash, kah nukqushhúk8ongan8 kuhk8tomoadtin, nashpe wosketompae kogohk8waongash.
29.14 Newutche kusseh nukkutchittôusha[m] ussenat monchanatamwe usseonk ut kenugke yeug missinninnuog, monchanatamwe anakausuonk, kah monchanatam8onk: newutche 8waantam8ongan8 waantamwog pish wutahquohtauun, kah 8wohwohtam8ongan8 wunnupwom8oh pish adtahtauóneau.
29.15 Missi wutonkapunnaongan8 neg m8nôi natinneáhogig adtahtauunat ukkogáhqutteam8onk Jehovah, kah wutanakausuongan8oash pohkenaiash, kah n8waog, howan kenogkumun? kah howan k8wahikumun?
29.16 Wunnamuhkut kukqushkohteáshitteaongan8, pish tatupontamun ahk8hqutteae[nin] umman8nskumut: newutche sun woh anakausuonk n8wom8 noh kezteungkup, matta nukkezhik8? asuh ne teag ne weekitteamuk, sun woh unnau neh weekitteanepoh, matta wohwohtam8?
29.17 Sunnummatta majish ogguhsese, kah Lebanon pish quinnuppenumun en mishummeechumue ohteakonit, kah misummeechume ohteuk pish ogquontamun touohkomuk?
29.18 Kah ne kesukok kogkopsau pish n8tam b8ke kutt8wongash: kah pogkinnumwe muskesukquash pish naum8m8ash wutch pogkenum8onganit kah pohkenaiyeuut,
29.19 Manunnissuog wonk pish pishkonteauog 8wekontam8ongan8 ut Jehovahut, kah matchekuog ut kenugke missinninnuog, pish weekontam8oneau 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
29.20 Newutche unkqunneunkqussit mattohhentuppéheau, kah mamanauwontamwenin mohtupáeu, kah wame neg askuhwhontogeg matcheseonk tummehtahwhoog.
29.21 Neg ayeuoncheg wosketomp matcheseaenuunneat wutche kutt8onk, kah upponamauónaoont noh áuskôadt ut usquontamut, kah wutamaunónaoont sampweusseaenuh wutche monteag.
29.22 Newaj yeu n8wadt Jehovah noh pohquohwhunomp Abrahamoh, papaume week Jakob, J[o]kob pish yeuyeu matta akodchu, asuh matta yeuyeu wuskesuk womukushànó.
29.23 Qut nauont wunneechanoh nunnutchegáne anakausuonk ut wunnashomut, nag pish wunneetupanatamwahtoog n8wesuonk, kah pish wunnetupanatamwaheaog 8neetupanatam8moh Jakob, kah pish wabesuonaog um-Manitt8moh Israel.
29.24 Nag wonk pannesitcheg ut nashauonganit pish wohwohtamwog, kah nag m8m8sk8wacheg, pish nehtuhtóog kogohk8wáonk.
30.1 MIssi wutonkapunnaongan8 cheketamwe mukkiesog, n8wau Jehovah, neemunnumwog kogohquttuonk, qut matta nashpe nen, kah neg ágqutcheg onkwhonk, qut matta nashpe nunnashauanitt8moh: onk woh k8tnehteauog matcheséonk en matcheseonganit.
30.2 Neg pomushacheg womsinneat en Egypt (kah matta kogáhqutteog ut nutt8nut) ummenuhkehheonaóont wuhhogkauh nashpe ummenuhkesuonk Pharoh, kah pabuhtantamunat wutonkouohtom Egypt.
30.3 Newutche ummenuhkesuonk Pharoh ne pish k8takodchuwonkaninneau, kah pabahtanumonat onkouòhtom Egypt ne pish kenaswaiyeuongan8.
30.4 Newutche wussontimósimoh apinitcheh Zoan, kah wutann8naéneumoh peyaog Hanes.
30.5 Nag wame akodchuheóog missinninnuog neg matta aninnumauunkig, asuh waneheunkig, kah wadchiyeumu[k]eg qut akodchu[h]éoog kah ukkekontuwaheouh.
30.6 OOweanunn8 sowanie puppinashimwog en wuttamehpunáe kah unkquanumóe, ohkeit uttoh wagk wuske kah nukkone qunnonou, viper, kah n8tae pummunáe ask8k: nag pish kenunnumwog 8weenauwetuongan8, ut uhpegwann8óo[u]t wuske assesog, kah wunnompako[ú]unn8oash 8nuhquiyeum8out camelsog, en missinninnúut ne woh mo wanenehikquéhhettegeh.
30.7 Newutche Egyptiansog pish tahn8che aninnôsuog, kah en wanne wanegik, newaj yeu papaume mishont8wi, nag ummenuhkesuongan8 ne chequnappuonk.
30.8 Yeuyeu monchish wussukwhush ut tableut, ut anaquabhettit, kah wussukwhush ut b8kut, onk woh ne chékeyeu88 micheme kah micheme.
30.9 Yeug cheketam8e missinninnúog, pann8wae mukkiesog, mukkiesog neg matta k[o]hkeihtam8gig wuttinnaumatuonk Jehovah.
30.10 Neg anoncheg namunutche ahque naum8k, quoshódtumwaénúh, ahque sampwe quosh[ó]dtamwiinneau: ussinnan mam8sagish, as8kekodteam8e quoshodtumaiiñean.
30.11 Amayek wutch mayut, pohchagk wutch mayut: 8neetupanatam8moh Israel wohkukquosun ut anaquabeog.
30.12 Newaj yeu n8wadt 8neetupanatam8moh Israel; newutche yeu kutjishantamuneau kutt8onk, kah kuppabahtantamumw8 mukk8kinnuwaonk, kah wounkkag, kah ne kutompadtussinuneau.
30.13 Newaj pish yeu matcheseonk tatuppeyeu88k n8kompskishunk, p8tôem8uk qunuhque qussukquaneutunk, noh uppokshaonk koshkomme teanuk peyaum8.
30.14 Kah noh pish wuttinne sokqshadtauun sokqshadtomuk ahkuhqutteaenin 8wisq, ne sohquetahhamuk, matta pish ukkishpadtam8un; newaje pish mat namehteauomuk, ne adt sohqueta[hh]amuk, kodchuhkisq, nemequomunat n8teau wutch n8teau ahhohtag, asuh quomphamunat nippe wutch passohtheganit.
30.15 Newutche yeu n8wau Lord Jehovah, 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, qushkémuk kah anwôsinimuk pish k8wadchanitteamw8, manunnissimuk kah wutt8anatamuk, ne pish kummenuhkesuongan8, kah kussekenamumw8.
30.16 Qut kussimw8, matta, newutch pish n8semun nashpe horsesog, ne$waj pish wussemwe[y]óg: kah naiyeumutteamun kakenupshoncheg, newaj neg n8swuttahukqueógig pish kogkenupwusháog.
30.17 Muttanonganogkussuog pish wussem8og, pasuk wabuwonont, kah napannatahsuog wabuwunáhettit, pish k8semw8 nô pajeh keánewunneaóont beakon koduhkôagk, kah onatuh muttaagk ut wadchuut.
30.18 Newaj Jehovah pahtussit, onk woh kukkitteamonteanumukou, kah newaj mishehit, onk woh kummonánumukou: newutche Jehovah noh wussittumóe Manit. Wunanumunach neg wame pahtussuonóncheg.
30.19 Newutche missinninnuog pish ayeuog ut Zion, ut Jerusalem: pish matta wonkkummâou, noh pish ahche kukkitteamonteanumuk, ut k8wadtauatonkqussue mauonganit, n8tog neit kenamp8hamunk.
30.20 Kah tohkônogque Lord kittiñumunkquneau onkquommom8e petukqunneg, kah wuttammepunnae nippe, qut onch kukkuhk8tomwehteaeneumog matta pish wonk ontasháog en p8chekeheganit, qut kuskesukquash pish nâau kukkuhk8tomwehteaeneumoh.
30.21 Kah kehtauogash pish ken8tam8m8 kutt8onk en kuppusquanit, n8wau, yeu may, ne pomushagk, quinnuppéog en kuttinohk[ô]unit, kah quinnuppeóg en menadcheani.
30.22 Kah pish wonk kenishketeomw8 wuthogk8ongan8 silvere kittinneukontunkán8, kah wuthogk8unash kussabossume golde unneukontunkanog: nag pish kutogque pogkenóog qushinausue kodchuhkonákinit, pish kuttittamun amaish.
30.23 Neit pish kittinnumunk sokanon ut k8skannemuneat, ne woh ahketeáan, kah petukqununk nashpe ne teashegik wutch ohkeit, kah ne pish wunogk8m8 kah monat: ne kesukok kenetasumog pish nadtupp8og en mummiske tanadtupp8onganit.
30.24 Kah wonk oxinog, kah wuske assesog ne anaskohhogeg ohke, pish mukk8tanéhteamwog weatchimineash, ne seahamoe pahketeamukup nashpe shovel kah paanonteg.
30.25 Kah nishnoh ut kussohkôi, kah qunuhqui wadchuut na pish sepu8 kah kussehtan nippeyeu8, ut pagwanittue kesukodtut, qunuhkquikommukquash panshunk.
30.26 Nano, 8wôhsumóonk nanepaushadt pish tatuppeyeu8 nepâuzsae pumôsum8onganit, kah 8wôsumóonk nepâuz pish nesausuk tahshit tahshin; onatuh nesausuk tahshit kesukquae wôhsum8onk, ne kesukog Jehovah waashpunont uppokshaonganóoash ummissinninneumoh, kah neetskehteunk n8chumwehtahwaeu annehtahwaonganooash.
30.27 Kusseh, 8wesuonk Jehovah n8adtit 8m88, nashquneau nashpe ummusquanittam8onk, kah ne weanun tuhkequan, wussissitt8nit numwohteau nukque musquanittam8onk, kah wenan tatuppeyeu8 mahchekuss8wae n8taut.
30.28 Kah wunnashauonk ánuwutchuwane kussehtanup, pish ohqussinin nôeu mussittipukonit, nohnohkinnumunat wutohtimoneash, nashpe tahn8chee nanahkineg: kah na pish bridle ut wutompekon8wout missinninnuog, panneseáheont.
30.29 Pish kutahtomw8 unn8homaonk nukkonáeu, wunneetupanatamwe moéonk nanawehteomuk, kah wekontamwáeteaháonk, onatuh noh p[a]ont nashpe puhpekq ut 8wadchumut Jehovah ummissugken8moh Israel.
30.30 Kah Jehovah wunn8tamwáheuh wussohsumóe wadtauatonqussuonk, kah pish nahtitteau, 8pittene kutshaumun nashpe wutuhquanittamwe musquanittam8onk, kah nashpe n8n8nae mahchekussuáe n8teau, nashpe seaham8e mishehtash, kah missegan.
30.31 Newutche nashpe 8wadtauagonkqussuonk Jehovah wut-Assyrian quttaúwetáhwóu, togkomit nashpe pogkomunk.
30.32 Kah nishnoh ut ayeuonganit uttôh adt menuhki anwohhou pish pamshunk, ne Jehovah pish ponamauont, ne pish nashpe tabretsash kah harpsash, kah nunnuksháe ayeuwuttuonganehtu, pish ne nashpe ayeukontamun.
30.33 Newutch Tophet kukkuhquttumunah nôadt, nux quagquoshwehtamauun ketass8t, umm8unonteauun, kah kishki: ne noh ohtag n8tau kah monatash wuttuhqunash wunnashauonk Jehovah wunnashqunánumun, ogqueneunkqut brimstone kussitchuwanut.
31.1 MIssi wutonkapunnaongan8 neg wômussitcheg en Egypt wuch aninnumoadtuonk, kah ompatissinwog horsesoh, kah pabuhtantamwog chariotsash, newutche monaash, kah nayeumukqunutcheh horsesoh, newutche ahche menuhkesuoh: qut matta mouninneauou8og 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, asuh matta natinnewhau[ó]og Jehovah.
31.2 Qut onch waantam, kah pish paudto machuk, kah matta pish ontattó8 ukkutt8ongash, qut pish waabéhtauau matcheseaenúe weetu, kah ayeuuhkonittue wutannosuongan8 neg asécheg matcheseonk.
31.3 Qut Egyptiansog wosketomp8og, & matta Mani[t]tt88og, & wut-horsesum8oh weyausu8oh, kah matta nashauanitt88og: Jehovah summagunuk wunnutch, naneese noh aninnausit pish penushau, kah noh aninnumauut pish penushau, kah nag wamu pish moeu penusháog.
31.4 Newutch[è] yeu nuttugqun Jehovah: onatuh qunnonou, kah qunnonuwem, mishont8wae tohq[u]nont ne tohqunoncheh, monanutcheh nanaushipsaen[ù]h ayeuuhkonittue wehquetuog nah wutch, matta wabesu wutch 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8, asuh matta mishanehheaout wuhogkuh wutche nag monacheg: netatuppe Lord ayeuhteaunit pish n8keu wutáyeuwehteaunsh[ô]nat wadchu Zion, kah wutche 8wadcheum.
31.5 Onatuh psuksesuk pâmunáhettit, netatuppe Jehovah ayeuhteaunit pish wadchanau Jerusalem, kah wadchanuwae pish uppohquohwhuttauun, kah quoshkodteadt pish 8wadchanumun.
31.6 Qushkek noh en, neh wunneechanoh Israel menuhke amaehtauoncheh.
31.7 Newutche ne kesukok nishnoh pasuk mittamwossis pish pogkenau silvere wuttinneukontunkoh, kah wosketomp golde wuttinneukontunkoh; neh nehenwonche kenutchegash kezheumpuh wutche matcheseonk.
31.8 Neit wut$Assyrian pish penushau nashpe wuttogkodteg, matta menuhkesu[é]nin: kah wuttogkodteg matta kuttamunge wosketomp, pish ummahtupanukqun: qut noh pish wussemo wutch togkodteganit, kah 8skeneumoh pish papuhquojhéonineuh.
31.9 Kah wabesue pish qushkodteau en 8manskut, kah wussontimósimoh pish qusháog mataag k[ó]unumunutcheh, wussin Jehovah, noh wunn8tom ohtag ut Sion, kah ahhut sabasósit ut Jerusalem.
32.1 KUsseh, ketass8t pish sampweusseáe nanauwunnuau, kah sontimosog pish wussittumoe nanauwunnuáog.
32.2 Kah wosketomp pish tatuppeyeu8 asompamukque ayeuonganit wutche wabanit kah unkwhonk wutch mishehtash, onatuh sepue nippeash ut [n]abohteaiyeuut, onatuh mishikqussukquane onkauohteau, ut sauunnumoe ohkeit.
32.3 Kah wuskesuk88ash neg nagig matta pish pogkenum8mun8ash, kah wuhtauogk8oash neg n8togig, pish kuhkeihtamwog.
32.4 Wuttah wonk kákinne musquantog posh wohtam8m8 wahteóonk, nohnogkiáe meenan, pakodche pish wunának8waog.
32.5 Nishkeneunkqussuenin matta pish wonk hennau chippinin, kah kasenussit matta pish hennou mag8énin.
32.6 Newutche nishkeneunkqussuaénin unn8wau nishkeneunkquokish, kah wuttah ussémo matcheseonk eiantukiyeue ussenat, kah ayeuuhkônitt8e unnónát Jehovah, mohchiéhheonat ukketeahogkounoh noh kódtupwit, kah wohkuhquohsumwaheau kohkutt8nutcheh 8tattam8onk.
32.7 Wutauwohteaongash wonk noh kasenussit matchi[t]ash: natwontam matche natwontam8ongash, paguanonat matchekuwog nashpe pann8wae kutt8wongash, quenahikqutcheg sampweyéhettit[.]
32.8 Qut wunnenéhuwaénin natwontam wunnenehuae teaguassinish kah nashpe wunnenehuwae teaguassinish pish neep[o]u.
32.9 Nepo8k kenaau mittamwossisog sasegeneamogish: n8tam8k n8wadtauatonkqussuonk mattohhentupontamwe wuttauninneunk, kuhkeihtam8k nukkutt8wonk.
32.10 M8chetikquinne, & kodtum8ash pish k8tamehpunomw8, kenaau mat toh$hen tupantam8e mittamwossissog: newutche wenominneash pish mat nekininn8ash, matta pish mauunneaun.
32.11 Nunnukshunk kenau sasegenamwe mittamwossissog, wuttamanátam8k kenaau mattohhentupanatam8ogish, mukk8keg, kah poskishegk, puttukquobpissuontam8k man8tionak ut kussegon8out.
32.12 Nag pish mauog wutch sogkodtunkash, wutch wunne ohteuhkonash, wutch mishummeechume weenomwussippog.
32.13 Ut wutohk8out nummissinninnumog pish 8tch sonkinneau asinnekoussog, kah koussog, nux nish$noh ut wekontamwe wetuomut, ut wekontamwe otanat.
32.14 Newutche mishikkomukquash pish ahquontamunash, keitotanae monacheg pish nukkonnoog, ummanshkash kah qunuhk8komukquash, nish pish asampamukquotash micheme, 8wekontam8ongan8 touohkomukque assessog, flokse tanadtupp8onk.
32.15 Nô pajeh nashauanit sokenumonteaog wutch wohqut, kah touohkomuk mishummeechumme ohteukonu8k, kah mishummeechume ohteuk ogquontamuk touohkomuk.
32.16 Neit wussittumoonk pish ayeum8 touohkomuk, kah sampweusseonk ohtaut mishummeechumue ohteuhkonit.
32.17 Kah sampweusseae anakausuonk ne pish wunohteaonk: kah sampweusseae usseonk ne manunnissuonk kah pahkontam8onk micheme.
32.18 Kah nummissinninnumog pish ayeuog wunohteae ayeuonganit, kah menuhki ayeuonganehtu, kah wunohteae anwohsinwe ayeuonganehtu.
32.19 Missegog, n8kit ut touohkomuk, kah keitotan pish tiohqunkquodt, tiuhquonkque ayeuonganit.
32.20 Wunnanumittegk ohketeaogish kiṣhke wame nippeit, na en sohh8kouogish wussét8ash oxinog kah assesog.
33.1 MIssi kutonkapunaonk woskhuwaan, kah matta k8woskhitteop, kah as8kekodteam8e ussean kah nag matta kutas8kekomuk8panneg: chequnapean wutch k8woskhuwaonganit pish ken k8woskhit, chequnapean wunassumuwae usseonganit nag pish k8nassum8e unnehikquog.
33.2 Woi Jehovah, kitteamonteanuminnean, kuppahtsuonumunonup: ken nag uhpittenhettich nish$noh mohtompan, kah wonk n8wadchanitteaonganun wuttamehpunamuk.
33.3 Wogkouee wadtauatongqussimuk missinninnuog wussem8og: tahshinadt kuhhog, wutohtimoneash seahhamunapash.
33.4 Kah kussequttahhamoonk pish mohmounumun onatuh mohmounuk m8p: onatuh quaqueshontae popomshaonk, ne pish wuttinne quogqueeu tahtashkuhkauon.
33.5 Jehovah misheheau, newutche qunuhqui ayeu, numwohtau Zion wussittumoonk kah sampweusseonk,
33.6 Kah waantamoonk kah wahteoon pish ne ummenuhkesuonk kutahquompiyeum, kah wadchanuae menuhkesuonk, qushaonk Jehovah ne wunnompakou.
33.7 Kusseh, ummenuhkeseum8uh nag pish poquadchit ut móoh: wunohteae ann8nitcheg pish weesogohposuog.
33.8 Taumaogquash yaunegenash: pomushaenin ahqshau: noh pohqunum wunn8waonk, noh jishontam keitotanash: mattohhentupanumau8 howae wosketompoh.
33.9 Ohke maueem8, kah ahp8teau, Lebanon akodchu, kah tummetahwhau: Sharon ogqueneunkqussu touohkomukqut, kah Baashan; kah Carmel ne[n]emonteáog ummeechummuóngan8.
33.10 Yeuyeu nutomohkem n8wau Jehovah, yeuyeu nummishhit, yeuyeu nuttahshin nuhhog.
33.11 Pish k8wompequomw8 wussadteamunash, pish keneechamw8 séque kepenunk: kenashaongan8 onatuh n8tau, pish kummahtsikquneau.
33.12 Kah missinninnuog pish ogqueneunkqussuog chokkoswut lime, onatuh tummehtahwhaeu asinnekôussog pish chikoswóog ut n8taut.
33.13 N8tam8k kenaau nôappéogish uttoh asée, kah kenaau paswoppéogish, wahteau8k nummenuhkesuonk.
33.14 Zione matcheseanuog wabesuog, wabesuonk nuhkuhkongquog eiantogkeiog, howan ut kenugke nuhhogkanonut pish ayit mahchukkissuwaeu n8taut? howan ut kenugke nuhhogkanonut pish ayit micheme chikohsuonganit?
33.15 Noh sampweusseae pomushadt, k[à]h sampwe án8wadt, noh sekeneog woskehuwae anuhamoadtúongash: seahog wunnutchegash wutch kogkôunumunat kemunkquodtunk, noh kobhog wuhtauogash wutch n8tamunat musqueheonk, kah yanunuk wuskesukquash wutch naumunat machuk.
33.16 Noh pish qunuhqui ayeu, wutushphouaongane ayeuonk, ne ukqussukquanonkônous, petukqununk pish aninnumauau, wunnippe pish papaneyéu8.
33.17 Kuskesukquash pish naau ketass8toh ut wunnetuonganit: nag pish kuhkinneamwog ohke ne n[ó]ohtag.
33.18 Kuttah pish natwontam unkqueneunkquok, uttiyeuoh Scribe? uttiyeuoh attumunumwenin? uttiyeuoh agketog qununkqui kommukquash.
33.19 Matta pish kenauoh nashquetue missinninnuog, siohkont8wae missinninnuog neg woh mo wohtauoacheg: nahnagkiae menan ne woh mo wohtam8an.
33.20 Kukinneam8k Zion moeongane nukkeitotat: kuskesukquash pish naum8m8ash Jerusalem manunne ayeuonk, Tabernakle ne matta pish n8kinum8muk, matta pasuk nepattuhquonk pish ontahto8un micheme, kah matta pasuk uppemunneat pish pokshan8.
33.21 Qut na$ut sohsumoe Jehovah noh pish kuttatupanumoun mishekishkae kah kussitchuwane sepue ayeuonk: ne matta pish aomun8g wuttuhhongane kuht8nog, kah matta pish wunnegane kuht8nog paumushomun8.
33.22 Newutche Lord noh k8sittumwaeneumun, Jehovah noh naumatuonk ayimunkqueog, Jehovah nukkehtass8tamomun, noh pish k8wadchanukqun.
33.23 Kukkishpinegash ompinimunash, matta wunne menehkheauog wussepogkonganuhtugk8oh, n8nanumoog sépagkinnumun sepagheg: neit mishe tohqunumwe sequttahhamoonk chachaubenumun n8chumwesitcheg nemunnumwog tohqunnumoonk.
33.24 Kah noh wadôhkit matta pish n8woou nummahchinam: missinninnuog neg na wadohkitcheg, pish ahquontamauóog ummatcheseonganooash.
34.1 PAhs8tshagk, kenaau wutohtimóneash n8tamunat, kah kuhkeitam8k kenaau missinninnuog, ohke n8taj, kah wame ne naohtag, muttaok, kah wame ne waj sohham8m8uk.
34.2 Newutche ummishe musquanitteaonk Jehovah ohteau ut wame wutohtimóneat, kah wutôskoméhheaonk ut wame ukkenauwameongan8oont: noh uppápaquane pagwanoh, nah upponuh paguanaonganit,
34.3 Kah wonk pagwatauutcheh pish sohwhôokonuh, kah wuttann8wongan8 pish wutch sohham8m8 wunnupwe hogkaóont, kah wadchuash pish mohtupohtaash nashpe 8sqheongan8.
34.4 Kah wame kesukque kenauwameonk pish ompéog, kah kesukquash pish ogque tuttuppaginausuash ahtunk wussukwhosimuk, kah wame ukkenawameonk pish ogque penushaog weenómwussippog pá[n]shunk, kah onatuh panshunk wutch figsuhtugqut.
34.5 Newutche nuttogkodteg kutchissittauun ut kesukqut, kusseh, pish 8núhkuhkongquneau Idumea, kah ut nummatánumáe missinninnuut, en wussittum8onganit.
34.6 Wuttogkodteg Jehovah numwohteau musqueheonk; ne wu[u]nogquehteauun nashpe wanogqinnu8k, kah nashpe lambse kah goatse 8squeheonk, nas[k]pe ramse wutt8unnusse wees: newutche Jehovah ayim sephausuonk: ut Bozrah kah miṣhe paguanittuonk ut Idumea ohkeit.
34.7 Kah nequttu[un] pish 8weeche w8mseumoh, & oxinog weeche bulsog, & wutohkeu pish wuttadtippáh naṣhpe musqueheonk: kah uppuppissiyeum8 pish weesteauun naṣhpe wees.
34.8 Newutche ne Jehovah wutann8tauwae kesukodtum: kah onkquatongane kodtum8ash wutche Zione penuanittuonk.
34.9 Kah nish kussehtannuppeash pish quinnuppenumunash en pittu$ut, kah uppuppissiyeum en brimstonut kah ne ohke pish chikohtae pitteu8.
34.10 Matta pish ontham8un nukonae kah kesukodae, ne pukuttau pish micheme ushpem8: wutch pometuonganit onk yean pometu[o]nganit pish mohtuppashin, matta pish howan uppamuhkom8un micheme.
34.11 Qut kuttis kah bittern pish wutohta[n]unneau, kah wonk k8k8khos, kah konkont pish 8tohkin, kah pish naswaiyeue pemunneohtane ukkuhkhamun kah mahchiyeue qussukquanash.
34.12 Pish wekomaog wussontimosum8oh en ass8tam8onganit, qut matta howane pish na wutappeinneau, kah wame wussontimos[u]m8oh pish monteag wunnuoh.
34.13 Kah asinnekoussoh pish sontuoh ut ummishekommukquehtu; netlesash kah koussog ut 8wonkôn8sinn8wout, & ne pish wutayeuongan8 Dragonsog, kah ummoeayeuongan8 k8k8khausog.
34.14 Touohkomukque wonk puppinashimwog pish nogkishkouaog munnahhanne puppinashimwog; kah satyr pish wehkomau weecheheioh: kah weewes na pish wuttit anwósinin, kah pish namehteou anwosinoe ayeuonk.
34.15 Mishe k8k8khaus ná pish wuttit wadchishahkon, kah pish ahtinahsin, kah pwohkuhhoeyau, kah miayeu ut agwu wutonkouohtomut: na wonk pish ut vultursog miaeog nish$noh pasuk weeche wutishquoshomoh.
34.16 Natinneakontam8k ut upb8kum Lord, kah ogketam8k: wanne pasuk yeush pish mat teagwuninno, wanne pasuk pish quenauhik8 wutishquoshomoh: newutche nut8n wutann8hteamun, & wunnashauanitt8moh ummukinoh.
34.17 Kah wuttit tanohtóadtuwanshuh, kah wunnutcheg pemuneat wunnashpe chachabinuh: nag pish ummichemohtauuneau, wutch pometuonganit onk yaan pometuonganit na pish wuttaiinneau.
35.1 TOuohkomuk kah touwushinne ayeuonk pish nah 8wekontam8onuh, kah touohkomuk pish muskouantam, kah peṣhauau onatuh rose.
35.2 Pish m8cheke peṣhauau, kah pish wekontamwe kah ket8hamáe muskouantam: wussohsumoonk Lebanon pish unninnuma[u]on, 8neetuonk Carmel kah Sharon: nag pish naumwog wussohsumóonk Jehovah, kah 8neetuonk kum[-]Manitt8mun.
35.3 Menehketeo8k n8chumwe menutchegash, kah menuhkesuweheuk n8chumwe mukkuttukquog.
35.4 Unnók nag wabesuwutte[à]honcheg, menuhkesek, ahque wabesek, kusseh, kum-Manitt8mw8 pish ann8tauwae peyau Manit nashpe onkquatunk, noh pish peyau k8wadchanukqunnaout.
35.5 Neit wuskesuk88ash pogkenukeg pish wohshwem8[à]sh, kah kohkobsahtauogash pish pohquaémoash.
35.6 Neit pish n8chumwesuenin ogque quequeshau áyompaut, kah mo kakutt8e meenan pish ketohomom8: newutche nippe pish sonkhetchuan wutch touohkomuk, kah kussitchúanash ut touohkomuk.
35.7 Kah kôhkohteadtáe ohke pish nuppissú8, & kúhkuht8n8e ohke ne pish nippeae tohkekomu8, ut dragone ayeuonganit, uttoh nish$noh pasuk sepsuk, na pish mosketú8 wekinashquash, kah rushes[á]sh.
35.8 Kah toumaog na pish ohteau, kah may, kah ne pish hettamun wunneetupanatamwe may, nishkeneunkqussit matta pish uppaumukkomm8un, qut ne pish yeug wutche, papaumusháenuog, tohkônogque ass8khettit, matta pish pehchumma8og.
35.9 Na matta pish qunnón8wunn8, kah wanne m8wheyausae puppinashim na pish ukkuhkuhquein, matta pish na$ut nameheaun: qut manouhwhutcheg na pish uppomushoneau.
35.10 Kah manouwhoncheh Jehovah pish qushkeog, kah pish peyaog Sion nashpe ket8hom[á]ongash, kah machemohtag wekontamoonk ut uppuhkuk8óut, nag pish attumunumwog mskauantamoonk kah wekontamoonk, kah unkquanumoonk kah mishânom8onk pish pt8sheau.
36.1 KAh n$nih nabo weyáue kodtom8m Hezekiah ketass8t, Sennacherib Assyriae ketass8t ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhquehtauau wame pummeneutaúsue keitotanash Judah, kah nish wussohkomunash.
36.2 Kah Assyriae ketass8t ann8nau Rabshekah wutch Lachish en Jerusalem, en Hezekiah ketass8t[im]wut, weeche miṣhe kenauwameoh: kah ne[é]pau kishke kohkuhquóhtag ohtopaṣhitteunk, ut mayut wutohteuhkonit pôanek8énin.
36.3 Eliakim wunnaumonuh Hilkiah noh en sohham, noh piahquttuk weetu, kah Shebna noh Scribe, kah Joash wunnaumonuh Asaph mehquontamwahuwaénin.
36.4 Kah Rabshakeh nah wuttinuh, yeuyeu unnók Hezekiah, yeu wussin miṣhe ketass8t, Assyriae ketass8t, chaugua yeu teagwe yeu wutt8anatam8onk ne pabahtantaman?
36.5 Nussim (kussim, qut webe tahn8che kutt8wongash) nutóhto kog[à]hquttuonk, kah menuhkesuonk en ayeuuhkonat: qut h[o]wan kuppabahtanum, waj chek[é]htauwéan?
36.6 Kusseh, kuppabahtantam pohquiyeue k8wékinasque anwohhou, ut Egypt, ne howan ompatussum8óntog, woh ummiskouwutchinun: ne wuttátupéyeuwunneau Pharaoh Egypte ketass8t, wame neh pabahtanumukqutcheh.
36.7 Qut ussean, nuppabahtanumómun Jehovah num-Manitt8mun[?] sun noh matta, ukqunúhqui ayeuongash, kah wut-altarumash Hezekiah wunneemunumunapash, kah unnóp Judahoh kah Jerusalemoh, pish k8wowussummuwómw8 ut anaquohtag yeu Altar?
36.8 Newutche yeuyeu mag8k kenohtohsuongash, k8wehquetumoush, en nussontimômut Assyriae ketass8t, kah kuttinninnumoush neese muttañonganogkussuog horsesog, tapenuman wutch k8weech8humukqunnaóut neh ná8mahetticheh.
36.9 Tohwutch neit quinuppequaéhtauadt pasuk peississit mugquomp nussontimom wuttinneumoh, kah pabahtánumadt Egypt wutch chariotsash kah nay8mukqutcheg horsesoh?
36.10 Kah yeuyeu nen ayeuuhkonittue nukkuhkuhquéhtamun yeu ohke matta wusseinat Jehovah, pagwatauunat? Jehovah nuttinuk, ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhquéhtash yeu ohke, kah pagwataush.
36.11 Neit Eliaim kah Shebna, kah Joah unnaog Rábshakehoh, unnont8wanumau k8wehquetumoush kittinneumog Syraie unnont8waonk, newutche n8wohtamunan: kah ahque unnont8wanumaiinnean Jewse unnont8waonk, ut wehtauogk8wout missinninnuog neg apitcheg pummeneutonganit,
36.12 Qut Rabshakeh n8wau, sun nussontimom nutann8nukqus en kussontimomut, kah en kuhhogkat, unneat yeush kutt8wongash? sunnummatta nuttin ánn8nuk8h wosketompahtu neg apitcheg pummeneutonganit, onk woh meechuog nehenwonche umm8yu, kah wuttattamwog wunnuneyeu, weeche kenauu?
36.13 Neit Rabshakeh neepáu, kah mishont8wau, nashpe Jewse unnont8waonk, kah n8wau, n8tám8k ukkutt8wongash mishe ketass8t, Assyriae ketass8t.
36.14 Yeu wussin ketass8t, ahque Hezechiah as8kekomuk8k, newutche matta pish tapenum8 kuppohquohwhunukqunnaoout.
36.15 Asuh ahque Hezechiah pabahtantamwahik8k Jehovah$ut, n8wonat, Jehovah pish wunamuhkut kuppohquohwhunukqun, yeu keitotan matta pish mag8un, en wunnutcheganit Assyriae ketass8t.
36.16 Kuhkehtauuhteok Hezechiah, newutche yeu wussin Assyriae ketass8t, wunn8waonk ayimaiek nashpe mag8onk, kah sohham8k en nuhhogkat: kah meech8k nish$noh pasuk nehenwonche, 8wenomwussippog, kah nehenwonche, figsehtug, kah wuttattam8k nish$noh pasuk ohtopashitteae nippeash.
36.17 Noh pajeh nuppéyonat, kah keneemunumunnaoout en ohket tatuppeyeu8uk nehenwonche kutohkeyeuout: weatchiminee ohke, kah wine ohke petukqunneganee kah weenominneohtekonee ohke.
36.18 Nupweshanukquehteok Hezechiah unn8wadt, Jehovah pish kuppohquohwhunukqun: sun howae wutohtimounneae Manittuog pohquohwúttoog wutohtu wutch wunnutcheganit Assyriae ketass8t?
36.19 Uttiyeug Hamathe kah Arpade Manitt8og? uttiyeug Sepharvaim8e M[à]nitt8og? kah sun nag pohquohwhunoog Samaria wutch nunnutcheganit?
36.20 Howanig neg ut kénugke wame yeug wutohtimoinne Manitt8og, neg pohquohwhuttunkeg wutohtu wutch nunnutcheganit, waj woh Jehovah pohquohwuttunk Jerusalem wutch nunnutcheganit?
36.21 Qut nag chequnappuog, kah matta wunnamp8hamauouh pasuk kutt8onk, newutche ketáss8t wutann8teám8onk, ne an8womuk namp8hamauuhteok,
36.22 Neit Eliakim wunnaumonuh Hilkiah, noh piahquttuk wetu, kah Shebna noh Scribe kah Joah wunnaumonuh Asaph mehquontamwayeuaenin, peyaunáog Hezechiahoh, sokqshadtauwehettit wuthogk8un8oash, kah nah wuttinnonaoash ukkutt8wongash Rabshakeh.
37.1 KAh n$nihyeup Hezechiah ketass8t yeu n8tog nehnekshadto wuthogk8unash kah man8tionak hogk8, kah petutteau wekit Jéhovah.
37.2 Kah ann8nau Eliakim noh nanauwunuk weetu, Shebna noh Scribe & Sepausuenue Eldersog, agqhettit man8tionak, en Esayah quoshodtumwaenuut wunnaumonuh Amoz.
37.3 Kag nág wuttinouh, yeu wussin Hezechiah, yeu kesukok wuttamehpunae kesukod, kah auskomae, kah Blasphemae, newutche mukkiog kodtauweetuog, kah matta menuhkesuonganun8h neechonat.
37.4 Pagwodcheh woh Jehovah n8tam ukkutt8wongash Rabshakeh, neh Assyriae ketàss8t, wussontimomoh an8nukqut kehkomonat pomantamwae God, kah pish auskontam kutt8wongash nish Lord kum$Manitt8m n8togish: newutche tahshinush kuppeantam8onk, wutche sequttahwhutcheg ne apitcheg.
37.5 Neit wuttinneumoh ketass8t Hezechiah peyaonaog Isaiahoh.
37.6 Kah Isaiah nah wuttinuh, yeu woh kittinnoneau kussontimom8h, yeu wussin Jehovah, wabesuontam8hkon kutt8ongash nish n8tamanish, nish nashpe wuttinneumoh Assyriae ketass8t nupblasphemónukquog.
37.7 Kusseh, nupponamau nashauongoh, kah noh pish n8tam unnussittunkquôt, kah pish qushkeu en nehenwonche wutohkit, kah nuppunushah nashpe togkodteg ut nehenwonche wutohkit.
37.8 Neit Rabshakeh qushkeu, kah namehheau Assyriae ketass8toh, ayeuuhkontamunat Libnah: newutche n8tamup, moncheai wutch Lachish.
37.9 Kah n8tamup papaume Tirhakah Ethiopiae ketass8t, noh sohham kutayeuuhkonukqunat: kah n8tog, ann8nau ann8náenuh en Hezechiahut n8wonat.
37.10 Yeu woh kuttinnoneau Hezechiah Judae ketass8t, n8wagk, kum-Manitt8m noh pabahtanumadt as8kukkomuk8hkon, n8wonat Jerusalem matta pish mag8un en wunnutchegani Assyriae ketass8t.
37.11 Kusseh, ken8tamup Assyriae ketass8tamwog, ne anteauhettit wame wutohtimoineash, papuhquanne pagwanonaoont, kah ken sun woh kuppohquohwhunit?
37.12 Wutohtimoune Manitt8og, sun nah uppohquohwhunouh, neh n8shog mahche pagwanahetticheh, ut Gozanut, kah Haranut, kah Rezephut, kah wunneechanoh Eden neg apitcheg Telassar?
37.13 Uttiyeuoh Hamathe ketass8t, Arphade ketass8t, kah Sepharvaimme otanae ketass8t, Henah kah Ivah?
37.14 Kah Hezechiah attumunum wussukwhonk, wutch wunnutcheganit ann8naenin kah wutogketamun: kah Hezechiah kuhkuhqueu en wekit Jehovah, kah wussepaginumun ut anaquabit Jehovah.
37.15 Kah Hezechiah peantamauau Jehovahoh, n8wau,
37.16 Woi Jehvoah ayeuteaunit, um-Manitt8moh Israel, ken ayean nashauwe Cherubimsut, ken um-Manitt8m8uh, ken webe, wame ass8tam8ongash ut ohkeit, ken kukkesteoh kesuk kah ohke.
37.17 Ahch8sitash, woi Jehovah, kah n8tash wôhshinush kuskesukquash woi Jehovah, kah naish, kah n8tash wame ukkutt8wongash Senacherib, nish an8teamwutcheh kehkomonat pomantamwae God.
37.18 Wunnamuhkut woi Jehovah, Assyriae ketass8tamwog, pagwodteoog wame wutohtimoneash, kah wutohtuoash.
37.19 Kah unnohteaog um[$]Manitt8m8uh en n8taut: newutche nag matta Manitt88og, qut wosketompae wunnutchegane anakausuongash, mehtug káh qussuk: newaj nah pagwanont.
37.20 Newutche yeuyeu, woi Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, wadchaninneau wutch wunnutcheganit onk woh wame ass8tam8ongash muttaohket, wahteauog, ken Jehovah, ken webe.
37.21 Neit Isaiah wunnaumonuh Amoz ann8team8, en Hezechiahut, n8wau yeu wussin Jehvovah um-Manitt8m8oh Israel, paantamauwean ayeuuhkonittue Senacherib, Assyriae ketass8t.
37.22 Yeu ukkutt8onk Jehovah ne an8wop papaume nagum: peénomp, wuttaunoh Zion kutjishanumuk, kah momontauae kutahan8wehtunk, wuttaunoh Jerusalem, kenónokuhquaehtunk.
37.23 Howan kuhkékom, kupblasphemon? kah howan ayeuuhkonittue kummishont8wánumau, kah kukqun[ú]hque táhshinum kuskesukquash, ayeuuhkonittue 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
37.24 Nashpe kittinneumog kukkehkom Jehovah, kah kussip, nashp[é] mataánukish nutchariotsumash, nukkuhkuhquem en kudohkôag wadchuuhkontu, sussippoeu Lebanon, kah nuttumehtah quanunkqussitcheg chikuppog, kah pepenamwe k8wâog, kah pish nuppetutteam kodukóag wussissipôiyeumut, kah uk-Carmelle touohkomuk.
37.25 N8wonuhkontamup kah n8tatumup nippe, kah nashpe nusseet nukôhkonéhteap wame wusseppum8ash neg wéenuhkauógkutcheg.
37.26 Sunnummatta n8adt ken8tam8mus uttoh ánteau, kah n8adt nukkuhkenauéhtinneap? yeuyeu nukkezteauun, onk woh ken kummahchumwehteauuneat pummeneutausue keitotanash wep8to8ut.
37.27 Newaj neg na wadohkitcheg n8chumwesuog, kah chepshanaog kah naswaiyeuog, tatuppeyeu8og ohteuhkone moskehtuut, kah ohchippogqut, kah, woskeche weetuome moskehtuut, kah pissagquodtinnit weachiminneash.
37.28 Qut n8wahteoh kutayeuonk, kah kussohham8onk kah kuppetukonat, kah kummusquanummuonk.
37.29 Newutche kummusquanummuonk, kah k8wogkoue[ó]nk kuhkuhquem8 en nuhtauogkut: newaj ponum n8hquon kutchónit, kah nup-bridlum ut kussisset8nit, kah kukkushquenush en mayut ne wâman.
37.30 Kah yeu pish kukkehkinneasuonk yeu kodtum8k pish kummeechumw8, ne nehenwonchekik: kah nahohtóeu kodtumuk, ne nan noh wadchegit: kah nishwe kodtum8k ohkehteagk, kah kepenum8k, kah weenominneohketeagk, kah meech8k ne meechu[m]muonk.
37.31 Kah sekqshoncheg ut wekit Judah neg pohquohhogig, nág pish ohkeayeu unuhchabukaog, kah wohkummiyeu unummeechummuog.
37.32 Newutche ashqushoncheg pish sohhamwog wutch Jerusalem, kah neg wutch pohquohhogig wadchuut Zion: wuszealum Jehovah ayeuteaunit yeu pish wutussen.
37.33 Newaj yeu n8wadt Jehovah papaume wutássyriae ketass8t, matta pish petutteaou pummeyeu keihtotanat kah matta pish nawuttit in kouhquodt kah matta pish naṣhpe peyoou ogqunegash, & matta pish wutayeuuhkonittue kutaham8un.
37.34 Ne may wagkup, ne pish wonk wuttin qushken kah matta pish yeu petuttutteaun keihtotan n8wau Jehovah[-]
37.35 Newutche yeu n8wadchumun keihtotan, wadchanumunat wutche nen nehenwonche, kah wutche nuttinneum David.
37.36 Neit wut-Angelumoh Jehovah sohhamwoh, kah nushau ut wuttuppukkussinn8wongan8wout Assyriansog, nequt pasuk8e, kah shwosuk tahshinchage, kah napanna tahshe muttanonganogkussuog: kah nompoaeu omohkehettit kusseh nag wame nupwog.
37.37 Neit Senacherib wut-Assyriae ketass8t amaeu kah monchu kah qushku, kah ayeu Ninive.
37.38 Kah nniyeup wó[u]ssumont weekit Nishroch ummanitt8m, Hidramelech kah Sharezer wunnaumonuh, wuttogkomukquoh ohkeit, kah Esarhaddon wunnaumonuh wunnompe nanawunnuwómukquoh.
38.1 YEush ut kesukodtash Hezekiah mahchinau en nuppunat, kah Isaiah quoshodtumwaen wunnaumonuh Amoz peyaonukquoh, kah wuttugquoh, yeu wussin Jehovah, wunohtoush kek, newutche pish kenup, kah matta kuppomantamóh.
38.2 Neit Hezechiah quinnippinnum wuskesuk en sussipponkomuk, kah péantamauau Jehovah.
38.3 Kah n8wau, mehquontash yeuyeu woi Jehovah k8wehquetumoush, uttoh an pomusháomp ut anaquabean wunnamuhkutée, káh pañuppeteaháeu kah nummahche ussem né wanekik ut anaquabean, kah Hezechiah muttauhpâsu.
38.4 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Isayah n8wau,
38.5 Monchish us Hezechiah, yeu wussin Jehovah, um-Manitt8moh David k8sh: nunn8tam kuppeantamoonk, nunnaum kussippegwash: kusseh, nukk8tn[e]hteoh kukkesukodtumash nabo napanna tahshe kodtumwae.
38.6 Kah pish kuppohquohwhunush kah yeu keitotan, wutch wunnutcheganit Ass[y]iae ketass8t: kah n8wadchanum yeu otán.
38.7 Kah yeu pish kuhkinneasuonk wutch Jehovahut, woh wutussen Jehovah ne an8wadt.
38.8 Kusseh, nutomponcheáhtoh dialle onkauohteau ne womussúm8uk ut Ahaze wussun-dialumut, ompo[h]ch[é]eu piogquonéhtuonk neit nepauz piogquonehtuongane qushkeu, nish mahche pamuhkogkish.
38.9 OOsukuhwhesuonk Hezechiah Judae ketass8t, mahchinadt, kah keteóp wutch ummahchinónat.
38.10 Nussip tâmussumuk nukkesukodtumash, pish nuttom weenohkée squontamut: sequnnumukish nukkodtum8mash nutamaunumonteanash.
38.11 Nussip matta pish nunnau Jehovah, Jehovah ut pomantamoe ohkeit: matta pish wonk nunnauoh wosketomp, weeche wadohkitcheg muttaohkit.
38.12 Nukkechisuonk nutontoht[ò]nteau onatuh nanaushepsaen wekit: nuttummussum nukketeaonk onatuh monakinehteáenin: pish nuttummussuk nashpé mohchim8e mahchinnaonguh: w[u]tch kesukodtut pajeh wunnonk8ut, pish kummahcheh.
38.13 Nutogketomup pajeh mohtompanúut, onatuh qunnonouut pish pokshadto wame nuskonash, wutch kesukodtut pajeh wunnonk8ut k8wohkukquohsumeh.
38.14 Onatuh sassadt asuh mameesashquis, ne nuttinn8won, nutogque mauop wuskuhwhunanâut: nuskesukquash sauunum88ash spadtauwompinneat: woi Jehovah, nussinukkuhhuk, nontumah.
38.15 Toh pish nussim? naneeswe nuttukqunáh, kah nagum wutussen: pish nukkemwusham ut wame nukkodtum8mut, n8wésogke keteahogkôunit.
38.16 Woi Lord nashpe yeush pomantamwog wosk[e]tompaog: kah ut wame yeush nunnashauongane pomantamoonk ohteau, neit kukketeáheh kah kuppomantamwaheh
38.17 Kusseh, wutche wunohteaonk nutáhtop mishe weesogkunóonk, qut k8womonomp nukketeahogkou, kah kuppohquohwhun wutch aninn8e pissohtheganit; newutch kuttinnôhteap wame nummatcheseongash kuppusquanit.
38.18 Newutche weenohk[é] mattá woh k8wóweenomuk8h, nupp8onk matta kummishanumuko[u], neg womussitcheg en passahtheganit, matta woh annoontamóog k8namuhkutéayeum.
38.19 Pâmontog, pâmontog noh pish k8woweenomuk, ne ásee yeu kesukok, wut8shimau pish wahteauwahuah k8namuhkutéyeum en mukkiesut.
38.20 Jehovah nukkenuppe wadchanuk, newaj pish unn8homóog nukket8homaongash nashpe pemunneohtone puhpegk, tosohke pomontamog ut wekit Jehovah.
38.21 Newutche Isaiah n8wop, neemunumohettich figse puttukqutchéi, kah ponaskéhtuáhettich mogquenit, kah pish keteau.
38.22 Hezekiah wonk n8wop, teagwe kuhkinneasuonk onk woh nukkuhkuhquem en weekit Jehovah.
39.1 NA ahquompak Merod[a]ch-Baladan wunnaumonuh Baladan Babylone ketass8t, negonshúau wussukwhongash noh en, kah mag8onk en Hezechiahut, newutche n8tam mahchinap, kah keteau.
39.2 Kah Hezechiah nah 8weekontam8ónuh, kah wunnohtinuh wunnompak8unikkomuk, silver, kah gold, kah spicesash, kah mishôadtue sussequeáeu pummeeash, kah wame ukkenauwamée week, káh wame ne ohtag ut weekit, kah ut wame wutass8tom8onganit, ne Hezechiah matta nohtinnunk.
39.3 Neit Isaiah quoshodtumwáen peyaonau Hezechiah ketass8toh, kah wuttinuh, toh n8waog yeug wosketompaog? kah tohnoh 8mwog en kuhhogkat, kah Hezechiah n8wop, neg nuppeyaonukquog wutch nôadtit wutohtimoneat, wutch Babylon.
39.4 Neit n8wop, teagwa naumwog ut kékit? k[á]h Hezekiah namp8ham, naumwog wame ne neekit ohtag, matta ne teag ut nunnompag8unnekomukqut, ne matta nóhtinóog.
39.5 Neit Isaiah unnau, Hezechiahoh, n8tash ukkutt8onk Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
39.6 Kusseh, kesukodtash peyom8ash, ne wame kekit ohtag, kah nish k8shog wadchanummóhetteupash pajeh yeu kesukok, pish uss8wuttauunash Babylon, matta pish teag ushqunnum8un wussin Jehovah.
39.7 Kah neg pish monchanaog kenaumonuh, neg sohhogig wutch kohhogkat, neg pish wânamoniéaneg, kah nag pish wuttinneumunneunk wekit Babylone ketass8t.
39.8 Neit Hezechiah unnau Isaiahoh, wunnegen ukkutt8onk Jehovah ne an8wáan: kah wonk n8wop, newutche wunohteaonk kah wanumuhkuteyeuuk ohteau ut nukkesukodtumut.
40.1 TAphéninongqutch, taphéninongqutch nummissinninneumog, n8wau kum-Manitt8m.
40.2 Tapheáe ken8nók Jerusalem, kah mishont8wánumók, ummattompagum wohkukquashin, ummatcheseonk ahquontamun: newutche attumunum wutch Jehovah wunnutcheganit, pápskeu wutch wame ummatcheseongash.
40.3 OOwadtauatonkqussuonk noh mashont8adt ut touohkomuk; quagquoshwehtam8k ummay Jehovah, sampwehteó8k ut touohkomuk ummay num-Manitt8mun.
40.4 Nishnoh 8nóuhkôi pish qunóhqutteauun, kah nishnoh wadchu, kah wadchuemes pish tiuhquohquttauunash, kah woonkagk pish sampweteauunash, kah machipsquehtuash pish m8siyeuash.
40.5 Kah wussohsumoonk Jehovah pish náhtúhkon, kah wame weyaus pish wunnaumuneau moayeu: newutche wutt8n Jehovah wussinnin.
40.6 Wadtauatonkqussuonk n8wop, Mishont8wash, Kah n8wau, Teagwe woh mishont8wai, wame weyaus moskehtu8, kah wame na$ut wanegik tatuppeyeu8 ohteuhkone uppeshaónut.
40.7 Maskeht ahp8hteau, uppeshau penusheau, newutche wunnashontamun Jehovah, wunnamuhkut missinninnúog moskehtu8og.
40.8 Moskeht ahp8hteau, uppeshau penusheau: qut wuttinn8waonk num-Manitt8mun pish michemohteau.
40.9 Woi Zion, noh wanonchimudt, kuhkuhquish en kussôhkôiyeue wadchuut: woi Jerusalem ken wanonchimwean, menuhke mishont8wash, mishont8wash, wabesehkon: utash Judáe keitotanash, moninneok kum-Manitt8mw8.
40.10 Kusseh, Lord Manit menuhku peyau, kah wuhpit nanawunnumwanshau: kusseh, wutonkquatunk weechayeumuk, kah wutanakausuonk ohteau anaquabit.
40.11 Pish sohkom8uneau uf-flockum onatuh nanaushepsaenin: noh pish mouneau lambsoh ut wuhpittenit, kah pish ukkeninuh ut upp8chenauónut, kah pish manunne sagkompanau wompeqúaunitcheh.
40.12 Howan quaquadh8k nippeash ut wunnutcheganit? kah quadompskinuk kesukquash nashpe wunnutcheg, kah miahtunk ohkee puppissai, ut quttuhhonganit, kah quadh8k wadchuash ut qutompagh8teganit, kah wadchuemesash quttompagh8teganit.
40.13 Howan kogáhtimont wunnashauanitt8moh Jehovah, asuh kogáhqutteamweneumwit ukkuhk8tomauuh.
40.14 Howaneh k8n8náhetteup, howan ukkuhk8tomauoh, kah ukkuhk8tomauoh wussittumóe may? kah ukkuhk8tomauoh wahteauonk kah wunnahtinuh wohwohtamwe may.
40.15 Kusseh, wutohtimoneash tatuppeyeu8ash pápenuppáshunk p8thonchuut, ogquanu[m]ukquss8og puppissiyeuwésit ut qutompagh8teganit: kusseh, nemunum ogquidnash onatuh ne teag peyasik.
40.16 Kah Lebanon matta wamuttinn8 chikohsumunat, kah puppinashimwog na apitcheg matta womattinn8 wutche chikohtae mag8onk.
40.17 Wáme wutohtimoneash ut anaquabit, onatuh matteagwuninu8g, kah náh wutogquanumoh anue peyasik onk ne mo teag, kah t[á]hn8che.
40.18 Neit Howan ogquanumôg Godut? asuh teagwe ogqueneunkqussuonk kutogqunneauau.
40.19 Anakausuen sabaswau nunneukontunkoh, kah Golde-Smith sepagenumauoh upputtoguhwaeu gold, kah wunnupasahdtoh silvere chainsash.
40.20 Noh machekit noh mat teag woh mag8k, pepenam mehtug, ne woh mo anittinn8g: natinnewhau nehtoou anakausuenuñeu ukquoshauehtauonat nunneukontungoh, ne matta woh ontapegk.
40.21 Sunnummatta k8wahteauomw8? sunnummatta ken8tam8m8? sunnummatta kuttitteaunaous, waj kutchissik? sunnummatta k8wohtamm8unnaous wutch quenohtagish muttaok?
40.22 Noh quenapit petukqui ohkeit, kah neg na wadohkitcheg tatuppeyeu8og chansompsit, noh agque sepagunuk kesuk onkwheganit, kah wutogque sepagunumunash weetu ne weetimuk.
40.23 Noh mat toh antuppehheunk sontimosoh: tahn8cheáheau ohkee wussittum8eneuh.
40.24 Nux nag pish matta ohkéhteaununk, nux matta pish seahwhoog, nux 8weepuhtugk8 matta pish wadchabukkinn8 ut ohkeit, kah noh pish wonk upp8tomuh, kah nag pish upp8suog, kah pemsquoh pish wutogque amaunuh sequkkepaneganit.
40.25 Neit hówan tatupanumeóg, asuh neanèyeue n8wau wunneetupantamwéyeuit?
40.26 Tahshinum8k qunuhqueu kuskesuk88ash, kah kuhkinneam8k howan noh yeush kahkénauwéhteunk, noh kuhkénaue sohh8wunont wutayeuwehteomoh: wame 8wesuongane missahwhoh, nashpe mohsag ummenuhkesuonk, newutche noh menuhkesu, matta pasuk quenauwadtinn8.
40.27 Tohwutch n8waan, woi Jakob, kah missohhaman, woi Israel, nummay adtahtôsu wutch Lordut, kah n8sumitteáonk paumushóm8 wutch num-Manitt8mut?
40.28 Sun matta k8wahteo8h, sun matta ken8tam8mus machemappue Manit Jehovah noh kezteunk weekqshinne ohke, matta kodtinneó8 asuh sauunnum8? matta howan woh wohkuhquónam8 noh 8wohwohtam8onk.
40.29 Noh ummenuhkesuáheau kôdtinneánitcheh, kah neh mat mánuhkesénitcheh nano ummenuhkeheuh.
40.30 Wuskenúog pish kodtinneaog kah sauunumwog, kah nunkompaog pish pápukquanne penushaog.
40.31 Qut neg pahtussuóunoncheg Jehovah pish wuskehteauog ummenuhkesuongan8: pish ogque ushpushaog wompussikukquaut nashpe wunnuppuhwhunoh; nag pish quogqueog kah matta sauunum8og, nag pish pomushaog, kah mat kodtinneau8og.
41.1 CHequnapek ut anaquabeh, woi munóhhanog, kah missinninnúog wuskehteauwehettich ummenuhkesuongan8: pas8tsháhettich kah ket8káhettich: moae peyontuh ut wussittum8onganit.
41.2 Howan omohkinont sampweusseaénúh wutch wutchepwóiyeu, weekomont en wusseetut, áninnumauont wutohtimoneash ut anaquabenit, kah nanawunnumwáheont ta[h]s8tamwoh? wutogque áninnumauoh wuttogkodteg puppissiyuut, kah wutohtompeh onatuh t8annóhhanne sequkkepaneg.
41.3 Nah wunn8swuttahwhóh, wunohteae paumwushau en may$ut ne matta wusseetue paumushog.
41.4 Howan ne ásit kah kezteunk, wehquetuk pometeongash wutch waj kutchissik? nen Jehovah, negonne, kah weeche maumachish, nen n$noh.
41.5 Munnohhanash wunnaumuneau, kah wabesuog, wekqshinne ohkeash wabesum8ash, pas8tsháog, kah peyaog.
41.6 Nishnoh pasuk [à]ninnumauau weetatteamungoh, kah nishnoh pasuk unnau weematoh wunne wutt8antash.
41.7 Neit wunnágittôhôsuénin wutt8anatamheau gold-smithoh, kah noh m8sitteunk nashpe hammer, kah noh togkodtog anvil, n8waog, pakodche kesompskutteau, kah ukkeneepunun nashpe kenontugwhegash, onk woh matta ontohtano.
41.8 Qut ken Israel, ken nuttinninneum, Jakob noh pepenauog, 8skannem Abram netomp.
41.9 Ken noh pepenauog wutch wehshik ohke, kah k8wehkomush wutch kenugke mogkouwáut, kah kuttinnunup, ken nuttinninneum, kuppepenaush, kah mattà kuppogkénun8h.
41.10 Wabesehkon, newutche k8wetomsh, chepshuhkon, newutche nen kum-Manitt8m: kummenuhkehesh: nux kutáninnumoush, n[ù]x nashpe nussampwée nuttinnuhkounne sampweusseonk kukkogkôunush.
41.11 Kusseh, wame nag m8m8qhikqueáneg pish akodchuog kah chepshaog, pish monteagk88og, kah neg mekonukqueaneg pish onkapunaog.
41.12 Nag pish kénátinneahwhòog, & matta pish kenamheoog, neg mekônukqueaneg, neg mátompaguhkónukqueaneg, pish monteagk88og, kah mat tohhentuppayeu8og.
41.13 Newutche nen Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, nukkinninum kuttinohkôu, kuttinnush, wabesehkon, kutanninnumoush.
41.14 Wabesehkon ken ask8kse J[o]kob, kah kenaau Israelle wosketomp[a]og kuttanninnumoush, n8wau Jehovah, kah kuppohquohwussuaéneum, OOneetupanatam8moh Israel.
41.15 Kusseh kuttayimoush wuske pogguhham8e weepittum8e auwohteaonk: pish k[u]ppogham wadchuash, kah kussukquttahhamunash, kah pish kuttogqueteoh wadchuash wussadteamunit:
41.16 Pish kuppáuanóntamunash, kah waban pish ummonchadtauunash, kah pemsquoh pish wusseáhhamunash: kah ken pish k8woweenoam ut 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
41.17 Mach[ee]k[u] kah qu[é]nahukquit natinnehog nippe, kah na monteagwuninno, kah weenan8 kohkutt8n8e sauunum8m8, nen Lord pish nag nunn8tauoog nen um-Manitt8moh Israel matta nunnukonóog.
41.18 N8wôshwunum sepuash ut qunuhqui ayeuonganit, kah tohkekomm[ú]ash ut nôeu 8nóuhkôiyeuut, nupseeu nuppéhteau touohkomuk, kah nu[n]bobohteai nuttohkekomuúhteam.
41.19 Nutohketeam chikkuppog ut touohkomukqut, Shittahuhtug, kah Mirtluhtug, kah pummeeuhtug, kah ut touushinne ohkeit nutohketeam firruhtug, kah pineuhtug, kah boxuhtug moeu.
41.20 Onk woh nag naumwog, kah wahteauog kah natwontamwog, kah wohtamwog moaeu, wunnutcheg Jehovah yue ussem8, kah 8neetupanatam8moh Israel ukkezteauun.
41.21 Pas8che paduto8k kuppissaumatuonk n8wau Lord, s8h8wuttau8k kummenuhke unnaumaiyeum8ash, n8wau ukketass8tam8moh Jakob.
41.22 Sohh8wuttauwéhettich, kah nahtinnukqutteuh toh pish ônagk: natitteahettich mahche nnagish, uttoh ônagk, onk woh nunnatwontamunánonash, kah woh n8wahteomun adt wohkukquoshik, asuh wahteauwahinnean toh pish ônagk.
41.23 Nahtitteagk nish pish ompetak ônagish, onk woh n8wahteomun, kum-Manitt88mw8: nux wunnesek ash matchesek onk woh nutchepshomun, kah woh moéu naumunan.
41.24 Kusseh, matta toh kuttin tuppéayeu8mw8, kah kutanakausuongan8 matteagwunninn8: noh jishánumukqussu noh pepenunkqueóg.
41.25 Nutomuhkin pasuk wutch nanumaiyeu, kah noh pish peyau: waj pashpishont pish wehquetum n8wesuonk, kah pish ogque nuhkuhkauau sontimoh, man8nskut, onatuh ahkuhqutteaenin tahtashkuhkauont man8nskoh.
41.26 Howan wahteauwáhu[a]dt waj kutchissik, onk woh n8wahteauunan? kah nish asquam ahquompan8g; onk woh nussimun noh sampweusseaenú8? qut matta howan wunnahtitteauunash, qut matta howan 8wahteauwahuwáunash, nux matta howan n8tam8 kukkutt8wongan88ash.
41.27 Negonnu pish unnau Zion, kusseh, nag naau, kah nuttinninnumau Jerusalem neh wanaunchumwunutcheh.
41.28 Newutch nummoninneam, kah na matta wosketompaun8, ut kenugke nagoh, kah na matta kogohqutteamwenuunn8, noh woh namp8hamiit pasuk kutt8onk, nat8tomauog.
41.29 Kusseh nag wame tahn8cheyeu8og, wutanakausuongan88ash matteagwunun8ash: nag wussabassumwe nunnekontunkan8oh waban[n]u8oh, kah naswaiyeu8oh:
42.1 Nók nuttinneum noh kónunog, noh pepenauog, nukketeahogkou womononcheh, nupponamau nunnashauanitt8moh, noh pish sohh8wuttauau wussittumoonk Gentilsuh.
42.2 Matta pish mishont8woou, asuh tháhshinnum8 asuh n8tamwahuwoou 8wadtauatonkqussuonk ut maikontu.
42.3 Sukqutchoshae wekinasq mâtta uppohquanum8un k[á]h pukuttae hashábpoh matta wutontahwhoh, pish sohh8wuttáu wussittum8onk en wunnamuhkuteyeuut.
42.4 Matta pish sauunum8, asuh paunompasu noh pajeh upponamunat wussittumoonk ut ohkeit, kah munnohhanash pish pahtsuwontamog wuttinnaumatuonk.
42.5 Yeu wussin Manit Jehovah, noh kahkenauwehteunk kesukquash, & noh sepaginuk, noh mashegskehteunk ohke, kah ne noh waj sohham8m88k, noh nashauwaheont missinninnuh na$ut, kah nashauanitt8heont neh ne paumushanitcheh.
42.6 Nen Jehovah k8wehkomush ut sampweusseonganit, kah pish nukkenunnum kenutcheg, kah pish kenananunush, kah pish kuttinninnumoush wutche 8n8waongan8 missinninnuog, wutche 8wequaiyeum8 gentilsog.
42.7 Woshwunnumunat pogkenumwae muskesukquash sohh8wunonat kobshagkinitcheg wutch kubshagkinnittuonganit, kah neg apitcheg pohkenaiyeuut, wutch kuppishagkinnittuae kommukqut.
42.8 Nen Jehovah, ne n8wesuonk, kah nussohsumoonk matta nuttinnumauoun onkatuk, kah matta n8woweenomuwaonk nunneukontunganog.
42.9 Kusseh, negonae ônagish nnihyeuash, kah wuske teagwasinish n8wahteauwáhuwam; asquam sasonkunun8gkup, kuttinunnanaôash.
42.10 Unn8hamok Jehovah wuske unn8homáonk; kah woweenomaonk wutch wehqshik ohke, kenaau w8mséogish en kehtahhanit, kah wame ne noh ohtag, munnohkanash, kah neg na wadohkitcheg.
42.11 Touohkomuk kah 8tanash naut, mishont8wáhettich, otanamesash nish Kedar wadohkitchish: wadohkitcheg qussukquanit ket8hamahettich, mishont8wahettich wutch kussôhkôiyeue wadchuut.
42.12 Sohsumm8wounáhettich Jehovah, kah wahteauwaheáhettich waweenomaonk munnáhhunoh.
42.13 Jehovah pish ogque sohham menuhkesuenûut, pish wogkowunum m8sitteam8onk, onatuh mattompagwehteaénin: pish mishont8wau, nux onkquont8wau, pish sohkauau ummatwomoh.
42.14 Nussepe chequnap, nummanunap, nukquihtin nuhhog: eyeu nutogque mishont8wam neechae mittamwussissut, pish nuppagwohteam nummishashquinneunk pasukqut.
42.15 Nummáhchumwéhtoh wadchuash kah wadchuemesash, kah nunnunassum wame weherbsum8ash, kah sepuash nummenúhhann8team, kah nunnunassum nuppissepagwash.
42.16 Kah pogkenumwog nuppas8 mayut ne matta wahteauhetteg, nutuss8unóog maikontu ne matta wahteauhetteg: pohkenai n8wequaiyeuhteam ut nag anaquabhettit, kah woonkagish nussampweteauunash, yeush nuttinheonaoash, kah matta nutohquanumóog.
42.17 Nag pish qushkeog, pish mishe akodchuog, pabuhtanumoncheg nunneukontunkoh, neg anoncheg sabassume nunneukontunkoh kenaau num-Manitt8munónog.
42.18 N8tam8k kenaau kôkobsóogish, kah natauwompek kenaau pogkenumógish, onk woh kenaumw8.
42.19 Howan pogkenuk webe nuttinninneum? asuh kôkohsont qut nutann8naeneum noh an8nog? howan pogkenuk neane noh pannuppeyeuit, kah pogkenuk neane wuttinneumoh Jehovah?
42.20 Nauman monatash qut matta kukkehkinneasséinash: wôhshinnuman mehtauogash, qut matta n8tam8.
42.21 Lord tapeneam wutche 8nomwausseonk, pish mishehteau naumatuonk, kah ukquhtiánittamutteauun.
42.22 Qut yeug missinninnuog mukk8kinaog kah matcheheóog, wame puttahwh[ô]og ut wonogquehtu, kah adtashôog ut kuppishaginnitteae kommukqut: nag másompanitcheg, kah matta howan uppohquohwhunoh nag mukk8kinôog, kah wanne howan n8wau ompontin8k.
42.23 Howan ut kenugke kenaau, yeu n8tog? howan ahchuwussittog kah n8tog wutche ompetak?
42.24 Howan anumauont Jakoboh wutche matchehtóonk, kah Israeloh chechequnnuaenúh? sun matta Lord, noh matcheneheogkut? newutche nag cheketamwog pomushonat ummayut, kah matta noswehtamwog wuttinnaumatuonk.
42.25 Newaj sokenumauont ummishe musquantam8onk, kah menuhkesue ayeuwuttuonk: kah wéenohtauoh n8teau, qut onch matta wahteauun, kah wutchikoswoh, qut matta upponam8un ut wuttahhut.
43.1 QUt yeuyeu, yeu wussin Jehovah noh kezhikquean, woi Jakob, kah noh kakénauáhikquean, woi Israel, wabesehkon: newutche kummanóuwhush, k8wesuongane missohwhush, ken nuttaihe.
43.2 Pannupwusháan nippéash, k8weetomsh, kah qushkodteaan sepuash nish matta pish kenehtipánuk8unash: pannupwushaan n8teau, matta pish kutchikkussu, kah n8n8uneau matta pish kenashqussuk8un.
43.3 Newutche nen Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, 8neetupanatam8moh Israel kuppohquohwussuaéneum: nummagup Egypt wutch kumman8whun8onk, Ethiopia kah Sheba wutche ken.
43.4 Nádteoh máshoadtean ut anaquabeh, kukquhtiánumukqus[si]p, kah k8womonsh, newaj mag8 wosketompaog wutche ken, kah missinninnuog wutche kuppomantam8onk.
43.5 Wabesehkon, newutche k8weetomsh: pish nuppas8 k8skannemunneog wutch wutchepwôou, kah kummohmóunush wutch wutcheksuiyeu.
43.6 Pish nuttin nanumit, magush, kah sowanish assaéhkon, pas8k nunnaumonunk wutch noadtit, kah nuttaunog wutch wehqshik ohke.
43.7 Nish$noh pasuk noh as8wesit n8wesuonk: newutche nukkezeh wutche nussohsumóonk, nukkehkenauéhheop, nukkezheop.
43.8 Sohh8wunok pôgkenukeg missinninnuog wuskesukqutcheg, kah k[ó]kobsonch$eg wohtauogkutcheg.
43.9 Wame wutohtimoneash miyaém8utch, kah missinninnuog móappéhettich: howan kenugke nagoh woh yeu wahteauwáhuadt, kah nahtinukqueog negonne anágkupash? sohh8wunáhettich 8wauwáeneum8oh, onk woh sampweógquanumóog, kah n8tamohettich, kah n8wahettich, wunnamuhkuteyeu8.
43.10 Kenaau n8wauwaeneumog wussin Jehovah, kah nuttinninneum noh pepenauog: onk woh k8wahteomw8 kah woh k8namptiimw8, kah woh k8wohtamumw8, noh nen: negonne onk nen matta Manittoun8, kah matta pish wonk asuhkaue onk nen.
43.11 Nen, nen Jehovah, kah matta wonk howan wadchanuwaenu8, webe nen.
43.12 N8wahteauwahuap, kah wadchanuap, kah nunnáhtitteap na matta penowe manitt8un8g ut kenugke kenaau: newutche kenaau n8wauwaeneumog n8wau Jehovah, nen Manitto.
43.13 Nux, asquam kesukodtin8g, nen n$noh, kah matta woh howan pohquohwussuóou wutch nunnutcheganit: pish nutanakaus, kah howan woh 8tamehtauun?
43.14 Yeu wussin Jehovah kum$Mano[u]huwaeneum8, 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, wutche kenaau, nutann8hteam en Babilon, kah nuttiuhkongqueh wame wussontimom8uh, kah Caldeansog, neg ummauongan8 ohtag kuht8nugquehtu.
43.15 Nen Jehovah k8neetupanatam8m8, kezkukqutche Israel, kukketass8tam8m8.
43.16 Yeu wussin Jehovah, noh ayik may ut kehtahhannit, kah may mishe nippekontu.
43.17 Sohh8wuttunk charit kah horse, kah menuhkesue kenauwameonk: nag pish mo[á]e sepsinwog, nag matta pish omohkeog: nag ontohwhoog, ogque wuhkohshanoog hashabput.
43.18 Méhquontam8hteok negonne anagkupush, kah natwontam8hteok noadt anagkupash.
43.19 Kusseh, n8skeu ussem: eyeu pish sonkun, sun matta pish k8wahte[u]uneau? nummayehteam touóhkomukqut, kah nussepuehteam touushinne ohkeit.
43.20 Ohteuhkônee puppinashimwog pish nukquehtianumukquog, Dragonsog, kah kuhk8khosog, newutche nummag nippe ut touohkomukqut, kah sepuash ut touushinne ohkéit, n8tattamheonat nummissinninnuog pepenauogig.
43.21 Yeug missinninnuog nukkuhkenauehteauonuh nuhhog, nag pish nahtitteaóg n8woweenomitteaonk.
43.22 Qut matta k8wehquetumiyeuh woi Jakob, qut kussauanumeh woi Israel.
43.23 Chiko[h]tae kummag8e puppinashimwog matta kuppaudtiyeuh, kah matta kenashpe quttiánumyeuh kussephausuongash: matta k8tinninneumuhkônuwahiñ8 nashpe mag8onk, kah matta kussauanunóh nashpe incense.
43.24 Matta kutteagwu kuttaphumwanshu weetemungque wekinask, kah matta k8wamepwuhheuh k8nogk8e sephausuongash, qut k8tinninneumuhkausuwáheh nashpe kummatcheseongash, kussau[u]neh nashpe kummatcheseongash.
43.25 Nen, nen noh jishkhog kuppanneseseongash wutche nen nehenwon[c]he, kah matta nummehquontam8h kummatcheseongash.
43.26 Mehquontamwaheh, ken8tamwanshittitteuh: wahteauwahuash, onk woh kussampweogquanumit.
43.27 Negonne k8sh matcheseup: & kukkuhk8tomwehtamog nuppannesehtunkquog.
43.28 Newaj matchetupanatamwaheog peantamwaekomukque sontimóog, kah nummag Jakob én matánumónat, kah Israel en kekontinneat.
44.1 QUt onch yeuyeu n8tash woi Jakob, nuttinninneum, kah ISrael noh pepenauog.
44.2 Yeu wussin Jehoah noh kezhukquean, kah kahkenauwéhikquean wutch ôontomukqut, noh aninnumunkquean: wabesehkon woi Jakob nuttinninneum: kah ken Jesurun noh pepenauogkup.
44.3 Newutch nussokanumau nippe noh kohkutt8g, kah tomogkonash ut nobohteaiyeuut: nussokun nunnashauanitt8m k8skannemunit, kah n8nanitteaonk ut kutontseonganit.
44.4 Kah nag pish ogque sontuog ut kenugke moskehtekontu, onatuh anumwussukuppeit ut kishke nippekontu.
44.5 Pasuk pish n8wau n8chi Jehovah, kah onkatuk pish ussowenau wuhhogkuh 8wesuonk Jakob: kah onkatog pish wussukwhosuohtu nashpe wunnutcheg en Jehovahut, kah nahohtoeu 8wesuonganeh[e]au Israeloh.
44.6 Yeu wussin Jehovah Israelle ketass8t, kah ummanouhuaeneumoh, Jehovah ayeuteaunit, Nen negonáe, k[á]h nen maumachish, kah chonchippe nen wanne Manitt8un8.
44.7 Kah howan neane nen, pish wehqutteamwit, kah pish 8wahteauwahuon, kah pish n8nohtonkqun, náiteuh kahtimog nukkône missinninnuog? kah nish paóm8gish, kah pish peyom8ash? nah nohtin[á]hettich.
44.8 Wabesehteok kah chepshonteog, sunnummatta kuttinn8n[á]s nâ wutch ahquompag, kah n8wahteauwahuwon[á]h? kenaau n8wauwaeneumog, sun wonk Manitto8 chonchippe nen? nux na matta Manitt8un8, matta pasuk n8waheoh.
44.9 Neg ayeuoncheg nunneukontungoh, wame neg tahn8cheyeu8og, kah ukkodtantamukóm8ash matta pish 8chienáoash, kah nag nehenwonche 8wauwóm8oh, nag mat naumóog, kah matta wahteáu8og, onk woh akodchuog.
44.10 Howan káhkenauweheont manitto, kah sabaswont nunneukontunkoh, ne matta tohhentupán8g?
44.11 Kusseh wame weetomukqutcheh pish akodchuoh: kah anakausuenuog, neg wosketompo8og, wame miyaehettich, kah neepauwehettich: nag pish wabesuog, pish moeu akodchuog.
44.12 Smith nashpe wuttongsumash naneeswe, wutayimun nashpe mohkohsaash, kah kehkenauwehtin nashpe hamer, kah nashpe wuhpitte[n]ue menuhkesuonk wutayimun: nux kodtupp8, kah sa[u]unum, matta wuttattam8 nippe kah sauunum.
44.13 Wunnagkittuhhausuenin sampwompanum ukkehkinneasuonk ukkuhkhamun nashpe pemuneat: 8nteouun nashpe upplainsumash kah ukkuhkhamun nashpe ukompasash, kah wutogquehteauun wosketompaut, neaunak wosketompae wunneetuonk, onk woh ohteau wetuomut.
44.14 Wannagittahwau chikkupoh, kah nemunnum cypressuhtug, kah n8timis, ne sampwuttahhamont, ut kenugke touohkomukque metugquekontu, ohkehteau monunkqsoh, kah sokanon wunnekheuh.
44.15 Neit pish ponamon: newutche na 8tinnumun, kah pish auwossu, nux wunnashqunánumun, kah apwau petukqunneg, nux, ayeuau manitto kah wowussumoh: ayeuau nunneukontunkoh, kah wunnauwaéhtauoh.
44.16 Nawhutche chikohsum n8taut, nashpe nawhutche meechu weyaus: app8sue app8su, kah wamep8h, nux, ouwassu, kah n8wau, kah nutáuwas, nunnaum n8teau.
44.17 Kah nawhutche um-manitt8hkon, wuttinneuhkontunkoh[;] wunnauwaéhtauoh, kah 8wowussumoh; peantamauoh kah n8wau, pohquohwusseh, newutche ken num-manitt8m.
44.18 Matta wahteau8og asuh wohtamwog: newutch yânunum wuskesukquash, nag matta woh naumoog, kah wuttah8oash, matta woh wohtam8mun8ash.
44.19 Kah mtta howan natwontam8 ut wuttahhut, kah matta wohwohtamóonk asuh wahteauonk ohteau n8wonat, nawhutche nutchikohsumun n8taut, nux wonk nuttittanapwon petukquinunk ut mukossáhtu, nutapwam weyaus kah nummechin, kah nawhutche woh nutayimun onkquontam8onk? sun woh nunnauwaéhtam mehtug.
44.20 Mechu pukquee: as8kekodteamwe metah wutamaunukqun, matta woh pohquohwhunóou ukketeahogkôunoh, asuh n8wóou, sunnummatta pann8waonganinn8 nuttinohkôunit?
44.21 Yeush mehquontash, (woi Jakob kah Israel) newutche ken nuttinninneum: kukkuhkenauwéhinup: ken nutinninneum, woi Israel, matta pish k8wanánumun8h.
44.22 Nutjiskham kummatcheseongash onátuh kuhpogki matokqsit, kah onatuh ongquohqut kuppanneseongásh, qushkek en nuhhogkat, newutche kuppohquohwhunush.
44.23 Ket8ham8k, woi kesukquog, newutche Jehovah ummahche ussen: mishont8wagk agwe ohkekontu: kuss8homunk, woi wadchuash, woi touohkomuk, kah nishnoh metug na ohtag, newutche Jehovah pohquohwhunau Jakoboh, kah sohsumwaheau wuhhogkuh ut Israelut.
44.24 Yeu wussin Jehovah kummanouhuwaéneum, kah noh kahkenauwéhikquean wutch ôontomukqut, nen Jehovah noh ayik wame teanteaquassinish, noh nahse sepákinuk kesuk noh sepagenuk ohke, nusse[u]:
44.25 Noh mat toh ken tuppehteo8k ukkehkinneasuongan8 pann8waenuog: kah kogkeaheont pauwauwoh, noh quoshkeaheont waantamwoh, kah mattammagwutteunk 8wahteauongan8.
44.26 Nóh manuhkehteunk wuttinn8waonk wuttinnúmoh, kah asit ukkuhqutteam8ongan8 wutann8naéneumoh, noh anont Jerusalem, ken pish wutohtuonk Judae keitotanash pish kutayeuwutteamw8, kah nuttahshinum mahchum8e ayeuongash.
44.27 Noh anont m8naiyeuoh, nunnappesish kah pish nunnunassum kussepeumash.
44.28 Noh anont papaume Cyrus, noh nunnanau shepsueneum kah pish pakodche ussen, wame nukkodtantamoonk, anont Jerusalem pish kutayeuit, kah Templeut, kukquenohtagom pish wunnushitteáuun.
45.1 YEu wuttinnon Jehovah Cyruṣoh sasequnoncheh; wuttinohkou nuttinnumau sohkomunat wutohtimoneash ut anaquabit: kah nutompinim wussegan8ash tahs8tamwog, wohshinumunat ut anaquabit neesikkuphouune squontamash, kah sqúontamash matta pish kuphôsin8ash.
45.2 Kenegonuhkouush, kah nussámpweteoh woonki ayeuongash, nussohquetahham wompohshogque squontamash, kàh nuppohshittahham moúhshogque pummetunkqshitteungash.
45.3 Káh kuttinnumoush pohkenae nompak8unash, kah adtahtoe w[é]nauwetuongash assampámukquehtu, onk woh k8wahteoh, nen Jehovah ne as8wenimuk, nen um-Manitt8moh Israel.
45.4 Newutche Jakob nuttinneum kah Israel pepenauog, kuttehenush: kuttohtoe wesuonganuhkoush, tohkonogque matta k8wahein.
45.5 Nen Jehovah kah matta onkatog, matta Manitt8un8h webe nen: kupputtugquabinuh tohkonogque mo k8wahein.
45.6 Onk wutch wutchepwoiyeu kah wutcheksuiyeu woh wahteauog, matta onkatog qut webe nen, nen Jehovah kah matta onkatok.
45.7 Nukkuhkenauwehteop wequai kah nukkezteop pohkenai: n8nohteahuam, kah matchit nukkezteoh: nen Jehovah wame yeush nutussenash.
45.8 Padtippashunk, kenaau kesukquog wutch waabe, kah kesukquash sokenumohettich sampweusseonk: ohke wóhshwem8utch, kah paudtauehettich wadchanittuonk kah sampweusseonk moae sonkitch: nen Jehovah nukkezteauunah.
45.9 Missi wutonkapunaonk noh mekonont kezhikqutcheh: kodchuhkishq mekontaj ohkee kodchuhkishq: sun woh man8nsk unnau neh kahkenauehhikqutcheh, teag kutayim? asuh kutanakausuonk, matta wunnutcheeu?
45.10 Missi wutonkapunaonk noh anont 8shoh teaguas k8naumoni? asuh mittamwussissoh, teaguas keneecham:
45.11 Yeu wussin Jeh[ó]vah 8neetupan[a]tam8moh Israel, kah kezhukqutch[é]h, nat8tomah papaume nish pish anagish, papaume nunnaumonuh, kah papaume nunnutchegane ánakausuonk, ann8negk.
45.12 Nutayimup ohke, kah nukkezheap wosketomp na$ut: nen nunnutcheg sepagunumup kesukquash kah wame ne kenauwameonk nutann8tamun.
45.13 Nutomohkinumauup ut wunnomwausseonganit, kah nussampweteoh wame ummayásh: noh pish ayim nukkeitotan, kah noh pish moncheaheau nummissinomon, matta unnoadtuut asuh onkquatunkanit, n8wau Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
45.14 Yeu wussin Jehovah, wutanakausuonk Egypté wutan[á]qushaongash Ethiopia kah Sabeansog, qunuhqussuenuog pish kuppeyaonukquog, kah kuttaiheog, nag pish kutassuhkungquog, kah nashpe chainsash, nag pish quṣhkodteaog: kah nag pish kenauwaehtunkquog, pish k8wehquetumunkquog, n8waog wunnamuhkut God kutapehtunk, kah matta onkatog, matta Manitt8[un]8.
45.15 Wunnamuhkut ken Manit padtogquean, woi Israelle Manit, wadchanuwaenin.
45.16 Nag pish akodchuog, kah nag wame wonk pish quehquenauanumoog, nag pish moaeu naswaiyeuog neg ayeuoncheg nunneukontunkoh.
45.17 Qut Israel pish wadchanau ut Jehovahut nashpe michemohtae wadchanittuonk, matta pish kutakodchu, asuh kukkuhquenauanum8h yeoyatche.
45.18 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah noh kezteunk kesukquash, God nagum nehenwonche noh kuhkenauwehteunkup ohke, kah kezteunkup, ummenuhkehteáuun, matta táhn8che ukkezteaúouun, wuttinuk|kezteauun wutohkineat, nen Jehovah kah matta onkatok.
45.19 Matta nukkeme eyin, ut pohkenaiyeue ayeuonkanit ohkéit: matta nuttinnoh 8skannemuneoh Jakob, tahn8che natinneahwhegk: nen Jehovah sampweusseonk nussim, n8wahteauwahuwam nish sampwagish.
45.20 Miyaek, kah peyunk moae pas8tshagk, kenau pohquohhamogish ut [vv]utohtimoneat nag matta wahteauunganaeog, neg wanohtunkig nunneukontungane mehtug, kah wowussumaog Manitto neh woh mo wadchanuwanegeh.
45.21 Unnok pas8tshan8k, nux miyae kogahq[ú]ttehettich: howan yeu wahteauwahuwon wutch n8wadt? sunnummatta nen Jehovah? kah na matta Manitt8un8 webe nen sampwu Manit, kah wadchanuwaenin, matta onkatuk webe nen.
45.22 Monunnéiegk, kah wadchanitteagk, wame kenaau wehqshit ohke, newutch[é] nen God, kah matta wonk howan.
45.23 Nutchad[c]h[e]keyeuwop nashpe nen, nuttinn8waonk sohham8m8 wutch nutt8nut ut sampweyeuong[a]nit kah matta pish qushkemun8ash, onk woh nish$noh mukkuttuk nunnauwaehtunk, kah nish$noh meenan pish nutchadchekeimuk.
45.24 Pish pásuk n8wau wunnamuhkut, ut Jehova[ú]t n8nomwausseonk, k[á]h nummenuhkesuonk ohteau: noh$ut pish wosketompáog peyoneau, k[a]h wame neg musq[ú]anumonch[e]g pish akod[c]huog.
45.25 Ut Jehovah$ut wame Israelle wuskannem pish sampweogquanittamun, kah pish waeenowaog.
46.1 BEL nauwaeu, Nebo nauwôsu, wuttinn[é]ukontunk[a]nouh woskeche puppinashimwut, ka[h] nee[t]asuut: k8weanunn8ash tuhkekomeechummuash, neg tuhkequane weanun sauunum8e puppinashimwut.
46.2 Nauwoseog, nauwaeog moaeu, matta pohquohwuttauoog weanun, qut nag nehenwonche missinohkonunk.
46.3 N8tiek woi Jakob week, k[à]h wame sequttahwhutcheg wekit Israel, neg konunutcheg wutch munnogkussit, kah tahshinutcheg wutch ôontomukqut.
46.4 Kah pajeh kukkehchiyeuunneaout, nen nnoh, kah pajeh wompoquonat kukkinnunnumw8: nukkezteop, kah kutashinnumw8 kah kukkinnunumw8, kah kuppohquohwhununumw8.
46.5 Howan kuttatupanumimw8, kah keananumimw8, kah kuttatupinomw8, onk woh nutogqueneunkqussin?
46.6 Mahtshadtoog Gold wutch munn8tadt kah quttompagh8teog silver ut quthompak8teganit, kah ann8naog gold$smithoh, kah um-Manitt8hkou, neg penushaog, kah wowussummuwaog.
46.7 Wuttahshinouh ut wuttugkeout, ukkenunnouh, upponouh ut wutayeuonganit, kah neepau: wutch wutayeuonganit matta pish ontappu: nux pasuk pish ummauunnitteauoh, qut matta woh wunnamp8hamunk8oh, kah matta 8wadchanuk8oh wutch 8tamehpunnaonganit.
46.8 Yeu mehquontam8k, kah nahtitteagk k8skeetompoongan8: wonk mehquontamwahuwagk, woi kenaau panneusséógish.
46.9 Mehquontam8k nish n8adt anagkupash, newutche nen God, kah matta onkatog, nen God, kah matta howan nean[é]yeuw8.
46.10 Wahteauwahuwáan wohkukquoshik waj kutchishik, kah wutch n8wadt, nish asquam anán8gish, an8waon, nukkogahk8waonk pish menuhkohteau, kah pish nutussen wame nean tapeneam.
46.11 N8wehkom mahchipp8áe psukses wutch wutchepwoiyeu, wosketomp noh kezteunk ne pakodtantam, wutch noadtit wutohtimóneat: nux nussinneap, kah wonk pish n[u]tussen, nuppogkodtantamunap, kah wonk nutussen.
46.12 N8tiek manuhkitteahô[ó]gish, nô8sukómógish wunn[o]mw[a]usseonk.
46.13 Nuppas8chewuttoh n8nomwausseonk: matta pish nôadtit ahtano, kah n8wadchanuwaonk matta pish pahtsúmun8, kah n8nohto wadchanittuonk ut Zion wutche Israel nussohsumoonk.
47.1 NOOkish kah apsh puppissiyeuut: woi penomp Babilone wuttaunin, apsh ohkeit: wanne t[a]hs8tamoe appuonganinno woi Caldeanse wuttaunin: newutche matta pish wonk kuttéhennitteoh kehkéchumwit kah mam[a]ttanumwit.
47.2 Nemunush toguhwóngan[ó]mp[u]sk, kah n8khikanehteaush, wohshinush kummeesunk, poskis kuhkont, poskinush kehquau, qushkodteash seipu[a]sh.
47.3 Kukkôussuonk pish wohshwohteau, nux kutakodchuonk pish naumun, kuttann8toush, matta kutogque nogkuṣhauun8 wosketompaut.
47.4 Numman8whunnuaéneum, Jehovah ut ayeuteaunit, ne 8wesuonk, 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
47.5 Chequnapsh, âush pohkenaiyeuut, woi Caldeanse wutta[u]nin: newutche matta pish wonk kutehennitteoh, ass8tam8e sonksq
47.6 Numm8squanum nummissinninnúmog? nunnishketeoh nutohtoonk, kah neg nummagununk en kenutcheganit: matta kummonanumoog, ut kutchisetu tuhkéque yoak kuppon.
47.7 Kah kussip, pish nummicheme sonksquau: newaj matta yeush ponam8an kuttahhut, kah matta kummehquontamoh ogkomáe ônag.
47.8 Newutche yeu n8tash n8sukog weekontam8ongash, kah mat toh hentupánatamwée ayig: kussim ut kuttahhut, nen, kah matta howan w[e]be nen, matta pish nussekousquaappu, kah matta pish n8wahteo8h wannehteaonk mukkiesog.
47.9 Qut yeush nesinash pish kénuppe kuppeyogqunash, pasuk kesukod: wanneheaonk mukkiog, kah sekousquaonk: nish pish papannuppe kenuhkuhkongqunash, wutche mataanukish kuppauwauongash, kah wutche kumm8cheke moneetue usseongash.
47.10 Newutche kuppabuhtantam kummatcheseonk, kussip, matta howan nunnogk8, k8waantam8onk kah k8wahteauonk k8wounkhik, kah kussip, ut kuttahhut, nen, kah matt[a] onkatuk webe nen.
47.11 Newaj machuk nuhkuhkongquean, mata pish k8wahteoh uttoh waj tahsheem8uk: kah woskeetuonk pish kenuhkuhkunk, kah matta pish kuttapenum8un kutamaunumunat: kah touushin tean[ú]k pish kenuhkuhkunk, ne matta pish wahteauouan,
47.12 Eyeu nepaush nashpe kuppauwa[u]ongash, kah mataane[k] kummonetuonk, uttoh adt anakausean wutch k8ske[m]unneat, tapenuman kah so[h]koman.
47.13 Kussauunum nashpe mataanukish kukkog[a]hquttuongash: Astrologersog, wauwacheg ut anogqsut, kah nepauzsae mashogig, neepauwehettich, kah nag wadchanuk8k wutch yeush pish nuhkuhkongqueogish.
47.14 Kusseh, neg pish tatuppeyeu8og sequekepuneganit: n8teau pish nah wutchikohsoh, nag matta pish pohquohwhunau8og wuhhogkauh wutch menuhke n8n8naut: na matta mohkussaun8 kutauwossinneat, asuh n8tau apinneat anaquohtag.
47.15 Yeu pish wuttatuppeyeuunneau, neg weetanakausumacheg, kutanaqu[s]haeneumog wutch k8skenuuneat, nag pish nanwiyeuog nish$noh pasuk ut wutayeuonganit, matta howan pish k8wadchanuk8h.
48.1 YEU n8tam8k woi Jakob wek, neg ahenutcheg 8wesuonk Israel, kah neg wutch sohhogig Judae nippekontu, neg chadchekeyeuwacheg nashpe 8wesuonk Jehovah, kah mâs[a]whoncheg 8wesuonk um-Manitt8moh Israel, qut matta wunnamuhkuteyeuut asuh sampwesuonganit.
48.2 Newutche nag hennaog wuhhogkauh wutch wunnetupanatamwe otanat, kah quensinwog um-Manitt8moh Israel, Jehovah ayeuteanit ne 8wesuonk.
48.3 N8wahteauwahuwam négonne ânagish wutch waj|kutchissik, kah yeush sohham8m8ash wutch nutt8nut, kah nish nunnahtukonash: nukkenuppe ussenash, kah n$niyeupash.
48.4 Newutche n8wahteop kussiogkus, kah kussittipuk moohshog kutchoht, kah kushkodtuk wompohshag.
48.5 Waj kutchissik k8wahteauwahunun, asquam anan8g, kenahtinununah: ishkont woh kussim, nuttinneukontunk yeu wutussen, kah nukkogkoksumwe kah sabassumwe nunnúkontunk, nah wutann8nuh
48.6 Ken8tamup, wame yeu, naish, kah sunnummatta k8wahteauwahuaneau? kenahtinush wuske teagwahsinish yeu$wutch, adtuhtosikish kah matta k8wahteau8unapash.
48.7 Nish yeuyeu kezteauunash, qut matta waj kutchissik negonae kesukod asquam n8tam8an ishkont woh kussim, kusseh nish n8wahteauunash,
48.8 Nux, matta ken8tam8, nux, matta k8wahteou, nux wutch na ahquompag kehtauog matta wohshinum8muk: newutch n8wahteoh, woh ahche k8nass8muwae ussem, & kuttehenit panneseaenin wutch ôontomukqut.
48.9 Wutche n8wesuonk nutassanumun nummusquantamoonk: kah wutch n8woweenomitteaonk, kummukk8naush, ishkont kuttummeswush.
48.10 Kusseh, kuppahkhesh, qut matt[a] nashpe silver, kuppepe[n]aush ut sabassumwe onkapunnaonganit.
48.11 Wutche nen nehenwonche, nux wutche nen nehenwonche pish nutussen: newutche u[t]toh woh n8wesuonk nishketeauun? kah m[á]tta howan nuttinnumauoh nussohsumoonk.
48.12 N8tah woi Jakob, kah Israel n8wehkumog: nen n$noh nen negonne, nen wonk maumachish.
48.13 Nunnutcheg wonk wunohtau quenohtag ohke, kah nuttinnohkou qutomskinnau kesukquash; nag wehkumog moae neepoog
48.14 Wame kenaau moegk kah n8tam8k, howan kenugke nagoh yeush wahteauwáhuwachish? Jehovah 8womonuh: pish ussu wuttenantam8onk ut Babilon, kah wuhpit pish nuhkuhkauau Caldeansoh.
48.15 Nen nen Nussin, nux n8wehkom: nuppas8, kah pish wutchayeuhteau ummay.
48.16 Pas8sukiek, yeu n8tam8k, matta nukkeme eyin wutch waj|kutchissik, wutch na ahquompak ne ânag, na nen, kah eyeu Lord Jehovah, kah wunnashauanitt8moh nutann8nuk.
48.17 Yeu wussin Jehovah kummanouhuwaeneum, 8neetupanatam8moh Isra[a]l, nen Jehovah kum$Manitt8m, noh kohk8tomungquean k8chiinneat, noh sagkompagunukquean en mayut ut$toh woh aóan.
48.18 Woi n8tamas nutann8team8ongash! neit k8nohteaonk woh tatuppeyeu8 sepuut, kah k8nomwausseonk onatuh ketahhanne tukk8ut.
48.19 K8skannemuneunk wonk woh tatuppeyeu8og naguntu; kah k8nogkusseeu ontseonk onatuhyeu8 mamossompsquehtu: 8wesuonk woh matta tummussum8un, asuh pagwotoouun wutch anaquabeh.
48.20 Sohham8k Babilon: wussem8k wutch Caldeansog nashpe ket8homae wadtautaonkqussuonk, wahteauwahuwak, yeu n8wak, unn8wak adt wehqshit ohken8wagk Jehovah man8whau wuttinnumoh Jakoboh.
48.21 Kah nag matta kuhkutt8n8og pamuwunont touohkomukquash: wussohwhutchuw[a]nehkauoh nippe wutch qussukquanit, pasehtham wonk qussuk, kah nippe sohwhutchuan.
48.22 Na matta wunohteaonganinn8, n8wau Jehovah, matcheetunutcheh.
49.1 KUhkehtiegk woi munnáhannog, kah n8tiek woi missinninnuog wutch n8adtut, Jehovah n8wehkomuk wutch ôontomukqut, wutch wunnogkussit nokas missohham n8wesuonk.
49.2 Kah ogquehteau nutt8n kenu togkodteg, ut wunnuppawhunne onkóohtómut nutadtahshik, kah nutayimunk kussenausue kôuhquod: ut uppetauwónut nutadtahshik.
49.3 Kah nuttinuk, ken nuttinninneum woi Israel, ut kuhhogkat sohsumm8w[ô]nit.
49.4 Neit nussip, tahn8tanakausip, nummohtshadtoh nummenuhkesuonk wutche monteag, kah tahn8che, wunnamuhkut n8sumitteaonk ohteau ut Jehovah, kah nutanakausuonk weechayeumukqun num-Manitt8m.
49.5 Kah eyeu, n8wau Jehovah noh kahkénauwéhit wutch ôontomukqut 8tinninnúmuneat, wonk uppaudtauónat Jakoboh: tókónogque Israel matta môunnôun, qut onch pish nussohsum ut wuskesukqut Jehovah, kah num-Manitt8m pish n8menuhkesuonkanin.
49.6 Kah n8wau, ne peasin woh ken n8tinninneumuneat, tahshinnumunat wutchippan8ongash Jakob, kah wunnompashónat neh wadchanonche Israel: kittinninnumoush wonk 8wequáiyeumunneaóut Gentilsog, onk woh ken n8wadchanitteaonk en wehqshik ohke.
49.7 Yeu wussin Jehovah noh manouwhont Israeloh, kah 8neetupanatam8moh, neh wosketomp jishanumoncheh, noh wutohtimoin uhquanumoncheh, neh wuttinninneumuneaóont nanawunnuácheg, ketahs8tamwog pish wunnaumuneau kah wáapeog, sontimoog wonk pish wowussitteamoog, wutche Jehovah, noh pabahtanumukqussit, kah 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, kah noh pish kuppepenunk.
49.8 Yeu wussin Jehovah, ut wussikkitteae aquompiyeuut ken8toush, kah ut wádchanittue kesukodtut kutáninnnumoush: kah pish k8wadchansh, kah kittinnumoush 8n8waongan8 missinninnuog, menehketeauunat ohke, wutohkéhtinneat touushinee ohtoongash:
49.9 Onk woh kuttin kobshogkinnutcheg, sohham8k: kah neg apitcheg pohkenaiyeuut, nókqussek: nag pish meetsuog en mayut, kah wuttittanadtupp8ongan8óash pish ohtaash wame qunuhqui ayeuonganéhtu.
