49.10 Nag matta pish kodtupp8og kah kôhkutt8nóog; kah kussitteau kah nepauz matta pish wuttogkomuh: newutche noh monanumont pish wussagkompánuh, kishke tohkekomuut nah pish puppummuwunuh.
49.11 Kah nummaáhteam wame n8wadchúmash, kah nummayash pish mishehteauunash.
49.12 Kusseh, yeug pish noadtit 8mwog: kah kusseh, yeug wutch nanumiyeu, kah wutch wutcheksuiyeu, kah yeug wutch Sinimme ohkeit.
49.13 Kutt8hamush, woi kesuk, kah weekontash, woi ohke, kah kussont8waóuhamunk woi wadchuash: newutche Jehovah tápheau ummissinninnúmoh, kah noh pish monanumau wutonkuppunômoh.
49.14 Qut Zion n8wop, Jehovah nutohquánumuk, kah nul-Lordum n8wanánumuk.
49.15 Sun woh mittumwossis wannánumau n8nunutcheh, matta woh ukkitteamonteanumóineat wutôontomukque wunnaumonuh? nux woh 8wanánumóuh, qut onch matta k8wunanumun8h.
49.16 Kusseh, k8sukuhwhu[s]h ut nogquanutchit: kukqussukquaneutungash nagwutteohtaash anaquabeh.
49.17 Kummukiésumog pish kenupsháog, paguanukqueáneg, kah nag máhchimwéhikqueaneg, pish kussohwhéhtunkquog.
49.18 Spádtauompsh wéenu, kah náish: wame yeug miyawéog, kah kuppeyaónukquog: pomantamon, n8wau Jehovah, wunnamuhkut pish neg wame kuthogqueneunk, onatuh wunn8whósuonganit, kah neg pish kupputtukquobpussuóunóog onatuh weetauwadteaénin.
49.19 Newutche kuppaguanue kah touushinne kutáyeuongash, kah kuppaguanue ohke, eyeu pish péeu kishki, wutche neg wadohkitcheg, kah neg moseask8wonukqueaneg pish nô appuog.
49.20 Mukkiog neg pish wadchánacheg, mahche wanehheont onkatogig, neg pish wonk n8waog ut kuhtauogkut, ayeuonk wussaume peasin wutche nen, aninnumah ayeuonk uttoh áei.
49.21 Neit pish kussim ut kuttahhut, howan yeuh n8neech[â]nuhkongqunuh, n8wanheompkuh nunneechanog, kah nunnussi, nummissineau, kah ohhontsapinneat? kah howan yeuh ukkesukéheuh? kusseh, nunnussiip, yeug, uttôh 8muneau?
49.22 Yeu wussin Lord Jehovah, kusseh nuttahshinum nunnutcheg ut Gentilsut, kah n8nahtoh nummuttaeg wutche missinninnumog; kah neg pish pas8áog kenaumonuh ut wuhpittén8wóut: kah kuttaunoh pish wuttukkéont upponóuh.
49.23 Kah ketass8tamwog pish kenanukéhteunk8wae k8shog, kah wussonksquom8uh kenánukéhteunk8e kokásog: neg pish kenauwanumunkquog wuskesuk8 en ohkeeiyeu, kah pish n8n8squodtámwog kusseete puppissi, kah pish k8wahteoh nen Jehovah; newutch nag matta pish akodchuwog pahtussuósitcheg.
49.24 Sun woh noh tohqunit amaunumauónuh manuhkesit, asuh wunnaumae missin sun woh pohquohwhunau?
49.25 Qut yeu wussin Jehovah, ummissinóm8uh mánuhkesitcheg pish amaunumauwonáuh, kah ne tohqunoncheh uhqunneunkqussit pish pohquohwhunau, newutche nummekonittinnean noh mekônukquean, kah pish n8wadchan keneechanog.
49.26 Kah neg nussohkómonóog sanukkuhhukqu[é]aneg nehenwonche weyaus8, kah neg pish kogkeissippam8og nehenwonche 8sqheongan8, onatuh weekog wine. kah wame weyaus pish wahteau, nen Jehovah k8wadchanuwaéneum, kah kummanouhuwaeneum, ummissugkeneumoh Jakob.
50.1 YEu wussin Jehovah, uttiyeu pogkénittue 8sukuhwhonk kokas, noh pagkénog? kah uttiyeug anúhtuhquóhikquéaneg, kenaau anumauogeh? kusseh, wutche kummatcheseonganoash kummagumw8 kuhhogkaóog, kah wutche kuppanneseonganoash k8kass8 pogkenau.
50.2 Tohwhutch paôon, wanne wosketompaun8h? wehqutteamwean wanne howan namp8hamunk8? sun nunnutcheg nano tiohqui, matta pohquohwhutteamun8? asuh sun mat n8menuhkesuongan8 pohquohwuss8wónat? kusseh, auskonteamweon, nunnunassum keitoh sepuash nuttouohkomukquehteam: na$ut namohsog anunwog newutche mat nippeno, kah nupwog wutch kuhkutt8n8wonk.
50.3 Nuthogquodtum kesukquash pohkenag, kah man8tiónak nutonkwhonkanéhteam.
50.4 Lord Jehovah netuhtoe meenan nuttininnum8uk, woh n8wahteaunat uttoh ut8chee kutt8onk woh ne anog noh sauunup: nutt8hkinuk noh nompoaeu, nehtauog wutt8hkinumun, ogque n8tamunat noh nehtuhtunk.
50.5 Lord Jehovah n8wohshinumunk nehtauog, kah matta nutcheketamweun8p, kah matta nutassa8p.
50.6 Nuttinninnumauop nuppuskq togkommuwaenuog, kah nan8nauash neg pogquinukeg meesunk, matta nutadtahto8p nuskesuk wutche akodchuwonganit kah suhquonittinneat.
50.7 Newutche Lord Jehovah nuttannumunk, newaje matta pish chepshi: newaj nuskesuk ogque ponam môshipsqut: kah n8wahteoh matta pish nutakodchu.
50.8 Noh sampwe ogquanumit pas8tappu, howan woh mehkâusit? moáeu neepauwitteuh: howan a8que, pas8sukiitch.
50.9 Kusseh, Lord Jehovah nuttannumunk, howan noh woh pakodchimit? kusseh, nag wame pish nano nukkoneyeu8og onatuh hogk8unit: moth pish ummahchipwunneauh.
50.10 Howan kenugke kenaau quoshont Lordoh, noh n8sweehtog 8wadtauatonkqussuonk wuttinneumoh, noh pohkenahtu paumushadt, kah matta wequaiyeumu? pabahtantaj 8wesuonk Jehovah, kah ompatissitch um$Manitt8moh.
50.11 Kusseh, wame kenaau nasqunanumógish, wéene ponamóôgis chikkinâsog: pomushagk ken8tómue wôsôhqunáut, kah chikkinásog neg nasqunanógig, yeu pish kutahtauuneau wutch nunnutcheganit, pish kutunkquanumóe sepsin.
51.1 KUhkehtiek asuhkomógish sampweuss[è]onk, natinneahwhógish Jehovah, mo[nunn]eám8k qussuk ne waj omogquehtáhwhutteaóg, kah wônogque passahtheg ne waj kódahtahwhutteáog.
51.2 Monunneók Abraham k8shw8, kah Sarah noh neechanukqueog: newutche noh nunnussu wehkom, kah n8nanum, kah nano nummisheh.
51.3 Newutche Jehovah pish tapeteo Zion: pish tapeteo wame wuttouushinne ayeuongash, kah wuttouohkomuk8m wutogqueteauun Eden, kah wuttouushineum wutogqueteauun wuttanohketeaonganit Jehovah; wekontam8onk, kah muskouanatam8onk na pish ut namehteauun, tabuttantamóonk, kah wunnont8waonk.
51.4 N8tiek nummissinninnúmog, kah ahch8sittiek woi nutohtimóin: newutche naumatuonk pish 8m nuhhogkat, kah nutanwôhsitteuh n8sittumóonk, wequai wutche missinninnúog.
51.5 Nussampweusseonk paswohteau: n8wadchanuwaonk sohham8m8, kah nuhpitenash pish wussumáog missinninnúh: munoh pish nuppahtsuónukqun, kah nag pish pabuhtantamwog nuhpit.
51.6 Ushpunnum8k kuskesukquash en kesukqut, kah mónunneám8k ohke agwe: newutche kesukquash pish mohtuppaem8ash onatuh pukuttaut, kah ohke pish nano ogque nukkoneyeu8 hogk8unit, kah neg na wadohkitcheg, ne pish wutogque nuppuneau: qut n8wadchanuwaonk pish michemohtau, kah nussampweusseonk matta pish matchehteauouun,
51.7 Kuhkehtiek kenaau wahteauógish sampweusseonk, kah missinninnúog nuttinnaumatuonk wuttahhut ohtag: wabesuontam8hteók wosketompae kekontuonk, kah wabesuontam8hteók matchenukqueóg.
51.8 Newutche moth pish ummahchipwunneuh onatuh hogk8unit, kah 8k pish wutogque m8whuh w8loh: qut n8nomwausseonk pish michemohteau, kah n8wadchanuáonk wutch pometuonk, en pometuonganit.
51.9 T8kish, t8kish, menuhkish, woi wuhpit Jehovah, t8kish neane n8adt, nukkone pometuonganit, sunnummatta ken noh tametahwhont Rahab, kah n8chumwetahwomp dragon?
51.10 Sunnummatta ken noh nanassukup keihtoh, m8noiyeue nippeash, kehtahhanne m8noiyeuash kummaehkon wutche man8wadcheg uppannupwushonaout.
51.11 Newaj man8whonche Jehovah pish qushkeog, kah nashpe peyaog ket8homaonk Zion: micheme wekontamoonk pish ohteau uppuhkukk8wout nag pish ohtaog wekontamoonk kah muskouantamoonk, neuantamoonk kah mauonk pish pt8eem8
51.12 Nen nen noh taphikqueog, howan ken quoshadt wosketomp, noh woh napuk? kah wosketomp wunnaumonuh ogquit maske[h]tuit?
51.13 Kah k8wanhik Jehovah noh kezhikquean, noh sepagenuk kesukquash, kah wanohtunk quenohtag muttaok? kah nagwutteae wabesuwontam asekesukokish, newutche ummusquantam8onk sanukkuhh8adt, onatuh nahen pagwohteadt? kah uttiyeu ummusquantam8onk sanukkuhh8adt?
51.14 Penuwohteae missin kenupshau woh ompinneonat, kah matta woh nupp8 ut passohtheganit, kah mat woh uppetukqununk mahtsheau.
51.15 Qut nen Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, noh chaubinuk keitoh wuttuk8moh mahshont8wanit: Jehovah ayeuhteaunit ne 8wesuonk.
51.16 Kah nupponam nukkutt8wongash kutt8nit, kah kupputtogguhwhush wutonkouwohtom nunnutcheg: onk woh nutohketeam kesukquash, kah woh n8nohto quenohtag ohke, kah woh nuttin Zion, ken nummissinninnúmog.
51.17 T8kish, t8kish, neepaush woi Jerusalem, ken wadtattaman wutch wunnutcheganit Jehovah, um̃usquantamwe wuttattamwaitch: k8tattamup sekqskoshunk ut nunnukshae wuttattamwaitchuut, kah sénupánumon.
51.18 Matta howan wunnanawunuh kenugke wame wunnaumonuh neh neechadcheh: kah matta howan wuttannunuh wunnutcheganit, ut kenugke wame wunnaumonat neh kesukkéheoncheh.
51.19 Yeush neesinash kuppeyógqunash, howan woh kenuánumuk? tawushik, kah paguanuonk kah mashagquodt kah togkodteg: howan woh kenashpe táphesh.
51.20 Kenaumonunk sauunumwog, nag sepsinwog wehqshik wame touumáogquehtu, onatuh sasagsúe bull ut hashabput; numwabetunkquog umm8squantam8onk Jehovah, wutaushkommuaonk kum-Manitt8m/
51.21 Newaj eyeu yeu n8tash, ken onkapunaan, kah kogkeussippamwéan, qut matta wine.
51.22 Yeu wussin ke-Lordum, noh Lord kah kumManitt8m, noh kôn8tamwonshont ummissinninnúmoh, kusseh, n8tinnum kenutcheganit nunnukshae cup, sekqskushae nummusquantamwe cup: matta pish wonk k8tattam8un.
51.23 Qut nupponumun wunnutchegan8out neg onkappunánukquean, neg anoncheg kukketeahogkôunoh, nauwaish onk woh kutánuwushkhôunumun: & kutogque pon kuhhog ohkeit, kah onatuh maikontu neg ánuushkhônukqueaneg.
52.1 T8hkish, t8kish, hogqush kummenuhkesuonk, woi Zion, hogqush k8ne hogk8unash, woi Jerusalem wunneetupanatamwe keihtotan: newutche yeu wutch matta quoshqusauseg, kah nishkeneunkqussit matta pish wonk kuppetutteaónuk8.
52.2 Tattauwonteash kuhhog wutch puppissiyeuut: omohkish kah nummatapsh, woi Jerusalem; ompin kuhhog wutch kussittippukane keneepsuongash, woi missinnoe wuttaunoh Zion.
52.3 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, kummagumw8 kuhhogkaóog wutche monteag: kah ne toh pish kuttit manonwhitteaneau matta wutch teaguas.
52.4 Newutche yeu wussin Lord Jehovah nummissinninnúmog n8adt w8msuog en Egypt, na wuttit appuóneau, kah wut-Assyrian tahwunn8che sunnukohwhôuh.
52.5 Newutche yeuyeu teag nutohto yeuut, n8wau Jehovah, waj nummissinninneumog wutch monteag amaunit? nag nanawunoncheg, mauáheuh, n8wau Jehovah, kah nagwutteaeu blasphemontamun n8wesuonk asekesukokish.
52.6 Newaj num̃issinninnumog pish wahteauhettit n8wesuonk: newaj ne kesukok, pish wahteauhettit, nen noh kodt8hkont, kusseh nen.
52.7 Uttoh unn8wunnegen wusseetash ut wadchuuhkontu, noh wanonchimwut, noh wahteauwahuadt wunohteaonk, noh wanonchem8kontog wanegik, noh wahteauwahuadt wadchanittuonk, noh anont Zionoh kum-Manitt8m nanawunnuau.
52.8 Kutaswhosuenumog pish mishont8waog wadtauatonkqussue pish moeu ket8hamaog: newutche nag pish muskesukque naittuog, Jehovah wonk paudtunk Zion.
52.9 Mishont8wae wekontam8k, moae ket8hamunk kenaau mahchum8e ayeuongash ut Jerusalem, newutche Jehovah tapheau ummissinninnumoh, noh pohquohwhunóp Jerusalemoh.
52.10 Newutche Jehovah poskinum 8neetupanatamwe wuhpit ut wuskesuk8wout wame wutohtimoneunk, kah wame aongkoue weekqshik ohke, pish naumwog 8wadchanuwaonk num-Manitt8m8uh.
52.11 Amaek, amaek, na wutch sohham8k, missinnum8hteok nishkenéungque teag, sohham8k wutch wunnashomut: pahkesek kenau kônunnumogish 8wishquash Jehovah.
52.12 Newutche matta pish kukkenuppe sohham8m8, asuh wusseem8e: newutche Lord kenekonukkongkou: kah um-Manitt8moh Israel kuppishquan8e wadchanukqueog.
52.13 Kusseh, nuttinneum pish waantamwe ussu, noh pish misheheau, kah woweenomau kah pish ahche qunuhqussu.
52.14 Neane monaog chepshunkquean, (wuttinnussuonk matcheteanum anue onk howa onkatuk, kah wuttinnompamukqussuonk anue onk neh wosketompaog wunnaumonauh.)
52.15 Neweyane pish seanumun monátash wutohtimoneash: tahs8tamwog ukkupputt8naehtauouh: newutche ne matta anont pish wunnaumuneau, kah ne matta n8tammóhetteg pish wunnatwontamunéau.
53.1 HOwan wanamptog nukkuhk8tomwehteaonk? kah háwane Jehovah wuhpit wahteauwaheont?
53.2 Newutche noh pish ogque neetu kuhkushque ahhohketeamuk, ut anaquabit, kah onatuh wadchaubuk ut nobohteaiyeuut: matta wunneku asuh tapeneunkqussu: kah nauogkut, matta wunnetuonk ohtoou woh kukkodtanumonanonut.
53.3 Noh sekeneauau, & uppogkenouh wosketompaog, onkuppunnaenin, kah nagwutteohto neuanatam8onk: kah onatuh adahtauogkut nuskesukqunonash, noh jishanumop kah matta n8t8anum8un.
53.4 Wunnamuhkut tahshinnum nutonkapunnaonganunonash, kah noh kenunnum nunnuantam8onganunonash: qut n8t8ánumouunónup togkomau, wuttogkomuh God, kah onkapunau.
53.5 Qut noh n8chumwehtahwhop wutch nuppanneusseonganunonash, noh puppukittahwhop wutch nummatcheseonganunnonash, n8nohteae sasamatahwhutteáonk, wuhhogkat ohtóp kah nashpe togkommaongash neetskehitteamun.
53.6 Wame neenawun nutogque wowó[un]immun sheepsut: nukquinuppemun en nishnoh pasuk nehenwonche ummayut; kah Lord upponamuaoh wame nummatcheseonganunonash.
53.7 Noh sanukkuhwhop, kah noh onkapunóp, qut matta wôhshinum8 wutt8n: noh ogque pas8au nashómuk lamb: kah onatuh kupputt8ne sheep ut anaquabenit m8sukqutcheh, ne weyane matta wôhshinum8un wutt8n.
53.8 Noh amaunap wutch kuppishagkinittinneat, kah wutch wussittum8onganit: kah howan woh wahteauwahuau uppometuonk? newaj tametahwhit wutch pomantamwae ohkeit, wutche uppanneseongan8 nummissinninnúmog togkomop.
53.9 Kah ayim 8wenohke ut kenugke matchet8ut, kah ut kenugke wena[n]wetuut, napuk, newutche matta chekéusseup, kah matta as8kekodteamowonganinno wutt8nit.
53.10 Qut onch Jehovah tapeneam uppuppukkehtahwhónat, wutuhquanumwuhheuh: ukketeahogkô[u]noh sephausuwáheadt wutch matcheseonk, noh pish naum 8skannem pish sepohtau ukkesukodtumash, kah wuttapeneaum8onk pish wunnaiyeum8 ut wunnutcheganit.
53.11 Pish naau ukketeahogkôunne neetuonk, kah pish tapheau: nashpe waheaonk nussampweusseae nuttinninneum noh pish sampwe ogquanumau monaoh: newutche noh pish kenunum ummatcheseonganooash.
53.12 Newaj pish chadchabenumauog ohtóonk ut kenugke masugkenutcheh, kah noh pish chadchapenum sequttahhamóonk ut kenugke mamanuhkesitcheg: newutche sok[e]nau ukketeahogkôunoh en nuppunat: kah noh weetogkemóp panneusseaénuh, kah noh kenunum monaog ummatcheseongan8, kah ken8tamwanshau pannesénitcheh.
54.1 KEt8hamush, woi mahchéean, matta neech8an, mishont8wa8hamush, kah mishont8ash, ken matta neechaan: newutche wunneechanoh nohsiit neg anuwânwog, onk neh wunneechanoh weetauwadteadt, n8wau Jehovah
54.2 Mishegskehteoush keeke ayeuonk, kah sepagenáhettich kutáyeue onkwheganog: wohquontogan, qunnompágunush kuppemuneat, menehketeaush kuppogkomunkquongash.
54.3 Newutche pish kuppishkôem ut kuttinohkôunit, kah ut kummenadcheanit, kah k8skannem pish wuttaihéeu Gentilsoh, kah touushinne otanash pish 8tohkeúhkonáoash.
54.4 Wabesehkon, newutche matta pish kutakodchu: asuh quequenauánum8hkon, newutche matta pish kutakodchéhetteúh: newutche pish k8wanantam k8skenue akodchuonk, kah matta pish wonk kummequontam8 kussekousquae kekómitteaonk.
54.5 Newutche noh kezhukquean 8wessukiin, (Jehovah ayeuteaanit, ne 8wesuonk) kah kummanouhuwaéneum 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, mamusse ohkée um-Manitt8moh ne ussowé[n]on
54.6 Newutche Jehovah kutogque wehkomuk pôgkénit mittumwossis, kah neuanittamwutteáhont, kah wuske[n]ue mittamwussi[n], pogkéinumuk, n8wau kum-Manitt8m.
54.7 Ogguhsese kuppogkensh, qut nashpe mogke monanetuongash kummukkinush.
54.8 Ogguhse musquanittamon kutadtahtaush nuskesuk, ogguhsese, qut nashpe machemohtag monanittuonk kummonanumush, n8wau Jehovah kummanouhuwaéneum.
54.9 Newutche yeu nuttatupontamwe wunnippéimut Noah: newutche neane chadchekéyeui wunnuppemash Noah matta pish wonk nuhkuhkom8mun8 ohke, ne nuttinne chadchekeyeuon, matta kummusquanumun8, asuh kutauskómun8.
54.10 Ne wadchuash pish amaém8ash, kah wadchuemesash pish ontohtaash: qut n8womoausuonk matta pish kenukonuk8, kah n8nohteáe wunn8waonk matta pish ontohtano, n8wau Lord noh monanumukquean.
54.11 Woi ken onkquanumwean, pâpomanómukquean mishehtash, kah matta taphenn8muk: kusseh, nupponam kukqussukquanumash wunnompamukquadtut kah n8nahtóh kukquenahtagkomash nashpe Saphirsash.
54.12 Kah nutayim kukkenogkinnegash nashpe carbunklsash, kah wame kussissippóiyeumash nashpe wunnequssukquanash.
54.13 Kah keneechanoh wame pish ukkuhk8tomauoh Jehovah, kah keneechanog missi pish 8nohteaongan8.
54.14 Ut sampweusséonganit kummenuhkéhit, kena8sukom mukk8kinittuonk, newutche nag pish k8wabesu, kah quequenauanumoonk, newutche matta pish kuppas8sukongk8un.
54.15 Kusseh, nag pish wunnamuhkut miyaweog, qut matta nashpe nen, howaneg ayeuuhkonittue miyaetunkquean, nag pish penushaog wutche ken.
54.16 Kusseh, nukkezheomp Smith noh p8p8tauontog mokkossaash ut n8taut, kah noh paudtunk auwohteaonk wutch wutanakausuonk, kah nukkezteop nippe pagwohteom8ut.
54.17 wanne kenauwameonk ne ayeuuhkonittue kezteauunumuk pish wunnesemun8, kah nish$noh meenan ne áyeuuhkonittue waabetunkquean ut wussittum8onganit, pish kuppogkodchimit, yeu wutohtoongan8 wuttinneumoh Jehovah, kah wussampweusseongan8 wutchaiyeum8 nuhhogkat n8wau Jéhovah.
55.1 EHoh nish$noh pasuk noh kuhkutt8g, peyonch nippekontu, kah noh mátta ohto8g teaguas: peyonk, adtôagk, kah meets[e]k, nux peyonk, adtóagk wine kah sogkodtunk matta wutch teaguas, kah matta noadtue.
55.2 Tohwutch mag8og teagwash ne matta pâdtukqunnunganun8g? kah kutanakausuongan8, wutche ne matta taphuomun8? menuhke n8tiegk, kah meech8k ne wanegik, kah kukketeahogkoun8 weekontaj ut wunogquneat.
55.3 Ahch8suttah, kah peyaauseh n8tam8k, kah kutteahogkoun8 pish pomantam; kah kutayimauonumw8 m[â]chemohtag wunn8waonk, papane monanumaongash David.
55.4 Kusseh, nuttinninnumau missinninnuh 8wauwonat, sagkompaginnuen, kah ann8nuwaenin en missinninnuut.
55.5 Kusseh, pish k8wehkom wutohtimoin ne matta wahteauo[n]an, kah wutohtimoneash nish matta wahik8unish, pish kukquentunkqunash, wutche Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, k[a]h wutch 8neetupanatam8moh Israel: newutche noh kussohsum8wahik.
55.6 Natinneah8k Jehovah woh ash namhit: wehkomash pas8tappit.
55.7 Matchetou nukkotutch ummay, kah matsampweusseaenin wuttenantam8ongash, kah qushkeitch en Jehovah$ut, kah pish ummonanumuh, kah en num-Manitt8mut newutche noh pish m8cheke ahquontam.
55.8 Newutche nuttenantam8ongash matta k8tenantamuonkaneinash, kah kummayash matta nummayash n8wau Jehovah.
55.9 Newutche neane kesukquash anue qunuhquotash onk ne ohke, netatuppe nummayash qunuhquodtash anue onk kummayash kah nuttenantam8ongash, onk kuttenattam8ongash.
55.10 Newutche neane n8kem8[u]k sokanon kah k8n wutch kesukqut, kah matta qushkeog, qut nippehkontamwog ohke, kah ummechumuhkon, kah 8nt8nohquamuhkon, onk, onk woh 8skannemunneuhkauonat ahketeanutcheh, kah petukqununk wutch noh meetsit.
55.11 Ne pish nneu nuttinn8waonk ne sohham8m8ug wutch nutt8nut: matta pish mahchiyeue qushkemun8 en nuhhogkat, qut pish kézteau8m8 nê tapeneam, kah pish wunayeum8 uttôh áne ann8tam.
55.12 Newutche pish k8wekontamwe sohham8m8, kah pish k8nohteae monchanitteamw8: wadchuash kah wadchuemesash pish mishont8a8hamóm8ash ut anaquabeog, kah wame ohteakon8e mehtugquash pish pohponkinitchahhuog.
55.13 Nonompu asinnekô[á]s pish wutch sonkin firuhtug, kah nonompu kôus pish wutchegin myrtlúhtug: kah ne pish wutch wesuonk Jehovahut, kah wutch machemohtag kuhkinneasuonk, ne matta pish támuttahham8muk.
56.1 YEu wussin Lord, nanawehteau8k wussittumóonk, kah s[a]mpweussek, newutche n8wadchanuwaonk pas8che peyom8: kah nussampweusseonk wahteauwahuwon.
56.2 Wunánumau wosketomp noh yeu asit, kah wunnaumonuh wosketomp noh másunuk, noh nanawehteunk sabath wutch matta wunnishketeau8unat, kah noh nanawehteunk wunnutcheg wutch matchesenat.
56.3 Kah wunnaumonuh penuot noh weetashunt wuhhogkuh Lordut, ahque n8waj, n8wonat, Jehovah papaquanne nutchippunuk wutch ummissinninnúmut: kah eunuchsog n8wahettékitch, kusseh, nen nunohtae mehtug.
56.4 Newutche wuttinnon Lord eunuchsoh, neg nanawehteunkig nussabbat8mash, káh neg pepenogig nish woh wohsikkitteahikqueanish, kah neg manúhkenukig n8n8waonk.
56.5 Nuttinnumauóog ut neekit, kah anóme nuppummenutonganit, ayeuonk kah wesuonk, anue wunnegen onk 8wesuongan8 wunnaumoniitcheg kah wuttaunitcheg: nuttinnumauóog machemohtag wesuonk, ne matta pish támatahham8muk.
56.6 Kah wonk wunnaumonuh pen8wot neg agwappéhtauáhettit Jehovah, wowussumónat, kah womantamunat 8wesuonk Jehovah, 8tinninneumuneat, nishnoh pasuk noh nanawehteunk Sabbath matta niṣhketeau8unat, kah noh kônunuk n8n8waonk.
56.7 Neg nuppas8oog n8neetupanatamwe wadchúmut, kah n8weekontamwaheóog, ut nuppeantamwáe kommukqut, wutchikohtae mag8ongan8oash, kah wussephausuongan8oash, nish pish tapeneamunash ut nut[-]altarumut; newutche nek pish hettamun peantamwae kommuk wutch wame nummissinninneumog.
56.8 Jehovah Manit, noh móunont pakenitcheh nummissinninneumoh, n8wau, nano nummóunúmau, chabesitcheg neh m[o]etunkqutcheh.
56.9 Wame kenaaú ohteakóne puppinashimwog peyunk mahchipwunneat, wame kenaau touohkomukque puppinashimwog,
56.10 Wutaskwhôsuéneumoh pogkenumwoh: nag wame as8tuog, nag wame mokákutt8e anumwog, matta wohwóhteau8og: kouéog, sepsinwog, wekontamwog kogkouequon.
56.11 Nux, nag nehnehteáp8e anumwog, neg woh mo wamep8gig, kah nag nanaushepsaenuog matta wohwohtamóog: nag wame moninneamwog nehenwonche ummayyeu, nishnoh pasuk wutch wutonts8nam8onk, wutch wutchippaiyeumut.
56.12 Peyunk, n8waog, nunneemskom wine, kah nunnumwohtauómun nuhhogkanonog onkuppe, kah saup pish neyane yeuyeu kesukok, kah m8cheke muttae.
57.1 SAmpweusseaen nup, kah matta howan upponam8un wuttahhut: kah monaneteaénuog amaunóog, matta howàn wunnatwontam8un, sampweusseaenin am[à]unau wutch machuk ne paóm8ug.
57.2 Noh pish petutteau wunohteaonganit, nag pish anwôsinwog ut wutapinneaóut, nish$noh pasuk paumwushadt ut wussampweusseonganit.
57.3 Qut pas8tshagk, kenaau wunnaumonauh pauwásq, 8skannem mamussuaenin, kah nanwun8dsquâsuen.
57.4 Howan ayeuuhkonittue chétwhók kuhhogkaóog? howan ayeuuhkonittue mashe kushkutt8naéhtauóg, kah sonkhénanúwaéhtauóg? sunnummatta kenaau panneseae wunneechaninneunk? pann8wae wuskannem?
57.5 Kukkussináheomw8 kuhhogkaóog nashpe nunneukontunkkanog, ut agwe nish$noh askuh[n]kq nushonat mukkiesog 8nôuhkôiyeutu, ut agwe pass[o]mpsk[o]déhtu.
57.6 Ut kenugke kussitchuáne m8sompsquéhtu, ne kutchippiyeum: nish, nish kutittanohtôadtuonk: kussókanumau[ô]og nag wuttattam8e sephausuonk, kummag meetsue mag8onk, sun woh nutattumunum taphettuonk yeush ut?
57.7 Ut qunuhqui kodohk[ó]ag na kupponamun kutappin: na kuttinne kuhkuhquen kumm[à]gunat sephausuongash.
57.8 Onkauùssquont wonk, kah pogkomukquongash ne kupponamun kummequantam8onk: newutche kuposkehtau onkatok onk nen, kah kukkuhkuhquem: kummisheu kuskéhteop kutappin, kah nag k8n8wón[a]óog, k8womontam wutappinneau ut$toh ut nauman.
57.9 Kah kutóm ketass8tamwut nashpe pummee, kah nano kummishteo k8weetemunkquot8mash, kah kutann8n kutann8naeneumog wutch n8adtut, kah kuttiahquonkqueh kuhhog wehque chepiohkomuk.
57.10 Kussauunuk kumishe mayuk8m, qut onch matta kussú, matt[a] annoôsuonganinno: kummishkom kenutchegane pomantam8onk, newajeh matta n8henn8muk.
57.11 Howan wabesuônadt kah quoshadt, waj pann8wáan, kah matta kummequanumu, asuh kupponam8un kuttahhut? sunnummatta nutchepappu wutch n8adt, kah matta kukqushéu?
57.12 N8wahteauwáhuam kussampweusseonk, kah kutanakausuongash: newutche nish matta pish n8chiéinash.
57.13 Máuan, weechógquéaneg pohquohwhunukqush: qut waban pish 8wame monchanuh: tan8cheéyeuuk pish wunneemunuh; qut noh pabahtanumit, pish ohtau ohke, kah pish ahtou n8neetupanatamwe wadchúm.
57.14 Kah pish n8waog, kuhkuhquonteagk, kuhkuhquonteagk quoshauwehtam8k may, amaunum8k togkussittassunóonk wutch ummayeuont nummissinninnúmog.
57.15 Newutche yeu wussin noh quanunkqussit kah masugkenuk noh áyit machemóhtagit, noh as8wésit wanetupanatamweyeuit: nuttai qunuhqui kah wunneetupanatamwe ayeuonganit: n8weetom wonk, pohquehteáheont, kah ahohpateáhont, quaquakqheónat ahhohpanitcheh, kah quaquakqheonat pohqueteahónitcheh.
57.16 Newutche matta nummicheme mekónteóh, kah matta nagwutteae pish nummusquanittam8: newutche wunnashaongan8 woh sauunum8m8 ut anaquabeh, kah keteahogkôunog neg kezheógig.
57.17 Wutche wutiahchewont[à]m8e matcheséonk, nummusquantamup, kah nuttogkomop; nupputtogquep, kah nummusquantamop, kah pittuanumwu kutchitáushóp ut wuttahh8wáe mayut.
57.18 Nunnaumup ummayash, kah nunneetke[h] nussagkompagun wonk, kah nunnompinnumau taphettuonk, kah ummauunnitteaéneumoh.
57.19 Nukkezteóh ummeechummúonk mussissitt8n, wunohteaonk, wunohteaj noh nóapit, kah noh pas8tappit, n8wau Lord, kah nunneetskeh.
57.20 Qut matchetukeg tatuppeyeu8og mishontuk8e kehtahhanit, matta ch[é]pohtan8g, noh nippe sohwanúhtog pissag, kah nishkeneunkquok.
57.21 Matta 8nohteaonganúmu matcheetou n8wau num-Manitt8m.
58.1 MIshont8ash, wohquontogan, ogque mishont8ash monuhpuhpequonut kah náhtus nummissinninnúmog uppanneseongan8oash, kah wek Jakob ummatcheseongan8oash.
58.2 Qut onch nag natinneáhikquog asekesukokish, kah weekontamwog wahteauun nummayash, onatuh sampweusseae wutohtimóin, kah matta ahquontamoe ukkuhk8waongash um-Manitt8m8uh: nunnat8tamunkquog sampweusseae kuhk8waongash: weekontamup pas8sukauunat God
58.3 Tohwutch mat meetseog, kah matta kenaum8un? tohwutch onkapunnanogkut nukketeahogkôunoh, kah matta kukkehkinneaséin? kusseh, matmeetsue kesukkodtut kutohtóm8 weekontamóonk, kah chekée usséhuwom8 wame kutanakausuongánooash.
58.4 Kusseh, mekonittue, kah penuánittue matkummeetsúmw8, tattéohtinat machetoe menutcheg: matta pish matkummeetsumw8, neáseóg yeu kesukok kukqunúhque n8tunkqunuhkônaóut k8wadtauatonkqussuongan8.
58.5 Sun nein matmeetsuonk ne pepenam? kesuk neadt wosketomp uhquanumwéheunt ukketeahogkounoh? sun ne wunnauánumunat uppuhkuk onatuh bulrush, kah ogque upponamunat man8tiónak kah pukquee? sun yeu kuttéhettamun matmeetsuonk, kah 8sekitteae kesukodt8m Jehovah?
58.6 Sunnummatta yeu matmeetsuonk ne pepenam? ompinimunat matcheetowongane kishpissuongash, ompenimunat tuhkequanne weanunash, kah sânukahwhut wutchippinnúinneat, kah pokshanónat nishnoh yoak?
58.7 Sunnummatta ne kuttinnumauónat kuppetukqunnunk kodtupwutcheg, kah kuppasuonat kekit, matcheku noh sohwohteamuk: nauadt poskissu, kutonk8h, & matta kutadtahsh[o]h kuhhog wutch nehenwonche keyaus.
58.8 Neit k8wequáiyeum pish ogque sonkqsúm8 mahtompanut, kah k8niyeuonk pish kenuppe sonksum8: kah kussampweusseonk pish kenegonuhkunk, wussohsumóonk Jehovah, noh pish kuppisquane nanauhik.
58.9 Neit pish k8wehquetum, kah Jehovah pish kenamp8hamunk, pish kummauunnitteau, kah noh pish n8wau, nen yeu: amaunadt yoak wutch kenashómut, kenutcheg sontikquanuwóm8ut, kah tahn8che keket8kaonk.
58.10 Kôdtunadt kukketeahogkou en noh kodtupwit, kah wampwehe[à]dt unkuppunáe keteahogkou, neit k8wequaiyeum pish waapem8 ut pohkenaouut, kah kuppohkenaiyeum pish tatuppeyeu8 pohshaquadt.
58.11 Kah Jehovah pish nagwutteae kussamp8wunuk, kah pish wamepwéheau kukketeahogkounoh, kunkohteadtag, kah wunogquehteau koskonash: kah pish kuttatuppeyeu wuttadtippadtaueu tanohketeaonganit, kah tohkekomuut, noh wunnippe matta ahquohtán8g.
58.12 Kah nag wágig kuhhogkat, pish ayimwog nukkonne ayeuongash nish matchteomukish: pish kuttashinum monaash pometeongash quenohtagish: kah pish kuttehenit, onchteunk pokqshunk, kah nompenuk ayeuongane mayash.
58.13 Qushkinnuman kusseet wutch sabbath$dayut, matta kutusseinat nehenwonche k8wekontam8onk, ut n8eetupantamwe kesukodtumut, kah hettaman sabbath n8wekontam8onk, 8neetupanatam8m Jehovah, quohtianumukquok, kah noh quttianumadt, matta ussean nehenwonche kummayash asuh mat kenemunnum8unat nehenwonche wekontam8onk, kah matta kusseinat nehenwonceh kukk8ttwongash.
58.14 Neit pish k8wekontamwah kuhhog Jehovahut, kah kenayeúmukqu[éb]esh ut qunuhqui ayeuonganéhtu ut ohkeit, & pish kussohkom8nsh nashpe wutohtoonk Jacob k8sh, newutche wutt8n Jehovah ukkutt8kontamun.
59.1 KUsseh, wunnutcheg Jehovah tiohqutteauóuun, onk ne woh mo adchanuómun8, kah wehtauog matta tuhkequanun8 woh moh wunn8tam8unat.
59.2 Qut kummatcheseongash chippemoash ut nashaue kenaau, kah kum-Manitt8m8óut, kah kummatcheseongash adtahtau wuskesuk wutch kenaau, woh mo n8tam8unat.
59.3 Newutche kenutcheoash wunnishketeauunash musqueheonk, kah kuttinwhunutchegash nashpe matcheseonk, kah kussissitt8n8ash pann8wom8ash, keenan woonki m8m8sk8womo.
59.4 Wanne howan wehqueteum8 sámpweusseonk, kah matta howan ket8konshittam8 wanamuhkuteyeuuk: nag pabahtantamwog tahn8cheyeuuk, káh pann8waog, wompequo8og woskehuwaonk, kah neechaog panneusseonk.
59.5 Ahtinnasinwog 8woanash cokatrice, kah monakeneheaog manunapit wuthashabpoh: noh meechik nag 8woano8ash nup, kah ne sanukehthamuk, ⟦sohwutchuanu viper.⟧
59.6 Ummonakenehteaongan8 matta pish onkwhooog wuhhogkauh nashpe wutanakausuongash: wutanakausuongan8oash matcheseae anakausuongash, kah chekee usseonk ohteau wunnutcheganit.
59.7 Wusseetoash u[h]shom8ash matchitut, & kenupshaaog sokohkonat mat woskehuwae musqueheonk: wuttenantam8ongan8oash matcheseae unnantam8ongash, mahchumwehtoonk kah paguanuonk ut ummayeuout.
59.8 Wunohteae may matta wahteau8og, kah na matta wussittum8onganun8 ut ummoncheongan8out: neg ayimauaog woonki mayash wuttinniin howan na aont, matta pish wunohteaonk.
59.9 Newaj na8sukongqueog wussittumoonk, kah sampweusseonk matta kumatanuk8unan: nuppahtómun wequai kah kusseh pohkenai: wompag, qut nuppomushomun pohkenáhtu.
59.10 Nunn8sweemun qussukquaneuntunk onatuh pohp[ôg]kenumuk, kah nuppopogkénumunun, onatuh mat wuskesuk8og: nuttogkussittássunumun pohshequaeu, onatuh nohkog, touishinne ayeuonganehtu onatuh nápumuk.
59.11 Nutogquont8wómun mosqut, kah nutogque mishe maumun wuskuhwunanáut: nunnátauwompattamumun wussittumoonk, qut na matta ohtano, wadchanittuonk qut nô óhteau.
59.12 Newutche nuppaneseonganónash muttaánutash ut anaquabean, kah nummatcheseonganunonash nutayeuuhkônittue wauwaónukqunánonash: newutche nuppanneseonganunonash n8weetómukqunánonash, kah nummatcheseonganunonash n8wahteauunánonash.
59.13 Panneséog kah ayeuuhkonittue pann8waheogkut Jehovah, kah amaéog wutch num-Manitt8munónut, an8wáogish sunukkôwhuttuonk kah ontogquéhtam8onk, ananatamog, kah metass8wae kodt8kôog pann8waongash.
59.14 Kah wussittum8onk qushkem8: kah sampweusseonk nôadtit neepattau: newutche wanamuhkutéyeuuk pógkishin maikontu, kah tatuppenéhettuonk matta petutteamun8.
59.15 Nux, wunnamuhkutéyeuuk panushean, kah noh nôkodtuk machuk, muk8kinnuwaheau wuhh[h]ogkuh, kah Jehovah wunnaumun, kah matta 8sekitteáhik8un newutche matta wussittum8wonganinn8.
59.16 Kah naum na matta wosketompaunn8, kah monchanatam matta howan ukken8tamwanshuh, newaj 8hpit paudtauont wadchanittuonk, kah wussampweusseonk ukqukquninukqun.
59.17 Newutche ogque hogk8 sampweusseonk mohpanáganit ahhohtag, kah wadchanittue uppuhkukqut ahhohtag uppuhkukqut? kah hogk8 ann8tôadtue hogk8unash wutche wuthogk8onk, kah hogk8 zeale onatuh petashqusháonk.
59.18 Neaunak wutusseongan8oash, ne wuttinonkquttauun ayeuuhkonukqutcheh musquanittam8onk, kah onkquatunk en ummatwomut, pish onkquttauau munóhhanoh onkquatunk.
59.19 Neit pish wabesuontamwog 8wesuonk Jehovah wutch wutcheksuiyeu, kah wussohsumóonk waj pashpishont: matwau ogque petutteadt tomogkanit, wunnashauanitt8moh Jehovah pish wutáyeuuhkonittue tahshinnumauoh muttaagk.
59.20 Kah man8hhuwaenin pish peyau Zion, kah en nahoh ámaécheg wutch pannesénut ut Jakob, wussin Jehovah.
59.21 Qut nen, yeu n8n8waonganun nagoh wussin Jehovah, nunnashauanitt8m noh apehtunkquean, kah nukkutt8wongash nish ponamunish kutt8nit, nish matta pish amaémunoash wutch kutt8nut, kah matta wutch wutt8n8óut k8skannemuneog, asuh matta wutch wutt8n8wout k8skannemuneog 8skannémun8óut, wussin Lord, yeu wutche kah micheme.
60.1 TOOkish, wôhsish, newutche k8wequa8m peyom8, kah wussohsum8onk Lord k8waabéhtunkqun.
60.2 Newutche kusseh, pohkenái pish nuhkuhkom ohke, kah kuhpogke pohkenái ut missinninnutu: qut Jehovah pish kuppashpishaónuk, kah wussohsumóonk pish kenaumontean.
60.3 Kah Gentilsog pish peyaog k8wequaiyeumut, kah ketass8tamwog ut kussohsumóe omohkeonganit.
60.4 Spadtauomps waéenu, kah naish, nag wame miyaéog, kuppeyaônukquog, kenaumonunk pish nóadtit 8mwog, kah kuttaunog pish nanukkehéoog ut kishke ken.
60.5 Neit pish kenaum, kah kummoáeu tomogkem, kah kuttah pish wabesu, kah pish misheheau; newutche kehtahhanne monacheg pish qunnuppekompauog en kuhhogkat, ummenuhkesuongan8 Gentilsog pish kuppeyaónukqunash.
60.6 Mataánukeg Camelsog pish kenuhkuhkunk, Midiane kah Ephahe dromedarisog: wame neg apitcheg Sheba pish peyaog, neg pish paudtoog gold, kah weetemungquok, kah nag pish wahteauwahuwáog waeenomaongash Jehovah.
60.7 Wame Kedare floksog pish miyaéog en kuhhogkat: Nebajothe ramsog pish k8wowussehitteaonganog: nag pish tapenumoe kuhkuhqueog en nut-altarumut, kah nussohsum8wahteoh sohsumóe nek.
60.8 Howanig yeug agque pt8écheg matokqsit, kah onatuh wsk[uh]whunanáout en 8wadshaoont?
60.9 Wunnamuhkut munnáhanash pish nuppahtsuónukqunash, kah Tarshishe kuht8nogquash negonne, pas8ónat kenaumonunk wutch nôadtit, pas8ónat kenaumonunk wutch nôadtit, wus$silverum8, kah uk-goldum8 weeche nagoh; en 8wesuonganit Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, kah en 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, newutche kussohsum8ónuk
60.10 Kah wunnaumonaoh pen8wohteaog pish ayimwog kuthassunninneutungash, kah ukketass8tam[o]m8uh pish kutannumunkquog: newutche musquantamon kuttagkomunup, qut kodtumonteánitteon kummonánumunup.
60.11 Newaj pish kutishquontamash nagwutteáe wôshwohtag, nish matta pish kuppuhhaúsin8ash kesukodaeu asuh nukkonáeu, onk woh wosketompaog kuppaudtunkquog 8weenauweetuongan8 Gentilsog, kah ukketass8tam8m8uh woh paudtauonauh.
60.12 Newutche wutohtimoin kah ass8tamóonk ne matta wadtinninneumuhkonk8an, neg pish unkquanumôog, nux yeush wutohtimoneash pish papaquáne mohchimoash.
60.13 Wussohsumóonk Lebanon pish kenuhkuhkunk, firuhtug, pineuhtug, kah boxuhtug moeu, wunnehteauunat nus-sanctuarie ayeuonk, kah nussohsumwáhto nusseetoe ayeuonk.
60.14 Wunnaumonáuh wonk neg unkquanumwehikqueaneg, nag pish nauwaée kuppéyogquog kah wame neg jishanumukqueaneg, nag pish nauwaeog ut agwe kusseetut, kah pish kuttéhenukquog ukkeitotan Jehovah wus-Zion8m 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
60.15 Uttôhadt, ohquanumunumukup káh jishanumunumukup, newaj matta wosketomp pannuppuhkongk8an; kutáyimáush michemohtae wunneetuonk, 8wekontam8ongan8 monaash pometeaonganash.
60.16 Ken8n wonk pish wussogkodtunkan8 gentilsog: kah pish ken8nontam wohpanágun8 ketass8tamoh, kah pish k8wahteoh nen Jehovah k8wadchanuaeneum, kah kummanouhuwaeneum, ummissugkeneumoh Jakob.
60.17 Nompéeu brasse nuppaudtoh gold, kah nompéeu m8óhsh nuppaudtoh silver, kah nompeeu wudtuk brasse: kah nompe qussukquanash m8óhshag; kah n8nohteahéog kutannohsuénúmog, kah koshkomunukeg nussampweusseaenúheoog.
60.18 Chekeayeu8k matta pish wonk n8tam8un ut kutohkit, mohchumoonk asuh pagwanuonk ut kussissippóiyeumut: qut pish ku[téh]ettam kuthassunninnútungash, wadchanittuonk, kah k8squontamash waeenomaonk.
60.19 Nepauz matta pish wonk k8wôhsumungk8 kesukodae kah wutche wôhsittae nanepâuhshad matta pish k8wôhsumunk8. qut Jehovah pish noh kummicheme weequaiy8m, kah kum-Manitt8m noh pish kussohsum8onk.
60.20 Kenepauz8m màtta pish wonk wayau8, & kenanepauhshadt matta pish monchu, newutche Jehovah pish kummicheme ohtae wequai8m, kah kummauongane kesukodtash pish wohkukquoshinash.
60.21 Kummissinninnumog wonk wame pish sampweusseaenúog; pish ohtoog ohke micheme, 8tuhqunnum ne ahketeaomp, nunnutchegane anakausuonk, onk woh nussohsum8ónit.
60.22 Noh peississit pish muttannonganeyeu8, noh n8chumwesit pish menuhki wutohtimóin, nen Lord nukkenuppe ussen ut wutaquompiyeum8ut.
61.1 WUnnashauanitt8moh Lord Jehovah nutapéhtunk, newutche Jehovah nussusséqunuk kuhk8tomauonat manunnissitcheg wunaunchem8kaonk, nutann8[n]uk aseepinónat pohqutteahhoncheg, wahteauwaheonat chippinnú8onk en missinôut, kah wôshinnumauónat kuppishagkinnittuonk neg kashpissitcheg.
61.2 Wahteauwahuónat 8weekontamwae kodtum8m Jehovah, kah wutann8t8wae ukkesukkodtum num-Manitt8mun, tapheonat wame neg mógig.
61.3 Kehtimónaóont neg mogig ut Zion, aninnumauonát, wunn[é]tuonk nompee onk ne pukquee, weekontamoe pummee nompee mauonk, tabuttantamoe hogk8onk nompee tohkéqunoe nashauonk, onk woh neg hennóog sampweusseae mehtugquash, wutohketeaonk Jehovah, onk woh sohsum8waheau.
61.4 Kah nag pish ayimwog nukkône mohchum8e ayeuongash pish tahshinumwog negonáe touushinneash, kah pish onchehteóog mohchim8e keitotanash, nish tauuhshikish m8cheke pometuongash.
61.5 Kah penuohteaog pish neepóog, kah pish assamóog kuf-flocksum8uh, kah wunnaumonáuh penuwoht neg pish kutanaskúhhamwaenúm8óog, kah neg wánteunkeg k8weenominneohtekonash.
61.6 Qut pish kuttiss8wésimw8 wussephàusuéneumoh Jehovah: wosketompaog pish kuttéhenukkumw8 wuñohtompeantog8moh num-Manitt8mun: pish kummeechimw8 8wenauwetuongan8 Gentilsog, kah ut wussohsum8ongan8wout pish k8woweenauómw8.
61.7 Nompeeu kutakodchuongan8, pish keneese tahshe attumumunumw8: kah nompeeu naswáiyeuonk pish weekontamwog ut wutchippiyeum8óut: newaj ut wutuhkeout, pish neese pishkeu wutohteauuneau: machemohtag wekontamóonk pish apehtunkquog.
61.8 Newutche nen Jehovah n8womontam wussittumóonk, nusskeneam mukk8kinnuáonk wutche chikohtáe mag8ongash, kah nussampwehte[ó]h wutanakausuongan8 ut wanummuhkutéyeuuk, kah nag nutayimauóog machemohtag wunn8waonk.
61.9 Kah 8skannemun8 pish wahteauun ut kenugke Gentilsut, kah wutontseongan8 ut kenug[h]e missinninnuut: wame neg nauoncheg pish samp8áog, neg wuskannemuneog neh Jehov[á]h wunnanumoncheh.
61.10 Pish nummishe wekontamut Jehovahut, nukketeahogkou pish wekontam ut num-Manitt8mut, newutche noh nuthogkquanuk wadchanittue hogk8unash, nutunkqwhuk sampweusseae petashqushaonk, onatuh wussentamwaen agwheont wuhhogkuh wu[n]hogk8ongash, kah onatuh weetauadteáenúnt hogqunn[ú]mont nompakouunash.
61.11 Newutche onatuh ohke sonketeunk wunnéht8nunk, kah neane tanohketeaonk, so[h]kenuwáhtunk nish ne adt tanohketeamukish: ne ne Lord Jehovah sonketeauwáhteauun sampwuss[é]onk kah woweenomaonk ut anaquohtag wame wutohtimóneash.
62.1 WUtche Zion matta nutchequnappu, kah wutche Jerusalem matta nutannósin8, nô pajeh wussampweusseonk ogquesohham8m8ut wôhsittag, kah 8wadchanuáonk onatuh lamp châgkossit.
62.2 Kah Gentilsog pish naumwog kussampweusseonk, kah wame ketass8tamwog kuss[ó]hsum8onk: kah pish kuttéhenit wuske wesuonl, ne wutt8n Jehovah pish waésuonganehteunk.
62.3 Kah wonk pish sohsum8ongane kutchetuhquabéyeu ut wunnutcheganit Jehovah; kah tahs8tamoe chetuhquab ut wunnutcheganit kum-Manitt8m.
62.4 Matta pish wonk kuttéhennitteóh, ohquánumit, kah kutohke matta pish wonk hettam8un tawushik: qut pish kuttéhennit Hephzibah, kah kutohke Beulah: newutche Jehovah kuttapeneúnk, kah kutohke pish weetauadteom8.
62.5 Newutche neane wusken weetauomont peenompoh, kenaumonuk pish k8weetauómunk: k[a]h neane wessentamwaen weekontam8ônont weetauadteánutcheh, ne ne pish kum-Manitt8m k8weekontam8ónuk.
62.6 Nuppon askuhwhosuenuog ut kukqussukquaneutonganit, woi Jerusalem, neg matta pish chequnapékeg kesukodtae kah nukkonáe: ken[à]au masuhwhógish Jehovah chequn[á]péhteok.
62.7 Kah anwôhsumûhteogk nô pajeh menehkhit, kah nô pajeh woweenomwáheónat Jerusalemoh ut ohkeit.
62.8 Jehovah chadchekeyeuau nashpwe wuttinuhkou, kah nashpe menuhke wuhpit, wunnamuhkut, matta wonk nummagou k8weatchimineash kummatwom8óog 8meechuminneaóont, kah wunnaumonáuh penuohte[a]og matta pish wuttattam8og k8winum, ne anakausuontaman.
62.9 Qut nag magunukeg pish ummeechineau kah pish wowussumaog Jehovah, kah neg mom[ó]unukeg, pish 8tattamuneau ut n8neetupanatamwe chippinneutunkanit.
62.10 Pannupwushak, pannupwushak squontamash, quashauwéhtam8k ummay8m missinninnuog: pogkétimómukquag, pogketimomuhquag may mukkinnumok qussukquanash, tahshinum8k muttoagk wutche missinninnúog.
62.11 Kusseh, Jehovah wahteauwáhuwau en wéhqshik muttaok, unnók wuttaunoh Zion, kusseh, k8wadchanitteaonk peyom8: kusseh, wutonkquatunk nashpeu, kah wutanakausuonk ohteau anaquabit.
62.12 Kah pish wuttehenóuh, wunneetupanatamwe missinninnuog, man8whoncheh Jehovah: kah pish kuttehenit, nátinneáwhut, matta ahquontamoe keitotan.
63.1 HOwan yeuoh wag Edom, wag Bozrah, nashpe adtissohs8e hogk8unash? noh wanegik wuthogk8onk, noh paumushadt ut mishe ummenuhkesuonganit? nen an8wi ut sampwesuonganit, menuhkesue n8wadchánuam.
63.2 Toh waj musquag kuthogk8onk, kah kuth[ó]gk8ongash onatuh noh tahtahtushkog wine wisq?
63.3 Nunnusse tahtaskom wine-presse, kah matta howae missinninnuog n8weetomuk8: newutche nag nuttahtaskuskauóog ut nummusquanittam8onganit, kah nussissequohkauóog musquantamon, kah wusqueheonk pish séahôsu ut nuthogk8onganit, kah nunnishketeóh wame nuthogk8unash.
63.4 Newutche ann8tóadtue kesukod nuttahhut ohteau, kah ukkodtum8m8 man8hogig peyom8.
63.5 Kah nunnatauwompip, kah na matta howan aninnohsu: kah nummonchanatamup na matta howan wuttit tahshinnuwáun: newaj nehenwonche nuhpit paudtunkquée wadchanittuonk, kah nummusquantamóonk nuttahshinukqun.
63.6 Kah nuttahtashkuhkáu missinninnuog ut nummusquantam8onganit, kah nukkogkeissippamwuhheog ut nummusquantam8onganit, kah nuppaudto ummenuhkesuongan8 ohkeit.
63.7 Nummisham 8womoausuongash Jehovah, kah woweenomaonk Lord, neaunak wame ne Jehovah aninnumunkqueog: kah mohsag 8netuonk nogque en wekit Israel, ne a[n]inn[u]mauont, neaunak ummo[n]anitteuonk, kah neaun[á]k mataanukish 8w[ó]moauwuongash.
63.8 Newutche n8wop, wunnamuhkut nag nummissinninnúmog, matta pann8w[à]e mukkiesog: neit nag 8wad[c]hanuaenum8uh.
63.9 Ut wame 8tamehpunaongan8out noh wuttamehpunóp, kah wutanaquabee angelumoh nah 8wadchanuh: ut womoausuonganit, kah ut ukkitteamonteanitteaonganit nah umman8whuh, kah wuttahshinuh, kah ukké[n]unuh ut wame nôadte kesukodtut.
63.10 Qut nag wutcheketauóuh, kah m8m8sqheáog 8neetupanatamwe nashauonk: n[é]waj quinnuppeit nag 8matwóminneaóut, kah nah wutayeuuhkonuh.
63.11 Neit mehquontam nukóne kesukodtash Moses kah ummissinninnúmoh, n8wau, ut$toh wutappin noh pas8omp wutch ketahhannit, weeche uf$flocksumoe nanáshi[p]seaneumoh? uttoh wutapin noh ponamauont 8neetupanat[a]mwe nashauonganoh?
63.12 Noh sagkompanomp ut wuttinohkôunit Moses, nashpe wussohsumoe wuhpit, pohshinuk nippe ut anaquabenit, ummicheme wesuonganúhkau[ó]nat wuhhogkuh?
63.13 Noh sagkompanomp papannuppe m8noiyeuut, onatuh horse ut touo[h]komukqut, onk woh nag matta togkussittassun8og?
63.14 Onatuh puppinashim 8mussit ut 8nôuhkoiyeuut, wunnashauanitt8moh Jehovah wutanw[ô]hsum8wáheuh: ne kuttinne sagkompanánuh kummissinninnumog kutáyimauwonat sohsumoe wesuonk.
63.15 Womómpsh wutch kesukqut, kah naish wutch k8neetupanatamwe kah kussohsumoe ayeuonganit: uttiyeu kus-zealum kah kummenuhkesuonk, mishont8wae kenogkus, kah kummonánummuongash? sun kohkôunôsuash?
63.16 Wunnamuhkut ken n8shun, tohkônogque Abraham matta k8wahikk8unan, kah Israel matta k8wahik8un: ken woi Jehovah, n8shun numman8huwaeneumun, k8wesuonk wutch machemohtag.
63.17 Woi Jehovah tohwutch panneseáheog wutch kummayut? kah menehketeaháheog wutch kukqushitteaonganit? qushkish wutche [h]itti[n]ninnumog, kutohtoongane chippan8ongash
63.18 K8neetupanatamwe missinninnuog wutogguhse ohtauuneau: ayeúqueagig neg tahtashkuhkauóog ut k8neetupanatamwe ayeuonganit.
63.19 Nenawun kuttaiheog, nag matta kenánaánawunóog, nag matta hennóog k8wesuonk.
64.1 WOI napehnont nehnekikoman kesukquash onk woh ken8kem, onk woh wadchuash n8konóhanash ut anaquabean.
64.2 Netatupe sabasumwae n8tau chagohtag, n8teau quô[qu]ônche[k]o[m]euteau nippe: wahteauwahuonat, k8wesuonk ayeuqueaneg, onk woh wutohtimoneash nunnukshaash ut anaquabean.
64.3 Ase[à]n uhqueneunkquokish nish matta anantam8ágish, k8w8msip, wadchuash [n]8konóhanupash ut anaquabean.
64.4 Newutche nadteoh kádshi[k] muttaok, wosketompaog matta n8tam8og, asuh matta mehtauoge nunnáuhtam8og, asuh matta muskesukque naumoog, woi God, webe ken, uttoh an quoshauwehtauont neh pahtsuónukqutcheh.
64.5 Nog kenogskau weekontog, kah asit sampweusseonk, yeug mequanumukqueaneg ut kummayut: kusseh, ken kummusquantam, newutche nummatchesemun: yeush ut ohteau matchemohtag, kah pish k8wadchanitteamun.
64.6 Qut nenawun wame onátuh nishkeneunkquok, kah wame nussampweseonganonash tatuppeyeu8ash nishkeneungque monakenissit, kah nenawun wame nummass8pussimun onatuh wunnepogqut: kah nummatcheseonganonash, onatuh wabanit nutamaunukqun.
64.7 Kah matta howan wequttum8un k8wesuonk, noh wogkouunuk wuhhog kuttohqunukqunat: newutche kutunkhumaimun kuskesuk, kah kummahchukkussukqun newutche nuppanneseongash.
64.8 Qut [e]yeu, woi Jehovah, ken n8shun: nenawun man8nsk, ken nutohkuhquéhteaeneumun, kah nenawun wame kenutchegane anakausuonk.
64.9 Mishe musquanittogkon, woi Jehovah, mehquantogkon matcheseonk micheme, kuhkinneash, naish k8wehquetumauunumun, nenawun wame kummissinninneumog.
64.10 K8neetupanatamwe keitotanash touohkomukqueyeu8ash: Zion touohkomukk88: Jerusalem touwushin.
64.11 N8neetupanatamwe kah n8neetue wetuómun, uttoh n8shunónog adt, wowussumukqueap, ne mahchekutteau wutche n8teau, kah wame n8ne teagwasinnumunónash mohtuppashinash.
64.12 Sun woh kutchequnapeh kuhhog yeush wutche, woi Jehovah? sun woh kummanunap, kah kumm8cheke onkuppunasimun?
65.1 NAg nunnatinneóhikquog, neg matta nat8mukqueaneg: nag nunnamhikquog matta natinneawh[e]gig: nussip, mónunneaiek monunneaiek, nuttinnomp wutohtimóin, ne matta ahettam8muk n8wesuonk.
65.2 Nussepagenum nunnutchegash, qunnikesuk, en cheketamwe missinninnúut, neg aóncheg may ne matta wanegeninn8g, neaunak nehenwonche wuttenantam8ongan8.
65.3 Missinninnúog m8m8sqh[ú]kqutche nagwutte[à]eu, neg sephausitcheg ut tanohketeaonganéhtu, kah chogkositcheg weetemungquok ut brikse Altarsut.
65.4 Neg apitcheg weenohkekontu, kah kaecheg wadchuuhkontu, neg mechikeg swinese weyaus, kah sabahheg ne ayimuk wutch nishkeneunkquokish, ohteau 8wishquóut:
65.5 Neg án8wacheg, nussikkompau, pas8suksuhkon, newutche n8neetupanatamweyeu anue onk ken: yeug ogqueyeu8og pukut ut nutchânut, n8teau ne náhteagun[a]g.
65.6 Kusseh wussukwhosu anaquabean: matta nutchequnappu, qut nutonkquodtauoog, nutonkquodtauoog ut upp8chenauóun8out.
65.7 Kummatcheseonganooash, kah ummatcheseonganooash k8sh8oog moaeu (wussin Jeh[h]vah) neg châgossitcheg weetemungquok ut wadchuuhkontu, kah nup-blasphemónukquog wadchuésukontu: newaj pish quttuhhum nôadte wutanakausuongan8 ut upp8chenauón8óut.
65.8 Yeu wussin Jehovah, neane wuske wine naméhteómuk ut nequttachéiyeuut, kah howan n8wau, nehtóhkon newutche wunanitteaonk ohteau: ne nutussen newutche nuttinneum, onk woh mat nuppagwanoog wame.
65.9 Kah pish nussohh8wutto wuskannem wutch Jakob, kah wutche Judah noh ohtunk n8wadchumash kah pepenauogig pish wutahtauuneau kah nuttinneumog na pish 8tohkinneau.
65.10 Kah Sharon pish flokse chippinneutunkanu8 kah Achoré 8nouhkoi, ne herdse sepsinóe ayeuunk, wutche nummissinninneumog neg natinneóhikqueaneg.
65.11 Qut kenaau ahquanumoncheg Jehovah, neg wananatogeg n8neetupanatamwe wadchum, neg quoshauwéhtogig table wutche chipwushaog, kah quoshwéhtogig wuttattamoe mag8onk, ut neg adtasúkeg.
65.12 Newaj pish ogkémunóg wutch togkodteg, kah pish wame kenauwaemw8 en pagwanittinneat: newutche wehqutteamweon matta kenamp8ham8mw8, ket8kôon, matta ken8tam8m8, qut kummatcheussemw8 ut anaquohtag nuskesukquash, kah kuppepenamumw8 ne matta tapeneám8:
65.13 Newaj yeu n8wadt Lord Jehovah, kusseh nuttinneumog pish meetsuog, qut pish kenaau kukkodtuppumw8, kusseh nuttinneumog pish wuttattamwog, qut pish kenaau kukkuhkutt8numw8, kusseh nuttinneumog pish muskouantamwog, qut pish kutakodchimw8.
65.14 Kusseh nuttinninneumog pish weekontamwutte[a]hae ket8hamoog, qut kenaau pish ken[e]uántamwutteahaeu kummaumw8, kah pish pohquetteahaeu kutt8numw8.
65.15 Kah pish kenukkodtumumw8 k8wesuonkan8 wutch matánumáonk pepenauog: newutche Lord Jehovah pish kenushh[ú]k, kah pish penoweseonganeheau wuttinninneumoh.
65.16 Noh wunánumont wuhhogkuh ut ohkeit, noh pish wun[à]numau wuhhogkuh ut wunnamuhkut[e]é Manitt8ut: kah noh chadchekeyeuadt ut ohkit, pish nashpe chadchekeyeuau wunnamuhkuttee Manitto, newutche negonáeu wuttamehpunaongash wunanittamunash, kah newutche nish adtahtásuash wutch nuskesukqut
65.17 Newutche kusseh nukkesteoh wuske kesukquash & wuske ohke: kah negoneyeuit matta pish mequontam8un, asuh 8waantam8un.
65.18 Qut kenaau wekontam8k kah micheme muskouanatam8k ut ne kestéau: newutche kusseh nukkesteau Jerusalem, wekontamoonk, kah ummissinninumoh wutch wekontam8onk.
65.19 Kah pish nummuskouantam ut Jerusalem, kah pish n8wekontam ut nummissinninnúut, kah wussippég8e wuttauatonkqussuonk matta pish wonk n8tam8un naut, asuh wadtaúatonkqussue mauonk.
65.20 Na pish matta wonk wutch wusketuun8, asuh kehchis, noh matta nómwohto8g ukkesukodtumash: newutche mukkies pish nup nequt pasuk8ekodtumwohkog; qut matcheseaen nequt pasuk8 kodtumwohkog pish mattanum[a]u.
65.21 Kah nag pish ayimwog wetuomash, kah wutáyinaoash[:] pish weenominneohketeaog kah pish ummechineau meechummuonk.
65.22 Nag matta pish wekittea8og kah onkatog 8wekin: nag matta pish ohkehteauouog kah onkatog ummeechin: newutche neane nékuk mehtug ne wuttinnékinneau nummissinninneumog, kah pepenauogeg pish sepohtóog wunnetchegane anakausuonk.
65.23 Nag matta pish tahn8tanakauseog, asuh nechauóog wutch wuttamehpunáonk: newutche neh 8skannemun8ch wunnánumoncheh Jehovah, kah wutontseongan8 nag weeche.
65.24 Kah pish n$nih, ash waeequttumhettékup, nunnamp8hamauóog, kah ashp[à]me keket8kahettit, pish nunn8tauóog.
65.25 Mukquoshim kah lambe pish weetatupp8t[u]og, kah qunnonou pish ogque meech sekuppoghegash oxinut: kah puppissi pish meechuog ask8og. Nag matta pish woskehuwowog, asuh pagwohteauóog ut wame n8neetupanatamwe wadchúmut, wussin Jehovah.
66.1 YEu wussin Jehovah, kesuk nutappuonk, kah ohke nukquenannéhtuonk: uttiyeu weetu ne áyimaiye[o]g? kah uttiyeu nutann8sin8e ayeuonk?
66.2 Newutche wame yeush ukkesteauunash nunnutcheg, kah wame yeush nniyeupash, wussin Jehovah: qut nogque in yeuoh wosketomp nummónunneau, noh matchekit, kah pohqueteáhont, kah nanukshontog nuttinn8waonk.
66.3 Noh nashont oxinoh, onatuh nashont wosketompuh, noh sephausit lamboh, ontauh támehtahhog anum wussittipuk; noh maguk mag8onk, onatuh maguk pigse wusqueheunk: noh chogkussik weetemungquok, onatuh noh wunánumont nunneukontunkan: nux nag pepenamwog nehenwonche ummay[y]euóash, kah ukketeahogk8un8oh wekontamwoh wunnishkeneunkquodt8m8ash.
66.4 Nen wonk nuppepenam pohch8wunukquéhetticheh, kah nunnuhkuhkauwaheóog 8wabesuongash, newutche weehqutteamweon matta howan namp8hamunk8, kôdt8hk[ò]on nag matta n8tam8og, qut nag matcheseog ut anaquabeh, kah pepenamwog ne matta wekontam8h.
66.5 N8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, kenaau nanukushántamógish wuttinn8waonk: keematt8oog neg pagkénukqueógig wutche n8wesuonk, n8waog, Jehovah sohsumwáhunaj, qut noh pish nogqussu, wutche k8wekontam8wongan8, kah nag pish akodchuog.
66.6 Mishont8wae wadtauatonkqussuonk wutch keitotanat, wadtauatonkqussuonk wutch templeut, 8wâdtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah, noh onkquodtauont ummatwomoh.
66.7 Ahquam kodtauweekheunk, neechau, ash aonkquommam8kup, neechau mukkutchuksoh.
66.8 Howan n8tog neahunig? howan nag* neaûnagish? sun woh ohke neechahtauun pasuk kesukod, asuh woh wutohtimoin pasukqut neekin: newutche queenau Zion kodtauweekheont neechau wunneechanoh.
66.9 Sun woh n8wompikquáhuwam, kah sun woh matta nunneechahuóh, wussin Jehovah? woh nunneechahuwan, kah sun woh nukkuppoh wussin kum-Manitt8m?
66.10 Weekontam8k weeche Jerusalem, kah weeche muskouanatam8[é]nuk, kenaau wame womonógish, muskouanatamwe weekontamok noh weeche, kenaau wame mauunuitteauwánshógish.
66.11 Onk woh ken8numw8, kah woh kuttaphetteamw8 nashpe wekontamwe wussogkodtunk, onk woh kussesenamuneau, onk woh k8wekontam8wontamumw8 madta$áneuk wussohsumóonk.
66.12 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, nukqunteau wunohteaonk onatuh sepuut, kah wussohsum8ongan8 Gentilsog, onatuh kussitchuáne sep: neit pish ken8numw8, pish kukkinuk8, kah pish kuppumukahh8[n]uk8 ut ukkuttukqut.
66.13 Onatuh nah ohkasoh taphikquit ne pish kuttinne taphenineau: kah pish kuttaphetteamw8 ut Jerusalemut.
66.14 Kah yeu naumog, kuttahhou pish weekontamòm8, kah kuskonn8 pish ogque neekin mosketuut, kah wunnutcheg Jehovah pish wahteauun in nogque wuttinneumit, kah ummusquantamoonk nogque in ummatwomut.
66.15 Newutche kusseh, Jehovah pish nashpe peyau n8teau, kah nashpe wutchariotsumash onatuh pemsquoh: chekee onkquttauunat ummusquantam8onk, kah wutáuskomuongash nashpe n8n8unáe n8taash.
66.16 Newutche nashpe n8teau kah nashpe wuttogkodteg, Jehovah pish keket8kontam wame weyaus, kah nashoncheh Jehovah pish monaoh.
66.17 Nag waneetupanatamwaheoncheg wuhhogkauh, kah pahkheoncheg wuhhogkauh, ut tanohketeaonganehtu, ut onkauwonkq, ut nashauwe, meechhettit pigse weyaus, kah nishkeneunkquok, kah mishabohques, pish moaeu mohtupaeog wussin Jéhovah.
66.18 Newutche n8wahteoh wutanakausuonganooash, kah wuttenantam8onganooash: pish peyaum8, pish nummukkinnumunat wame wutohtimoneash, kah unnont8waongash, kah nag pish peyaog, kah pish naumwog nussohsumoonk.
66.19 Kah nupponum kuhkinneasuonk ut kenugke nagoh, kah nutann8noog en wutohtimoinneat, neg pohquohhokig, en Tarshish, Pul, kah Lud, neg p8tonkinoncheg ahtompeh, en Tubal, kah Javan, en noadtit munnohannehtu, neg matta n8tamógig n8woweenomitteaonk, kah matta naum8og nussohsumoonk, kah nag pish wahteauwahuwaog nussohsumoonk ut kenugke Gentilsut.
66.20 Kah nag pish paudtauaog wame kemat8oh, wutch mag8onk en Jehovahut, wutch wame wutohtimoinneat, ut horsesut chariotsut, kah littersut, kah ut mulsut, kah ut kogkinupshae puppinashimwut, ut n8neetupanatamwe wadchúmut, ut Jerusalem, wussin Jehovah, onatuh wuneechanoh Israel paudtaúunit mag8onk, ut pohkishqúadt, ut wekit Jehovah.
66.21 Kah wonk nag nawhutch nunneemunoog wutche sephausuenuog kah Levitsog wussin Jehovah..
66.22 Newutche neane wuske kesukquash kah wuske ohke, nish pish ayimonish,
66.23 Kah pish nnih, wutch pasuk wuske nepauzsaut en onkatoganit, & wutch pasuk saboth en onkatoganit, wame weyaus pish peyaog wowussitteamuneat ut anaquabeh wussin Jehovah.
66.24 Kah nag pish sohhamwog, kah pish moninneauwáog nupp8e wuhhogkau[h], wosketompaog neg ayeuuhkonittue panneussehtaitcheg, newutche wutask8kin8uh matta pish nupp8oh, kah wunn8tomw8 matta pish onthamm8un, kah nag pish unkquanumukqussuog ut wame weyausut.
